#Text:Vaikhānasaśrautasūtra
#Edition:Caland
#Data entry:F. Voegeli; sections 8-9, 11ff by O. Hellwig



1.1.1	athāgnyādheyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
1.1.2	brāhmaṇo vasante rājanyo grīṣme vaiśyaḥ śaradi rathakāro varṣāsu
1.1.3	sarve śiśira ity eke
1.1.4	rohiṇīkṛttikāmṛgaśiraḥpunarvasūttarānūrādhāśravaṇahastaviśākhāsv ekasmin nakṣatre 'māvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vādadhīta
1.1.5	kṛttikāsv agnim ādadhīteti brāhmaṇoktāni kāmyāni nakṣatrāṇi yathākāmam
1.1.6	yatraitāni trīṇi saṃbhavanty ṛtur nakṣatraṃ parva tad bhadram
1.1.7	vipratiṣedhe tu nakṣatram ṛtuś ca balīyaḥ
1.1.8	somena yakṣyamāṇa ādadhīta nartuṃ na nakṣatraṃ sūrkṣet
1.1.9	yathopapādaṃ śamīgarbham aśvattham
1.1.10	yady aśamīgarbhaṃ śuklāṅkuram aśanivāyvanupahatam agnyadagdhaṃ bahupakṣyanāvāsam aśuṣkam aśīrṇam antyajātyanupahataṃ gatvā vaiśvānarasūktena pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā praṇameta
1.1.11	tenaiva prācīm udīcīṃ vā śākhāṃ prāgādi pradakṣiṇaṃ chedayitvā prāgagram udagagraṃ vā nipātayet
1.1.12	patitottaram adharaṃ mūlam agraṃ ca yathā jñeyaṃ tathāṅkayitvā śākhāpatrāṇi prahāpayati
1.1.13	tāṃ dvidhā chedayitvādhobhāgenādharām araṇiṃ tvakpārśvordhvabhāgāṃ vigatatvacaṃ viśoṣitāṃ caturviṃśatyaṅgulāyatām aṣṭāṅgulivistārāṃ caturaṅgulonnatāṃ tathottarabhāgenottarām araṇiṃ ca gāyatryā karoti
1.1.14	tatra prathamāni yāni catvāry aṅgulāni śiraś cakṣuḥ śrotram āsyaṃ ca
1.1.15	dvitīyāni yāni grīvā vakṣo hṛdayaṃ stanaḥ
1.1.16	tṛtīyāny udaraprabhṛtīni
1.1.17	caturthāni śroṇī
1.1.18	pañcamāny ūrū
1.1.19	ṣaṣṭhāni jaṅghe
1.1.20	pādāv ity eke
1.1.21	evam araṇī sarvair aṅgaiḥ saṃpūrṇe bhavataḥ
1.1.22	yac chīrṣṇi manthati śīrṣaktimān yajamāno bhavati
1.1.23	yad grīvāyāṃ vepano 'yaṃ nirmanthet
1.1.24	yad udare 'nārabdho 'sya yajño bhavati
1.1.25	ūrū rakṣasāṃ yonir jaṅghe pādau piśācānāṃ śroṇī devānāṃ yoniḥ
1.1.26	tasmāc chroṇyām eva prathamaṃ manthet
1.1.27	mūlād aṣṭāṅgulaṃ parityajyāgrāc ca dvādaśāṅgulaṃ pārśvatas trīṇi trīṇy aṅgulāni prathamamanthane
1.1.28	evaṃ prajananaṃ kurvīta
1.1.29	uttarāraṇer aṣṭāṅgulayuktināhaṃ yathāyogapariṇāhaṃ pramanthaṃ chittvā manthamūle saṃdhatte
1.1.30	tena sahitaḥ ṣaḍviṃśatyaṅgulāyato mantho bhavati
1.1.31	tathā chidram iti
1.1.32	uttānā prākśirā araṇis tathā vediḥ
1.2.1	gṛhe saumye paścimapūrvāyatāṃ tathānuvaṃśāṃ pūrvadakṣiṇayor dvārayutām agniśālāṃ kalpayaty asthiromakeśāṅgāratuṣakāṣṭhāśmaloṣṭapipīlikādīn varjayitvā mṛdā śuddhayā
1.2.2	paścime bhūr iti gārhapatyāyatanaṃ rajjvāṣṭādaśāṅgulyā vṛttaṃ bhrāmayitvāṣṭāṅgulonnataṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ kṛtvā paritaś caturaṅgulivistāraṃ hitvā madhye ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ nimnaṃ khanati
1.2.3	śiṣṭaṃ tad ūrdhvamekhalā syāt
1.2.4	tatparigatāṃ caturaṅgulivistāronnatām adhomekhalāṃ karoti
1.2.5	tasmāt prācyām aṣṭapadaprakrame brāhmaṇasyaikādaśaprakrame kṣatriyasya dvādaśaprakrame vaiśyasyāpi suvar ity āhavanīyāgnyāyatanaṃ caturaśraṃ caturdikṣu dvātriṃśadaṅgulyāyatam aṣṭāṅgulonnataṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ prakalpya pūrvavat parito hitvā mekhalām ūrdhvāṃ madhye nimnam adhomekhalāṃ karoti
1.2.6	dvayor madhye vedir asīty uktvā gārhapatyāhavanīyasaṃbandhāṃ dakṣiṇottarayoś caturaṅgulivistāronnatāṃ tadantare ṣoḍaśāṅgulivistārāṃ vediṃ kurute
1.3.1	vedyāṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ paścime bhāge bhuva ity anvāhāryapacanaṃ pañcaviṃśatyaṅgulyā vṛttaṃ bhrāmayitvā dakṣiṇārdhe 'rdhacandrākāraṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ pūrvavat tasyonnataṃ madhyanimnam ūrdhvādharā mekhalā ca
1.3.2	vedyuttaraṃ tridhā kṛtvā pūrvabhāgottare prakrame vedyunnatam utkaraṃ kuryāt
1.3.3	āhavanīyāt prācyāṃ jana iti sabhyāgnyāyatanaṃ dvādaśāṅgulonnatam āhavanīyavac caturaśraṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ paritas tathaiva hitvā dvādaśāṅgulaṃ madhyanimnaṃ caturaṅgulivistāronnatās tisro mekhalāḥ pañcāṅgulivistārā madhyamā mekhalā
1.3.4	tatprācyāṃ maha ity āvasathyāgnyāyatanaṃ trikoṇaṃ paścimadakṣiṇottareṣu pañcacatvāriṃśadaṅgulāyataṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ tasyonnataṃ madhyanimnaṃ dve mekhale ca pūrvavat
1.3.5	āvasathyaṃ caturaśrim ity eke
1.3.6	sarveṣāṃ yājñikānāṃ yajamānasyādhvaryor vā dakṣiṇahastasya madhyamāṅguler madhyamaparvaṇā mānam ācarati
1.4.1	yuktaḥ śraddhānvito viprair anujñātaḥ keśān romanakhāni ca vāpayitvā vidhinā snāta iṣe tvorje tvetyādi svādhyāyam adhīyīta śataṃ prāṇāyāmāṃś ca kṛtvā dhyāyan nārāyaṇam upoṣya sapatnīko ghṛtamiśraṃ haviṣyaṃ kṣīreṇa prāśnāti
1.4.2	uktavratam ācaran pāvanārtham amātyahomān kūśmāṇḍahomāṃś ca juhuyāt
1.4.3	ahany upavasathe sarvakāmārtham agnīn ādhāsya ity uktvā yajamānaḥ keśaśmaśruromāṇi vapate
1.4.4	na vapata ity eke
1.4.5	tato 'bhyudayaśrāddhaṃ kurvīta
1.4.6	daivikavat sarvaṃ
1.4.7	dvau viśvedevau caturaḥ pitṝn vṛṇīte
1.4.8	nāndīmukhāḥ pitaraḥ sānugāḥ priyantām ity ārādhyārghyaṃ dadāti
1.4.9	dūrvākṣatayuktam udakumbhaṃ nidhāya pūrvavad daivikaṃ paitṛkaṃ ca hutvā tadānīm udakumbhādbhir yāsu gandhā rasā uti yajamāno 'bhiṣicya puṇyāhaṃ vācayati
1.4.10	svasti no mimītāṃ kṛṇuṣva pājaḥ svastidā viśaspatir iti pratisaraṃ baddhvā tasmin dine brāhmaṇān uktalakṣaṇān ṛtvijo vṛtvā saṃpūjya madhuparkaṃ dadāti
1.4.11	yajamānaḥ patnī ca navair vastrottarīyapuṣpādyair alaṃkṛtau bhavataḥ
1.4.12	adhvaryur yo aśvatthaḥ śamīgarbha ity araṇī uddhṛtyāśvatthāddhavyavāhād iti saṃbharati
1.4.13	āyur mayi dhattām iti saṃbhṛte abhimantrayate
1.4.14	adhivṛkṣasūrya aupāsanād dīptāñ chakalān yajamāna āyuṣe vo gṛhṇāmīti pañcabhiḥ śarāve gṛhṇāty āyur mām āviśatv iti gṛhītvā tāny upottiṣṭhati
1.5.1	apareṇa gārhapatyaṃ pālāśyā śāmyā vā śākhayāpeta vīteti trivīdhīs tryapakramam udagantaṃ mārjayitvoddhanyamānam ity uddhatya śaṃ no devīr ity avokṣya tam agniṃ brāhmaudanikam ādadhāti
1.5.2	nirmanthyam ambarīṣam uttapanīyaṃ vety eke
1.5.3	yady aupāsanaṃ na śiṣyate sāyam atra juhuyāt
1.5.4	niśāyām apareṇa brāhmaudanikaṃ lohitam ānaḍuhaṃ carma prācīnagrīvam uttaralomopastīrya tasmiṃś catuḥśarāvaṃ brahmaudanaṃ nirvapati
1.5.5	ākūtyai tvā kāmāya tveti niruptān abhimṛśyādbhiḥ prokṣya carmaṇy ulūkhalaṃ nidhāya niruptān opyāvahanti
1.5.6	śūrpeṇa tuṣān vivicya prajā sthālīm iti sthālīṃ saṃśodhya tasyāṃ brahmaṇe juṣṭam nirvapāmīti catuḥśarāvaiś caturdhā taṇḍulān āvapati
1.5.7	na nirṇenekti nānvavasrāvayati
1.5.8	payasi śrapayati
1.5.9	caturṣu vā pātreṣu śrapayitvābhighāryodag udvāsya darvyā brahmaudanād uddhṛtya prabhūtena sarpiṣopasicya pra vedhase kavaye medhyāyeti juhoty upatiṣṭhate vā
1.6.1	taṃ caturdhā vyuddhṛtya prabhūtena sarpiṣopasicya ṛtvigbhyo dadāti
1.6.2	te prāśyācamya rāddhas te brahmaudana iti praśāsanti
1.6.3	tebhyo vatsataraṃ dadāti
1.6.4	sthālyām ājyaśeṣam ānayati
1.6.5	tasminn ārdrāḥ sapalāśāḥ prādeśamātrīr lakṣaṇyāśvatthasya tisraḥ samidho 'bhyajya citriyād aśvatthād ity abhimantrya samidhāgniṃ duvasyatopa tvāgne haviṣmatīs taṃ tvā samidbhir aṅgira iti tisṛbhir gāyatrībhir brāhmaṇasya brāhmaudanike 'gnāv ādadhāti samidhyamānaḥ prathamo nu gharma iti triṣṭubbhī rājanyasya tvām agne samidhānaṃ yaviṣṭheti jagatībhir vaiśyasya
1.6.6	atra mithunāv asiktaretasau gāvau dadāti
1.6.7	etam agnim ito dhārayanty ekāhaṃ dvyahaṃ tryahaṃ caturahaṃ dvādaśāham ṛtuṃ saṃvatsaraṃ vā
1.6.8	anugata etasminn agnau prayāṇe yajamānasya ca punar evaṃ vihitaṃ brahmaudanaṃ
1.6.9	brāhmaudaniko yajamāno vrataṃ carati
1.6.10	na striyam upaiti na māṃsam aśnāti nāsya gṛhād agniṃ haranti nānyataś cāharanti
1.6.11	yadi saṃvatsare nādhātuṃ śaknuyāt punar evaṃ brahmaudanaṃ vihitaṃ
1.6.12	śva ādhāsyamānaś ca brahmaudanaṃ pacaty adhvaryuś caitāṃ rātrim etad vrataṃ carati
1.6.13	prajā agne saṃvāsayety uttareṇa gārhapatyāyatanaṃ kalmāṣam ajaṃ saṃyacchet
1.6.14	śalkair agnim indhāna iti śalkais tāṃ rātriṃ vinidro yajamāno 'gnim inddhe
1.7.1	vedyāṃ saṃbhṛtān saṃbhārān saṃgṛhṇāti
1.7.2	vaiśvānarasya rūpam iti sikatā yad idaṃ divo yad ada ity ūṣān ūtīḥ kurvāṇa ity ākhūddhatam ūrjaṃ pṛthivyā iti valmīkavapāṃ prajāpatisṛṣṭānām iti sūdaṃ yasya rūpam iti varāhoddhataṃ yābhir adṛṃhad iti śarkarāś ca
1.7.3	saptaitān pārthivāñchuddhān pratyekaṃ kuḍuvaṃ śarāve pṛthag eva gṛhītvāśvo rūpaṃ kṛtvety āśvatthaṃ prādeśamātraṃ sapatrāgram ūrjaḥ pṛthivyā adhyutthito 'sīty audumbaraṃ gāyatryā hriyamāṇasya devānāṃ brahmavādam iti dvābhyāṃ pālāśaṃ yayā te sṛṣṭasyāgner iti śamīṃ yat te sṛṣṭasyeti vaikaṅkataṃ yat te tān tasyety aśanihataṃ
1.7.4	yo aśvatthaḥ śamīgarbha ity atraike 'raṇī ca saṃbharanti
1.7.5	yaṃ tvā samabharaṃ jātaveda iti yajamānaḥ sarvān saṃbhārān punaḥ saṃgṛhṇāti
1.7.6	upavyuṣaṃ sarvādhānino brāhmaudanike 'gnau prātar aupāsanahoma ity eke
1.7.7	jātavedo bhuvanasya reto 'yaṃ te yonir ṛtviya iti dvābhyām asminn agnāv araṇī niṣṭapati
1.8.1	mayi gṛhṇāmi yo no agnir iti dvābhyām ātmany agniṃ gṛhītvā dohyā ca ta ity araṇī yajamānāya prayacchati
1.8.2	mahī viśpatnīty araṇī pradīyamāne yajamānaḥ pratīkṣate
1.8.3	ārohataṃ daśatam iti pratigṛhya ṛtviyavatī stho agniretasāv ity abhimantrya mayi gṛhṇāmi yo no agnir iti dvābhyām ātmany agniṃ gṛhṇāti
1.8.4	idam aham anṛtāt satyam upaimīti vācaṃ yacchati
1.8.5	agnī rakṣāṃsi sedhatīty adhvaryur brāhmaudanikam abhimantrya tam anugamayati
1.8.6	yajamānaḥ pañcadhāgnīn vyakramad iti pañcadhāgnīn saṃkalpayed idaṃ viṣṇur iti tridhā vā
1.8.7	gārhapatyānvāhāryapacanāhavanīyasabhyāvasathyānām āyatanāni śundhadhvam iti gomayenopalipyāpeta vīteti pūrvavat saṃmṛjya rakṣohaṇam eto nv indram ity avokṣati
1.8.8	śaṃ no devīr ity eke
1.8.9	mayi devā ityādibhiś caturdiśaṃ darbhān saṃnyasyoddhanyamānam iti sauvarṇena rājatena vā navadhā khanet
1.8.10	brahma jajñānaṃ pūtaṃ hyatana iti dvābhyāṃ prādeśasaṃmitāḥ prāgantās tisras tathottarāntāś ca lekhā ullikhya sāvitryāvokṣya śaṃ no devīr iti saṃbhārān prokṣyāyataneṣu hiraṇyaṃ nidhāyod vayaṃ tamasa ud u tyaṃ citram iti pṛthak sthaṇḍile juhoti
1.9.1	sikatārdhaṃ dvidhā kṛtvārdhaṃ gārhapatyāyatane nivapaty ardhaṃ dakṣiṇāgner itarārdhaṃ tridhā kṛtvā pūrveṣv āyataneṣu
1.9.2	sabhyāvasathyayor anārambhe sarvam āhavanīye
1.9.3	evaṃ kṛtvetarān pārthivān nivapati
1.9.4	agner bhasmāsīti sikatāḥ
1.9.5	saṃjñānam asīty ūṣān nivapan yad adaś candram asi kṛṣṇaṃ tad ihāstv iti manasā dhyāyati
1.9.6	ud ehy agna ity ākhūddhataṃ yat pṛthivyā iti gārhapatyāyatane valmīkavapāṃ nidadhāti yad antarikṣasyeti dakṣiṇāgner yad divo 'nāmṛtam ity āhavanīyasya tūṣṇīm itarayoḥ
1.9.7	ut samudrān iti sūdam
1.9.8	iyaty agna āsīr iti varāhoddhatam
1.9.9	ado devīr iti śarkarā nivapan yaṃ dveṣṭi tasya vadhaṃ manasā dhyāyati
1.9.10	lohāny audumbarāṇi vā pārthivānāṃ sthāne vikalpārthāni bhavanti
1.9.11	ṛtaṃ stṛṇāmīty āyataneṣu saṃbhārān stṛṇāti
1.9.12	saṃ yā va ity ūṣān sikatāś ca saṃsṛjati
1.9.13	saṃ vaḥ sṛjāmīti vānaspatyān saṃsṛjyetaḥ prathamaṃ jajñe agnir iti sakṛd evaikaikasmin nivapati
1.9.14	tat tat saṃbhārasaṃgrahaṇamantrair ity eke
1.10.1	yās te śivās tanuva iti gārhapatye sauvarṇaṃ rukmaśakalam uttarataḥ saṃbhāreṣūpāsya candram agnim ity upāstam abhimantrya dveṣyāya rājataṃ rukmam atiprayacchati
1.10.2	yadi dveṣyaṃ na vindet tāṃ diśaṃ prati nirasyet
1.10.3	na tat punar ādadīta
1.10.4	evaṃ sarveṣv āyataneṣūpāsya nirasyet
1.10.5	divas tvā vīryeṇa kalpetāṃ dyāvāpṛthivī iti dvābhyāṃ sarvān nyuptān saṃbhārān kalpayati
1.10.6	saṃbhṛtā agnayo mā kaścanāntareṇa saṃcāriṣṭeti goptāram ādiśya prabhāte brāhmaudanikasya bhasmāpodūhya tatra muñjakulāyam āstīrya pratīcīnaprajananām adharāraṇiṃ nidhāya cittiḥ srug iti daśahotrottarāraṇiṃ prajanane nidhāyādharām araṇīṃ mantham ātmānaṃ viṣṇuṃ janyam agniṃ ca dhyāyan sahāgne agnineti manthaty upatiṣṭhati
1.10.7	aśve mathyamāne caturhotṝn yajamānaṃ vācayati
1.10.8	upāvaroheti jāyamānam agnim abhimantrayate
1.10.9	yajamāno vācaṃ visṛjate
1.10.10	jāte varaṃ dadāti
1.10.11	prajāpates tvā prāṇenābhiprāṇimi prāṇe tvāmṛtam ādadhāmīti dvābhyāṃ jātam agnim abhijighrati
1.10.12	ahaṃ tvad asmīty abhimantrayate
1.11.1	adhvaryur ajann agnir iti tam agnim abhimantryājījanann amṛtaṃ martyāsa ity añjalinā parigṛhṇāti
1.11.2	śarāve karīṣādiṣu jātam agniṃ nidhāya samrāḍ asi virāḍ asīti śalkaiḥ saminddhe
1.11.3	yajamānaḥ patnī ca kṣaume paridhāyāpavṛtte 'gnyādheye 'dhvaryave dadyātāṃ
1.11.4	rathantare gīyamāne 'gniṃ prāñcam uddhṛtyāsīnaḥ prāg udayād gārhapatyam ādadhāti prathamābhyāṃ vyāhṛtībhyāṃ bhṛgūṇāṃ tvā devānām iti bhārgavasyāṅgirasāṃ tvā devānām ity āṅgirasasyādityānāṃ tvety anyeṣāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ varuṇasya tveti rājña indrasya tveti rājanyasya manos tveti vaiśyasya ṛbhūṇāṃ tveti rathakārasya bhūmir bhūmneti prathamābhyāṃ sarparājñībhyāṃ gharmaḥ śirastad ayam iti prathamena ca gharmaśirasā yās te śivāḥ prāṇaṃ tvāmṛte divas tvā vīryeṇāgne gṛhapate 'he budhnya pariṣadyeti catasṛbhir gārhapatyāyatane saṃbhāreṣv agniṃ jvalantam abhyādadhāti
1.11.5	agna āyāhi samrāḍ asi virāḍ asīti śalkaiḥ saminddhe
1.11.6	yajamānaḥ sugārhapatya ity āhitaṃ gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhate tat tad ādhānamantraiś ca
1.11.7	adhvaryur grāmyāraṇyauṣadhibījāni yathālābham ājye 'vadhāya yā te agne paśuṣu pavamānā priyā tanūr iti śamanahomair āhitam agniṃ śamayeta
1.12.1	anv agnir uṣasām iti gārhapatye 'gnipraṇayanīyān idhmān ādīpyāśvaṃ purastāt sthāpayati
1.12.2	ojase balāya tvodyacche yas ta ātmā divaḥ pṛthivyā ud u tvā viśve devā iti catasṛbhir gārhapatyād āhavanīyaṃ śarāva uddhṛtya taṃ sikatāpūritena pātreṇopayamya jānudaghna udyacchati
1.12.3	tasmin dhāryamāṇe vāmadevye gīyamāne laukikaṃ mathitaṃ vāgnim āhṛtya dakṣiṇayā dvārordhvajānur upaviśyāgnīdhro dvitīyayā vyāhṛtyā yatharṣyādhānenāyaṃ gauḥ pṛśnir akramīt triṃśaddhāmeti dvitīyatṛtīyābhyāṃ sarparājñībhyāṃ vātaḥ prāṇa iti dvitīyena ca gharmaśirasā yās te śivās tanuvo vyānaṃ tvāmṛte divas tvā vīryeṇāgne 'nnapā mayobhuveti saṃbhāreṣv anvāhārapacanam ādadhāti
1.12.4	gārhapatyād agnim āhṛtyety eke
1.12.5	vyākhyāto bījahomo yajamānasya copasthānaṃ
1.12.6	yā vājinn agner ity agnitanūr aśvasya dakṣiṇe karṇe yajamānaṃ vācayati
1.12.7	vikramasva mahāṁ asi prācīm anu pradiśaṃ kramadhvam agnineti tisṛbhir aśvamukhāḥ prācīṃ gacchanti
1.12.8	iyaty agre 'gniṃ haraty atha madhyato nābhidaghne tṛtīyam āsyadaghne
1.12.9	nāgnim ādityaṃ ca vyavaiti
1.12.10	imā u mām ity ardhādhve hriyamāṇaṃ yajamāna upasthāya varaṃ dadyāt
1.12.11	tasminn adhvaryur nāko 'sīti hiraṇyaṃ nidhāyātikrāmati
1.12.12	bṛhaspate paridīyeti dakṣiṇato brahmā rathaṃ rathacakraṃ vā gārhapatyād āhavanīyāt saṃtataṃ triḥ parivartayati
1.12.13	yāvat triḥ parivartayati tāvad abhyasthād iti prāñcaṃ pūrvavāham aśvaṃ dakṣiṇena pādenottarapārśvataḥ saṃbhārān ākramayati
1.13.1	yathāhitasyāgner aṅgārā abhyavavarteran
1.13.2	taṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ parito nītvā yad akranda iti punar eva tathākramayati
1.13.3	purastāt pratyaṅmukham aśvaṃ sthāpayati
1.13.4	aśvābhāve 'naḍuho 'jasya pade vādadhīta
1.13.5	kamaṇḍalupada ādadhītety eke
1.13.6	yad idaṃ diva ity agnim abhimantrya purastāt pratyaṅmukhas tiṣṭhan sarvābhir vyāhṛtībhir yatharṣyādhānena bhūmir bhūmnāsya prāṇād iti prathamottamābhyāṃ sarparājñībhyām arkaś cakṣur ity uttamena ca gharmaśirasā yās te śivā apānaṃ tvāmṛte divas tvā vīryeṇāgne samrāḍ ity āhavanīyaṃ jvalantam agnim ūrdhvajñur eva saṃbhāreṣv asya pada ādadhāti yajñāyajñīye bṛhati śyaite ca gīyamāne
1.13.7	āhite vāravantīyaṃ gāyati
1.13.8	pratiṣiddhāny agnyādheye sāmāni vyāhṛtībhir evodgīthaṃ bhavatīty eke
1.13.9	laukikaṃ mathitaṃ vāgnim āhṛtyāhavanīyād vā pañcamyā vyāhṛtyā caturthyā ca yatharṣy ādhānena sabhyāvasathyau saṃbhāreṣv ādadhāti
1.13.10	vyākhyāto bījahomo yajamānasya copasthānam
1.13.11	ānaśe vyānaśe sarvam āyur vyānaśe 'haṃ tvad asmi ye te agne śive tanuvāv iti caitair āhavanīyam upatiṣṭhate
1.14.1	agna āyūṃṣy agne pavasvāgne pāvaketi tisṛbhir āśvatthīs tisraḥ samidha ekaikasminn ādhānavad ādadhāty āhavanīye gārhapatye dakṣiṇāgnau sabhyāvasathyayor iti vā sarvakarmasv eṣām evānūpūrvyam
1.14.2	samudrād ūrmir vayaṃ nāma catvāri śṛṅgeti tisṛbhis tisraḥ śamīmayīr ghṛtāktāḥ preddho agne dīdihīty audumbarīṃ vidhema ta iti vaikaṅkatīṃ tāṃ savitur vareṇyasyeti śamīmayīṃ
1.14.3	tatas tūṣṇīṃ prātar agnihotraṃ juhoti
1.14.4	athavājyaṃ saṃskṛtya caturgṛhītenāṣṭagṛhītena vā srucaṃ pūrayitvā dhyāyan nārāyaṇaṃ juhoti
1.14.5	sāgnihotrasya sthāne bhavati
1.14.6	yajamāno 'pareṇa sarvān agnīṃs tiṣṭhan ye te agne śive tanuvāv iti śivābhis tanūbhir upatiṣṭhate
1.14.7	yās te agne ghorās tanuvas tābhiḥ pāpmānaṃ gaccheti yajuṣopasthāya yās te agne ghorās tanuvaḥ kṣuc ca tṛṣṇā ceti ghorābhiś ca
1.14.8	atrāmum iti dveṣyasya nāma gṛhṇāti
1.14.9	apa upaspṛśati
1.14.10	juhūṃ sruvaṃ ca saṃmṛjya pūrvavat srucaṃ pūrayitvā pūrṇāhutī juhoti
1.14.11	yajamāno varaṃ dattvā punar ghorābhir upasthāya śivābhir upatiṣṭhate
1.14.12	narya prajāṃ me gopāyātharva pituṃ me gopāya śaṃsya paśūn me gopāya sapratha sabhāṃ me gopāyāhe budhnya mantraṃ me gopāyeti pañcabhir virāṭkramaiḥ pañcāgnīn upatiṣṭhate pañcadhāgnīn iti sarvān
1.14.13	athāgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
1.14.14	upasanne paridatte haviṣy aprokṣite sabhāmadhye 'dhidevanam uddhatyāvokṣyākṣān opya teṣu hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya niṣasāda dhṛtavrata iti rājanyasya juhoti
1.14.15	pra nūnam ity āvasathe pariṣado hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya tasmin juhoti
1.15.1	uta no 'hirbudhnya ity āvasathyam abhimantrya yajamānāya śatam akṣān adhvaryur dadāti
1.15.2	teṣu paṇamāno yajamānaḥ kṛtaṃ vijitya tad annaṃ śrapayitvā sabhāsadbhyo brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pradadāti
1.15.3	ta āvasathe bhuñjate
1.15.4	kalpetāṃ dyāvāpṛthivī ye agnaya ity etābhyāṃ yathartunāmnā yajamāno 'gnīn upatiṣṭhate
1.15.5	prokṣaṇaprabhṛtīni pratipadyate
1.15.6	vārtraghnāv ājyabhāgau
1.15.7	agnir mūrdhā bhuva iti haviṣo yājyānuvākye
1.15.8	anvāhāryam āsādyāgnyādheyasyā dvādaśebhyo dakṣiṇā dadāti
1.15.9	kāmam ūrdhvaṃ deyam
1.15.10	agnīdha upabarhaṇaṃ sārvasūtram ajaṃ pūrṇapātraṃ ca brahmaṇe 'śvaṃ hotre dhenum adhvaryave 'naḍvāham
1.15.11	mithunau gāvau vāso rathaś ca sādhāraṇāni
1.15.12	yady anāḍhyo gām ekāṃ dadyāt
1.15.13	sā sarvapratyāmnāyo bhavati
1.15.14	śeṣo vyākhyātaḥ
1.16.1	athāhitāgner dvādaśarātravratāni
1.16.2	na māṃsam aśnāti na striyam upaiti nānṛtaṃ vadaty amṛnmayapāyī svayaṃ pādaśodhy akṣāralavaṇāśy aśamīdhānyaṃ bhuñjāno 'nyatra tilebhyaḥ svayam idhmahāro 'gnyāgāre saṃviśati
1.16.3	dvādaśarātram ajasrā asyāgnayaḥ
1.16.4	nāsya brāhmaṇo 'nāśvān gṛhe vaset
1.16.5	atītāsu dvādaśarātriṣu pavamānahavīṃṣy anunirvapet saṃvatsara ṛtau māse 'rdhamāse caturahe tryahe dvyahe śvobhūte sadyo vā
1.16.6	agnaye pavamānāya puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvaped agnaye pāvakāyāgnaye śucaya iti
1.16.7	trīṇi havīṃṣi sākaṃ samasyet
1.16.8	pūrvaṃ nirupyottare samasyed vā
1.16.9	āgneyenāṣṭākapālena sākam etāni havīṃṣi samasyed ity eke
1.16.10	agneḥ pavamānasyāgna āyūṃṣy agne pavasveti yājyānuvākye
1.16.11	triṃśanmānaṃ hiraṇyam asya dakṣiṇā
1.16.12	agneḥ pāvakasyāgne pāvaka sa naḥ pāvaketi
1.16.13	agneḥ śucer agniḥ śucivratatama ud agne śucayas taveti
1.16.14	triṃśanmānaṃ hiraṇyaṃ madhyamasya catvāriṃśanmānaṃ hiraṇyam uttamasya
1.16.15	aindrāgnam ekādaśakapālam anunirvapaty adityai ghṛte caruṃ
1.16.16	saptadaśādityasya sāmidhenyaḥ
1.16.17	agninā rayiṃ gayasphāna iti puṣṭimantāv ājyabhāgāv indrāgnī āgataṃ gīrbhir vipra ity aindrāgnasya
1.16.18	uta tvām adite mahīm ū ṣu mātaram ity ādityasya preddho agna imo agna iti saṃyājye
1.16.19	saṃtiṣṭhate seṣṭyādhānam
1.17.1	hoṣyan prathamam agnihotraṃ daśahotāraṃ manasānudrutya sagraham āhavanīye hutvātha sāyam agnihotraṃ juhoti
1.17.2	vyāhṛtibhiḥ prathamam agnihotram upasādayati saṃvatsare ca
1.17.3	dvādaśarātram ādhānād ajasreṣv ājyenāhatavāsāḥ svayam apravasan yajamāno 'gnihotraṃ juhoti
1.17.4	yāṃ prathamām agnihotrāya duhanti sāgnihotrasya dakṣiṇā
1.17.5	prathamau darśapūrṇamāsau yakṣyamāṇaś caturhotāraṃ manasānudrutyāhavanīye sagrahaṃ hutvā pūrṇā paścād yat te devā adadhur iti sārasvatau homau hutvā pūrvasmin parvaṇi paurṇamāsyām anvārambhaṇīyām iṣṭiṃ nirvapaty āgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālaṃ sarasvatyai caruṃ sarasvate dvādaśakapālam agnaye bhagine 'ṣṭākapālam
1.17.6	agnāviṣṇū sajoṣasāgnāviṣṇū mahi dhāmety āgnāvaiṣṇavasya
1.17.7	pra ṇo devyā no diva iti sarasvatyāḥ
1.17.8	pīpivāṃsaṃ sarasvato ye te sarasva ūrmaya iti sarasvata ā savaṃ savitur yathā sa no rādhāṃsy ābhareti bhaginaḥ
1.17.9	purastāt sviṣṭakṛto jayānupajuhoti
1.17.10	mithunau gāvau dakṣiṇā
1.17.11	amāvāsyāyāṃ bhaviṣyantyām ādadhānasya nānvārambhaṇīyā
1.17.12	āgneyam evāṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapet
1.18.1	darśapūrṇamāsau cāturmāsyān vārambhamāṇo vyāhṛtībhir havīṃṣy āsādayati saṃvatsare paryāgate ca
1.18.2	āhitāgner vratāni
1.18.3	sūryoḍho 'tithir vasatyai nāparudhyaḥ
1.18.4	yady aparudhyetāsyāgnir anugacchet
1.18.5	narbīsapakvasyāśnīyāt
1.18.6	klinnamedho nāgnāv ādadhyāt
1.18.7	nāvyantaram apo nāśnīyāt
1.18.8	svakṛta iriṇe pradare vā nāvasyen na yajeta
1.18.9	hiṃkṛtya vāgyataḥ striyaṃ saṃbhavet
1.18.10	ahute 'gnihotre nāśnīyāt
1.18.11	na naktam anyatrānnād dadyāt
1.18.12	paśunāniṣṭvā saṃvatsare na māṃsam aśnīyāt
1.18.13	ādiṣṭas tu manasāgnibhyaḥ prahiṇomīti bhakṣayati
1.19.1	punar agnyādheyasyādhānena kalpo vyākhyātaḥ
1.19.2	agniṣv āhiteṣu yo 'smin saṃvatsare bandhujyāniṃ putrajyāniṃ vābhyeti na vardhate svenāṅgena vā vyṛdhyate sa udvāsya punar ādadhīta
1.19.3	darśena pūrṇamāsena veṣṭvāgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ vaiśvānaraṃ dvādaśakapālam agnim udvāsayiṣyan nirvapet
1.19.4	agnir mūrdhā bhuva ity āgneyasya vaiśvānaro ajījanat pṛṣṭo divīti vaiśvānarasya
1.19.5	yā te agne utsīdataḥ pavamānā yā te pāvakā yā te agne sūrye śucir yās te agne kāmadughā vibhaktīr yās te agne saṃbhṛtīr ye te agne vānaspatyā agann agnir iti saptāhutīḥ purastāt sviṣṭakṛta upajuhoti
1.19.6	siddheṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
1.19.7	jvalato 'gnīn utsṛjati yāvad darśapūrṇamāsau
1.19.8	saṃvatsaraṃ dvādaśāhaṃ vā visṛṣṭāgnir bhavati
1.19.9	tadānīm evādbhir agnīn samabhyukṣya brahmaudanaṃ śrapayitvopavasati
1.19.10	rohiṇī punarvasū anūrādhāś ca punarādhānanakṣatrāṇi prāvṛṭcharadāv ṛtū
1.19.11	na saṃbhṛtyāḥ saṃbhārāḥ
1.19.12	saṃbhṛtyā vā
1.19.13	saṃbhāramantrā bhavantīty eke
1.19.14	yajūṃṣi na bhavantīty eke
1.19.15	agnyāyataneṣu saṃvatsarapravātān darbhān saṃstīrya bhūmir bhūmneti sarparājñībhir gārhapatyam ādadhāti madhyaṃdina itarān
1.19.16	sarvān vā madhyaṃdine
1.19.17	purāṇair darbhair āhavanīyaṃ śarāva uddhṛtya yat tvā kruddhaḥ parovapety anvāhāryapacanam ādadhāti yat te manyuparoptasyety āhavanīye
1.19.18	mano jyotir juṣatām ity āhitam upatiṣṭhate
1.19.19	punas tvādityā rudrā iti dvābhyām upasaminddhe
1.19.20	mano jyotir juṣatām ity āhutiṃ juhoti
1.19.21	sapta te agne samidhaḥ sapta jihvā ity agnihotraṃ juhoti
1.19.22	sā pūrṇāhutir bhavati
1.20.1	āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ pañcakapālaṃ vā nirvapati
1.20.2	prāg uttamād anūyājād upāṃśu kriyate 'gne 'gnim agnināgnir iti caturṣu prayājeṣu catasro vibhaktīr dadhāti
1.20.3	samidhāgniṃ duvasyateti budhanvaty āgneyasyājyabhāgasyehy ū ṣu bravāṇi ta itīndumatī saumyasya
1.20.4	agne tam adyādhā hy agna iti paṅktyau yājyānuvākye bhavato 'dhā hy agna ābhiṣṭe adya gīrbhir iti vā
1.20.5	punar ūrjā saha rayyety abhitaḥ puroḍāśam āhutī juhoti
1.20.6	agniṃ prati sviṣṭakṛtaṃ nirāhābhiṣ ṭe adyaibhir no arkair iti
1.20.7	triṣṭubhau saṃyājye
1.20.8	punar niṣkṛto ratho dakṣiṇā punar utsyūtaṃ vāsaḥ punar utsṛṣṭo 'naḍvān
1.20.9	agner agnāv iti dvayor anūyājayor dve vibhaktī dadhāti
1.20.10	uccair uttamam anūyājaṃ saṃpreṣyati
1.20.11	agninyaktāḥ patnīsaṃyājānām ṛcaḥ syuḥ
1.20.12	āgnivāruṇam ekādaśakapālam anunirvapet tvaṃ no agne sa tvaṃ no agna iti yājyānuvākye
1.20.13	saṃtiṣṭhate punaragnyādhānaṃ
1.20.14	yas tṛtīyam ādadhāti lekaḥ salekaḥ suleka iti sa etān homān juhuyāt
1.20.15	arthāyārthāyāhavanīyaṃ gārhapatyāt praṇayet
1.20.16	nityo dhāryo gataśriya āyuṣkāmasya vā
1.20.17	apahṛtāgner naṣṭāraṇīkasya ca brahmaudanenaiva pratipadyate pratipadyate
2.1.1	athāgnihotram
2.1.2	agnihotraṃ sāyaṃprātargṛhāṇāṃ niṣkṛtim apaśyann iti vijñāyate
2.1.3	agnihotrasya yajñakrator eka ṛtvig adhvaryuḥ
2.1.4	sāyam adhivṛkṣasūrye 'dhāstamitasūrye vā jvalantaṃ gārhapatyād āhavanīyam uddharati prātar uṣasi prāg udayād vāpi vā naktam āhavanīyaṃ dhārayet
2.1.5	sugārhapatya ud budhyasveti dvābhyāṃ gārhapatyam upasthāyoddhareti yajamānaḥ saṃpreṣyati
2.1.6	dhṛṣṭir asi brahma yacchety adhvaryur upaveṣam ādāya vācā tvā hotreti tena gārhapatyād āhavanīyam uddharati
2.1.7	ihāmehām iti yathāyony anvāhāryaṃ nidadhāti
2.1.8	bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar ity uddhṛtaṃ yajamāno 'bhimantrayate 'hnā yad ena iti sāyaṃ rātryā yad ena iti prātaḥ
2.1.9	amṛtāhutim ity āyatane pratiṣṭhāpayaty agnim agnau svāheti sāyaṃ pratyaṅmukhaḥ sūryam agnau svāheti prātaḥ prāṅmukhaḥ
2.1.10	viśvadānīm ābharanta iti svayam idhmahasto yajamāno vihāram abhyeti
2.1.11	yad agne yāni kāni ceti pañcabhiḥ pratimantram agniṣv idhmān ādadhāti
2.1.12	agne gṛhapate śundhasvety etaiḥ pañcabhiḥ paryukṣaṇaparisamūhanoparipuṣpakaraṇair agnīn alaṃkaroti purastād upariṣṭāc ca
2.1.13	darbhaiḥ prāg uttarāgram agnīn paristṛṇāti
2.2.1	uttareṇa gārhapatyam agnihotrasthālīṃ sruvam agnihotrahavaṇīṃ ca prakṣālya kūrce prayunakti pālāśīṃ samidhaṃ ca
2.2.2	iḍāsi vratabhṛd iti dakṣiṇena vihāram avasthitāṃ gām agnihotrīṃ yajamāno 'numantryeyam asīti vedim abhimṛśati
2.2.3	adhvaryuḥ pūṣāsīti vatsaṃ dakṣiṇata upasṛjya prācīm udīcīṃ vāvṛtyānyaḥ śūdrād astamita udite cāgnihotrasthālyā dogdhi dohanena ca
2.2.4	dugdhvā sthālyām ānayati
2.2.5	na saṃmṛśati
2.2.6	pūrvau dahyāj jyeṣṭhasya jyaiṣṭhineyasyety uktaṃ
2.2.7	yajamāno vidyud asīty apa upaspṛśyāpareṇāhavanīyam atikramya dakṣiṇata upaviśati patnī ca svaloke
2.2.8	sāyaṃ prātaḥ saṃdhyayor hotavyam
2.2.9	nakṣatraṃ dṛṣṭvā pradoṣe niśāyām upoṣasi purodayaṃ samayāv iṣita udite vā
2.2.10	pradoṣānto homakālaḥ sāyaṃ saṃgavāntaḥ prātaḥ
2.2.11	tam atinīya doṣā vastor namaḥ svāheti sāyaṃ caturgṛhītaṃ juhuyāt prātar vastor namaḥ svāheti prātaḥ
2.2.12	ubhayatra vyāhṛtīr japitvā varaṃ dattvā juhuyāt
2.2.13	ā prātarāhutikālāt sāyam āhutikāla ā sāyamāhutikālāt prātarāhutikāla ity āpatkalpaḥ
2.2.14	ṛtaṃ tvā satyena pariṣiñcāmīti hastena sāyaṃ pariṣiñcati satyaṃ tvarteneti prātaḥ
2.2.15	yajñasya saṃtatir asīti gārhapatyāt saṃtatām apāṃ dhārāṃ srāvayaty āhavanīyāt
2.2.16	gārhapatyaśroṇim āsādya ghṛṣṭir asīti ghṛṣṭim ādāya bhūtakṛtaḥ sthety udīco 'ṅgārān nirūhya vyantān kṛtvā sagarāḥ sthety abhimantryāgnaya ādityaṃ gṛhṇāmy ahne rātrim iti sāyaṃ homyam ādāyeḍāyāḥ padam ity aṅgāreṣv adhiśrayati
2.3.1	ādityāyāgniṃ gṛhṇāmi rātryā ahar iti prātarhomyam
2.3.2	agnis te tejo mā dhākṣīd iti darbhair abhidyotyāmṛtam asīti sruveṇa dohanasaṃkṣālanaṃ ninīya punar eva pūrvavad abhidyotyāntaritaṃ rakṣa iti triḥ paryagnikaroti
2.3.3	gharmo 'si rāyaspoṣavanir iti vartma kurvann udag udvāsayati
2.3.4	iha prajāṃ paśūn dṛṃheti vedyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpya prajāṃ me yacchety antike kṛtvā pratyūḍhaṃ janyaṃ bhayam iti gārhapatye 'ṅgārān dhṛṣṭyā pratyūhati
2.3.5	devasya tveti sruvam agnihotrahavaṇīṃ cādāya pratyuṣṭam iti niṣṭapya suparṇāṃ tvety agnihotrahavanīṃ saṃmārṣṭi
2.3.6	ariṣṭo yajamānaḥ patnī cety ubhayaṃ saṃmṛjyom unneṣyāmīti sāyaṃ yajamānam āmantrayata om unnayāmīti prātaḥ
2.3.7	yajamāno havir devānām ity upāṃśūktvom unnayety uccaiḥ pratyāha
2.3.8	unnayanaprabhṛtyā homān na caṅkramyate
2.3.9	vācaṃ yacchati
2.3.10	agnaye ca tvā pṛthivyai connayāmīti caturbhiḥ sthālyāś caturaḥ sruvān pūrṇān agnihotrahavaṇyām unnayaty uttamena dviḥ pañcāvattinaḥ
2.3.11	unnītaṃ daśahotrābhimṛśati
2.3.12	sajūr devaiḥ sāyaṃyāvabhir ity unnītaṃ sthālīṃ ca sāyaṃ saṃmṛśati sajūr devaiḥ prātar yāvabhir iti prātaḥ
2.4.1	tāṃ samidham ādāyopariṣṭāt srugdaṇḍa upasaṃgṛhya paśūn me yacchety apareṇa gārhapatyaṃ kūrce nidadhāti
2.4.2	yajamāno nama īśāpatyārcir harati
2.4.3	prāṅ haran daśahotāraṃ vyākhyāyāgnaye tvā vaiśvānarāyeti madhyadeśe nigṛhya vātāya tvety udyamyāyur me yacchety apareṇāhavanīyaṃ kūrca upasādayati
2.4.4	eṣā te agne samid iti pālāśīṃ samidham ādadhāti
2.4.5	vidyud asīty apa upaspṛśyādīptāyāṃ samidhi prāṇāyāmaṃ kṛtvā payasā ghṛtena dadhnā taṇḍulair yavāvaudanena somena vāgnir jyotir jyotir agniḥ svāheti sāyaṃ kanīyasīṃ pūrvām āhutiṃ juhuyāt sūryo jyotir jyotiḥ sūryaḥ svāheti prātaḥ
2.4.6	agnir jyotir jyotiḥ sūryaḥ svāheti sāyaṃ sūryo jyotir jyotir agniḥ svāheti prātar ity evaṃ saṃsṛṣṭahomam eke samāmananti
2.5.1	varco me yaccheti punar eva kūrce upasādayati
2.5.2	lepam ādāyottarataḥ kūrce oṣadhībhyas tvauṣadhīr jinveti lepaṃ nimṛjyāgne gṛhapateti gārhapatyaṃ dakṣiṇāvṛt pratīkṣate
2.5.3	atihāya pūrvām āhutiṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar ity uttarāṃ bhūyasīṃ juhuyāt tūṣṇīṃ vā
2.5.4	bhakṣāya bhūyaḥ kuryāt
2.5.5	hutvā bhūmānaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyet
2.5.6	srucam udgṛhya rudra mṛḍeti srucodīcīṃ jvālāṃ trir ativalgayati
2.5.7	iṣe tveti sāyaṃ lepam abhyavamārṣṭi
2.5.8	ūrje tvety ūrdhvaṃ prātar unmārṣṭi
2.5.9	kūrce srucaṃ nidhāya pitṛbhyas tvā pitṝñ jinveti dakṣiṇataḥ sthaṇḍile nīcā pāṇinā lepaṃ nimṛjya vṛṣṭir asīty apa upaspṛśya pūṣāsīti dvir anāmikāṅgulyāśiñjann atihāya dataḥ prāśyācamya punaḥ prāśnāti
2.5.10	āgneyaṃ haviḥ prajananam iti prācīnadaṇḍayā srucā bhakṣayati sauryaṃ haviḥ prajananam iti prātar dviś ca nirleḍhi
2.5.11	darbhaiḥ srucaṃ śodhayityādbhiḥ pūrayitvocchiṣṭabhājo jinvety uttareṇāhavanīyam apo visṛjet
2.6.1	tām agnihotrahavaṇīṃ niṣṭapya punas toyaiḥ saṃśodhya punar adbhiḥ pūrayitvā sarpebhyas tvā sarpāñ jinveti pūrvasyāṃ saṃsrāvyākṣitam asīti vedimadhye gṛhebhyas tvā gṛhāñ jinveti patny añjalau ca
2.6.2	sapta ṛṣīn prīṇīhīty uttareṇa gārhapatyam apāṃ śeṣaṃ visṛjet
2.6.3	sruveṇāgnaye gṛhapataye svāheti gārhapatye 'gnaye 'dābhāya svāhety anvāhāryapacane 'gnaye bhūr bhuvaḥ suvaḥ svāheti sabhye 'gnaye 'nnapataye svāhety āvasathye hutvā sarveṣu viṣṇave svāheti dvitīyāṃ juhoti
2.6.4	punaḥ pūrvavat pariṣiñcati
2.6.5	sruvādīn prakṣālyottareṇāpo visṛjya vedyāṃ nikṣipet
2.6.6	tejo mūrtir ātmā hṛdaye 'ntar ūrdhvaṃ jvalann agniśikhāmadhye sthitas tasyāḥ śikhāyā madhye param ātmeti śrutiḥ
2.6.7	tato homānte sarvatrātmānaṃ prokṣya gārhapatyād bhasmādāya lalāṭe hṛdaye kukṣau bāhvoḥ kaṇṭhe ca taj jvālārūpaṃ caturaṅgulaṃ dīpavad ūrdhvāgraṃ puṇḍraṃ kuryād yajamānaḥ
2.6.8	tena śubhaṃ labdhvātmayogam ante prāpnoti
2.7.1	uttarām āhutim anu yajamāna āyatanād utthāya kavātiryaṅṅ ivāhavanīyam upaprayanto adhvaram ity anuvākena sāyam upatiṣṭhate
2.7.2	tatrāgnīṣomāv imaṃ su ma iti pañcamyāgnīṣomīyayā pūrvapakṣa ubhā vām indrāgnī ity aindrāgnyā tatsthāne 'parapakṣe
2.7.3	agna āyūṃṣīti ṣaḍbhir uttarābhir upatiṣṭhat
2.7.4	agna āyūṃṣy agne pavasvety āgnipāvamānībhyāṃ saṃvatsare saṃvatsare gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhate pavamānahavirbhir vā yajeta
2.7.5	āyurdā agne 'syāyur me dehīty āhavanīyaṃ citrāvaso svasti te pāram aśīyeti rātrim upatiṣṭhate
2.7.6	indhānās tvā śataṃ himā ity upasaminddhe
2.7.7	saṃ tvam agna ity anuvākaśeṣeṇāhavanīyam upatiṣṭhate
2.7.8	saṃpaśyāmi prajā aham iti gṛhān paśūṃś ca
2.7.9	ambhaḥ sthāmbho va iti goṣṭham
2.7.10	revatī ramadhvam ity antarāgnī tiṣṭhañ japati
2.7.11	saṃhitāsīty agnihotryā vatsam abhimṛśaty agnihotrīṃ vā
2.7.12	apa tvāgne dive diva iti tisṛbhir gāyatrībhir agne tvaṃ na iti dvipadābhir gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhate
2.8.1	ūrjā vaḥ paśyāmīti gṛhān paśūṃś ca
2.8.2	tat savitur vareṇyam iti sāvitryāhavanīyaṃ somānaṃ svaraṇam iti ca
2.8.3	kadā cana starīr asīti rātrim
2.8.4	pari tvāgne puraṃ vayam iti gārhapatyam agne gṛhapata iti ca tām āśiṣam āśāse tantave jyotiṣmatīm ity ajātaputro 'muṣmai jyotiṣmatīm iti jātaputro 'muṣmā amuṣmā iti yāvanto 'sya putrā jātā bhavanti jyotiṣmatīm ity antato vadati
2.8.5	bhuvanam asi sahasrapoṣapuṣīti punar eva vatsam ālabhate 'gnihotrīṃ vā
2.8.6	mahi trīṇām avo 'stv iti māhitreṇa tṛcenāhavanīśam upatiṣṭhate
2.8.7	dūraṃ pravasataḥ svastikāmas tam etena tṛcena paśyet
2.8.8	svasti punar āgacchec chaddhikāmaś canaṃ japed anyatrāpi yajñāt
2.8.9	api vā bhūr bhuvaḥ suvaḥ suprajāḥ prajayā bhūyāsam iti sāyam upatiṣṭheta
2.8.10	api vā divas parīti vātsapreṇa sāyaṃ prātar upatiṣṭhate
2.9.1	payasā mumukṣoḥ śrīkāmasya vā juhuyād ājyena tejaskāmasya dadhnndriyakāmasya yavāgvā grāmakāmasyaudanenānnādyakāmasya taṇḍulair ojaskāmasya pāpmānaṃ hantukāmasya vā piṣṭena vidyākāmasya somena brahmavarcasakāmasya
2.9.2	dadhnas taṇḍulānāṃ somasya nādhiśrayaṇapratiṣecane
2.9.3	pratiṣecakāla ājyasya darbhataruṇau pratyasyet
2.9.4	parvaṇy eva rājanyasyāgnihotraṃ bhavati
2.9.5	aharahar nityaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo 'nnaṃ dīyate
2.9.6	tad etad antarāle 'syāgnihotraṃ bhavati
2.9.7	nityam agnir upastheyaḥ
2.9.8	yaḥ somayājī tasya sadāgnihotraṃ juhuyāt
2.9.9	ahar ahar yajamānaḥ svayam agnihotram juhuyācchiṣyo vā
2.9.10	dīdihi dīdyāsaṃ dīditā me 'asi svāhety agnīn upasaminddhe
2.9.11	apiprer agne svāṃ tanvam ayāḍ dyāvāpṛthivī ūrjam asmāsu dhehīty agnihotrasthālyāṃ barhir aṅktvāhavanīye 'nupraharati
2.9.12	sā hy agnihotrasya saṃsthitiḥ
2.9.13	na barhir anupraharet
2.9.14	asaṃsthito vā eṣa yajño yad agnihotram iti vijñāyate
2.10.1	yajamāno 'gnibhyaḥ pravatsyann agnīn samādhehīti saṃpreṣyati
2.10.2	śuciḥ svāyatane tiṣṭhan mama nāma prathamaṃ jātaveda iti jvalantam āhavanīyam upasthāya tat sakāśe vācaṃyamaḥ pravased asakāśe visṛjeta
2.10.3	adhaśśayyas tryupāyī
2.10.4	na daśamīm atipravasati
2.10.5	na parvaṇi
2.10.6	vratakāle vrataṃ carati
2.10.7	vihāram abhimukho 'gnīn upatiṣṭhata ihaiva san tatra sato vo agnaya iti ca
2.10.8	yady anupasthāya pravased etām eva vihāram abhimukho japet
2.10.9	proṣya samidho dhārayañ chadir darśe kaṃcid apy anādṛtyāgnīn pratīyāt
2.10.10	viśvadānīm ābharanta iti vihāram abhyetyāgnīnām sakāśe vācaṃ yacchati sakāśe visṛjate
2.10.11	agnīn samādhehīti saṃpreṣyati
2.10.12	mama nāma tava ca jātaveda ity āhavanīyam upatiṣṭhate
2.10.13	namo 'gnaye 'pratividdhāyeti gārhapatyam
2.10.14	tvat pitāra ity anvāhāryapacanam
2.10.15	ayam agniḥ śreṣṭhatama iti punar āhavanīyam
2.10.16	vratabhreṣe mano jyotir juṣatām ity āhutiṃ juhuyāt
2.10.17	pravatsyan proṣyāgataś ca virāṭkramair evopatiṣṭhata ity eke
2.10.18	pravatsyato 'dhvaryur agnīn na saminddha ity āhuḥ
2.10.19	kaḥ śreyāṃsaṃ viṣuptaṃ bodhayiṣyatīti
2.10.20	asamindhāno 'bhayaṃkarābhayaṃ me kuru svasti me 'stu pravatsyāmīti pravatsyann upatiṣṭhate 'bhayaṃkarābhayaṃ me 'kārṣīḥ svasti me 'stu prāvātsam iti proṣyāgataḥ
2.10.21	tūṣṇīm evāgnīn praṇamy apravased ity eke
2.10.22	gṛhā mā bibhīteti pañcabhir gṛhān abhyeti
2.10.23	pūrvasaṃjātam aparādhamasya tad ahar nivedayeyuḥ sa caitān nāpavadet
2.10.24	gṛhān aham iti saṃviśati
2.10.25	viśvā uta tvayā vayam iti patnīṃ samīkṣate
2.11.1	atha sagṛhaḥ pravatsyan yatra pañca nava daśa rātrīḥ saṃhitā vasati yatra vā navarātraṃ vāstu kutaś cit kāraṇāt punar abhyety ekām uṣitvā pravatsyan vāstoṣpatīyaṃ juhuyāt
2.10.1	yady anovāhyaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ syāt sarvamanasyādadhāti yad voḍhum aśakyaṃ syāt tad ahuta evopoddharanti
2.10.2	agniṣṭhasya dakṣiṇo yukto bhavati savyo 'yukto 'tha vāstoṣpata ity anudrutyottarayā gārhapatye juhoti
2.10.3	na hute 'bhyādadhāti
2.10.4	na hīnam anvāharanti
2.10.5	nāvakṣāṇāny asaṃprakṣāpya prayānti
2.10.6	ayaṃ te yonir ṛtviya iti pṛthag araṇīṣv agnīn samāropayate 'pi vā yā te agne yajñiyā tanūr ity ātmani hastaṃ pratāpya vā mukhāyāharata upāvaroha jātaveda ity ātmany ārūḍham araṇyor upāvarohya prāgastamayān manthet
2.10.7	api vā laukike 'gnāv upāvarohety upāvarohayata idaṃ śreya ity avasite juhoti juhoti
3.1.1	sarvebhyaḥ kāmebhyo darśapūrṇamāsau
3.1.2	tān yugapat kāmayeta
3.1.3	api vā pṛthakkāmaḥ pṛthag āharet
3.1.4	darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ yāvaj jīvaṃ yajeta triṃśataṃ vā varṣāṇi jīrṇo vā viramed ity eke
3.1.5	tābhyāṃ paramām eva kāṣṭhāṃ gacchatīti vijñāyate
3.1.6	tau samānopadeśau
3.1.7	vacanād vyavatiṣṭhete
3.1.8	yajamānasyaiva samaste kratau śrūyamāṇaṃ kāmānāṃ kāmanaṃ brahmacaryaṃ dravyopasthāpanaṃ dakṣiṇādānam akarmakaraṇā mantrāḥ pratyag āśiṣaḥ
3.1.9	candramasūnaṃ pūrṇaṃ vā vijñāya pūrvasmin parvaṇi paurṇamāsena yakṣya ity uktvā keśaśmaśrūṇi vāpayitvopavasati
3.1.10	candramasaṃ duṣṭam aduṣṭaṃ vā vijñāya caiva darśena yakṣya ity uktvopavasati
3.1.11	adhvaryuḥ prātaragnihotraṃ hutvānugamayitvāpoddhṛtya vodita āditye dhyāyan nārāyaṇaṃ viṣṇor nu kam iti japitvā gārhapatyād āhavanīyam uddhṛtyāhavanīyāyatane 'gniṃ pratiṣṭhāpya devā gātuvida iti japitvā mamāgne varca iti samidham anvādadhāti
3.2.1	yajamāno 'gniṃ gṛhṇāmi surathaṃ vasūn rudrān imām ūrjam iti trīn āhavanīye 'nvādhīyamāne japati paurṇamāsaṃ havir iti paurṇamāsyām āmāvāsyaṃ havir ity amāvāsyāyām
3.2.2	antarāgnī paśava ity antarāgnī tiṣṭhañ japati
3.2.3	adhvaryur mama devā iti gārhapatyam anvādadhāti
3.2.4	iha prajā iha paśava iti dvau yajamāno japati
3.2.5	adhvaryur mayi devā ity anvāhāryapacanam anvādadhāti
3.2.6	ayaṃ pitṝṇām iti yajamāno japati
3.2.7	vyāhṛtībhir anvādadhātīty eke
3.2.8	ajasraṃ tvāṃ sabhāpālā ity adhvaryuḥ sabhyam anvādadhati
3.2.9	tam eva yajamāno japati
3.2.10	annam āvasathīyam ity adhvaryur āvasathyam anvādadhāti
3.2.11	tam eva yajamāno japati
3.2.12	adhvaryuṇānvāhiteṣv idam aham agnijyeṣṭhebhya ity uttarata upaviśati japati
3.2.13	payasvatīr oṣadhaya iti prāg barhiṣaḥ paurṇamāsyāṃ dampatī māṣamāṃsavarjaṃ sarpiṣā dadhnā payasā vā miśram aśnītaḥ prāg vatsebhyo 'māvāsyāyām
3.2.14	kāmaṃ suhitau syātām
3.2.15	vidyud asīty apa upaspṛśyāpareṇāhavanīyaṃ dakṣiṇātikramya payasvatīr oṣadhaya ity apa ācāmati
3.2.16	devā deveṣu parākramadhvam iti devatā upatiṣṭhate
3.2.17	agne vratapata iti pañcabhir āhavanīye samidho 'bhyādadhāti
3.2.18	samudraṃ manasā dhyāyann agne vratapate vrataṃ cariṣyāmīti pañcabhir yathāliṅgaṃ devatā upatiṣṭhamāno vratam upaiti
3.2.19	samrāḍ asīty ādityam upatiṣṭhate
3.2.20	yady astam ite vratam upeyād āhavanīyam evaitenopatiṣṭhate
3.2.21	parvaṇi yajamānaḥ svayam agnihotraṃ juhoti yavāgvām āvāsyāyāṃ saṃ nayann agnihotroccheṣaṇam ātañcanāya nidadhāti
3.2.22	satyavādyas try upāyī sāyamāśe grāmyān upavasatyāraṇyasyāśnāty apo vāśnāti na vā kiṃcana
3.2.23	yena prātar yakṣyamāṇaḥ syāt tannāśnīyāt
3.3.1	upetavratasya saṃnayato 'dhvaryuḥ saṃgava iṣe tveti bahuparṇāṃ bahuśākhām aśuṣkāgrāṃ prācīm udīcīṃ vā palāśaśākhāṃ śamīśākhāṃ vācchinatty urje tvety anumārṣṭi saṃnamayati vā
3.3.2	imāṃ prācīm ity āharati
3.3.3	vāyavaḥ stheti tayā tryavarān vatsān apākaroti
3.3.4	sadarbhayā tayety eke darbhair vā
3.3.5	devā va iti tryavarā vatsamātṛgocaram abhi prerayati
3.3.6	śuddhā apa iti preritā anumantrayate
3.3.7	dhruvā asminn iti yajamānam īkṣate
3.3.8	agrenāhavanīyaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ śākhām āhṛtyāpareṇa gārhapatyaṃ yajamānasya paśūn pāhīty agniṣṭhe 'nasi mekhalāyāṃ vā nidadhāti
3.3.9	devasya tvety aśvaparśum asidaṃ vādāya yajñasya ghoṣad asīty abhimantrayate gārhapatyaṃ vopatiṣṭhate
3.3.10	pratyuṣṭam iti tasmin niṣṭapati
3.3.11	preyam agād ity urv antarikṣaṃ prehīti cahavanīyam abhipraiti
3.4.1	iha barhir āsada iti vediṃ pratyavekṣate
3.4.2	yatra barhir dāsyan bhavati tām diśam etya viṣṇoḥ stūpo 'sīty ekaṃ stambam utsṛjya devānāṃ pariṣūtam asīty anyaṃ pariṣauti
3.4.3	paśūnāṃ tvā bhāgam utsṛjāmīti pariṣūtasyaikāṃ darbhanāḍīm utsṛjyedaṃ devānām iti pariṣūtam abhimṛśyedaṃ paśūnām ity utsṛṣṭam abhimṛśya devasya tveti pariṣūtam abhigṛhya devabhyas tvety ūrdhvam unmṛjya deva barhir ity asidaṃ nidhāya yā jātā ity abhimantryācchettā ta ity ācchindand saṃnakhaṃ muṣṭiṃ dāti
3.4.4	sa prastaraḥ
3.4.5	etayaivāvṛtā pariṣavaṇotsarjanavarjam itarāṃs trīn pañca sapta vā muṣṭīn nidhanāni vā dāti yāvad āptaṃ bhavati
3.4.6	devabarhir ity āvraścanāny abhimṛśati
3.4.7	sahsravalśā ity ātmānaṃ pratyabhimṛśyādityai rāsnāsīti pradakṣiṇaṃ śulbam āveṣṭyāyupitā yonir iti tridhātu pañcadhātu vā pratidadhāti
3.4.8	dhātau dhātau mantram āvartayati
3.4.9	pṛthivyāḥ saṃpṛcaḥ pāhīti śulbaṃ prāgagram udagagraṃ vāstīryāparimitānām ity abhimantrya susaṃbhṛtā tveti yathālūnaṃ śulbe muṣṭīn nidhanāni vā saṃbharati
3.4.10	alubhitā yonir ity uttame prastaram
3.4.11	apāṃ medhyaṃ yajñiyam iti pitṛbhyaḥ samūlam upamūlalūnaṃ vā sakṛd ācchinnaṃ barhir ācchadya tūṣṇīṃ saṃbharati paribhojanīyaṃ ca
3.4.12	indrāṇyai saṃnahanam iti sarvān saṃnahya pūṣā ta iti pradakṣiṇaṃ grathnāti
3.4.13	sa te māsthād iti paścāt prāñcaṃ granthim upagūhati
3.4.14	āpas tvām aśvināv iti spṛśati
3.4.15	indrasya tvety udyamya bṛhaspater iti śīrṣṇā harati
3.4.16	urv antarikṣam anvihīti pratyetyādityāḥ sadety apareṇāhavanīyam andhaḥ sādayati
3.4.17	devaṃgamam asīty abhimantryādityās tvā pṛṣṭhe sādayāmīti gārhapatyadeśa uparīva nidadhāti
3.5.1	tūṣṇīṃ tridhātu śulbaṃ kṛtvā yat kṛṣṇo rūpam iti pālāśena khādireṇa yākṣikair vā vṛkṣair ekaviṃśatidārum idhmaṃ saṃbhṛtya kṛṣṇo 'sy ākharestha iti saṃnahya pūṣā ta iti pradakṣiṇaṃ granthiṃ kṛtvā barhiḥkalpena barhiṣā saha nidadhāti
3.5.2	vedo 'sīti vatsajñuṃ trivṛcchirasaṃ dārbhaṃ vedaṃ kṛtvāgrāt prādeśe parivāsayati
3.5.3	parivāsitāni vedāgrāṇīdhmapravraścanaiḥ saha nidadhāti
3.5.4	atrāmāvāsyāyāṃ vediṃ kṛtvedhmābarhir āhared ity eke
3.5.5	antarvedi śākhāyāḥ parṇāni pracchidya mūlataḥ śākhāṃ parivāsyopaveṣo 'si yajñāyety apareṇa gārhapatyaṃ mūlam upaveṣāya nidadhāti
3.5.6	tṛtīyasyai diva iti parivāsanaśakalam ādāya surakṣitaṃ nidhāya vasūnāṃ pavitram asi śatadhāram iti śākhāyāṃ trivṛd darbhamayaṃ pavitraṃ kṛtvā trivṛt palāśe darbha iti śākhāyāṃ śithilaṃ mūle mūlāny agre 'grāṇy avasajati
3.5.7	na granthiṃ karoti
3.5.8	agnyagāre 'gny āyatanānām upalepanādi devārhaṇy alaṃkaraṇāni dampatī cālaṃkurvāte
3.6.1	atropavasathe 'māvāsyāyām aparāhṇe 'dhivṛkṣasūrye vā piṇḍapitṛyajñena yajate
3.6.2	hute sāyam agnihotre vaikaṅkatīm agnihotrahavaṇīṃ kumbhīm upaveṣaṃ śākhāpavitram abhidhānīṃ nidāne dohanaṃ dārupātram ayaspātraṃ vaitāni sāṃnāyyapātrāṇi prakṣālyottareṇa gārhapatyaṃ darbhair antardhāyāvācīnāni prayunakti
3.6.3	samāvagravantau darbhau prādeśamātrau pavitre kṛtvā pavitre stha iti chinatti na nakhena
3.6.4	imau prāṇāpāṇāv ity abhimantrya viṣṇor manasā pūte stha ity adbhir anumṛjya gāṃ dohapavitre iti saṃpreṣyati
3.6.5	agnihotrahavaṇyāṃ pavitrāntarhitāyām apa ānīya devo va iti paccho gāyatryodagagrābhyāṃ pavitrābhyāṃ trir utpūyāpo devīr ity abhimantrayata uttanīkṛtya pātrāṇi śundhadhvam iti prokṣati
3.6.6	surakṣite pavitre nidhāyaitā ācarantīti gā āyatīḥ pratīkṣya niṣṭaptam iti sāṃnāyyapātrāṇi pratitapya dhṛṣṭir asīty upaveṣam ādāya bhūtakṛtaḥ stheti gārhapatyād udīco 'ṅgārān vyasya mātariśvana iti teṣu kumbhīm adhiśritya bhṛgūṇām aṅgirasām iti pradakṣiṇam aṅgāraiḥ paryūhati
3.7.1	vasūnāṃ pavitram asi śatadhāram iti kumbhyāṃ śākhāpavitraṃ prāgagraṃ sāyam adhinidadhāti vasūnāṃ pavitram asi sahasradhāram ity udīcīnāgraṃ prātaḥ
3.7.2	kumbhīm anvārabhya vācaṃyamaḥ pavitraṃ dhārayann āste
3.7.3	upasṛṣṭāṃ me prabrūtād iti saṃpreṣyati
3.7.4	upasṛjāmīty āmantryādityai rāsnāsīty abhidhānīm ādatte
3.7.5	pūṣāsīti vatsam upasṛjati
3.7.6	vihāraṃ gāṃ copasṛṣṭām antareṇa mā saṃcāriṣṭeti saṃpreṣyati
3.7.7	yady antareṇa saṃcaret sāṃnāyyaṃ mā vilopīti japet
3.7.8	yakṣmā vaḥ prajayā saṃsṛjāmīty abhimantrayate
3.7.9	ūrjaṃ paya iti dogdhopasīdati
3.7.10	dyauś cemam iti duhyamānām anumantrayata utsaṃ duhanti kalaśam iti dhārāghoṣaṃ hutaḥ stoko huto drapsa iti vipruṣaḥ svāhā dyāvāpṛthivībhyām iti skannān
3.7.11	kāmadhukṣa iti payaḥ pratyāharantaṃ dogdhāraṃ pṛcchati
3.7.12	amūṃ yasyām iti dogdhā pratyāha
3.7.13	sā viśvāyur iti gām adhvaryur upastauti
3.7.14	devas tvā saviteti payaḥ kumbhyām ānayati
3.7.15	kāmdhukṣa ity āha tṛtīyasyā ity uktam
3.7.16	sā viśvavyacā iti dvitīyāṃ sā viśvakarmeti tṛtīyām upastauti
3.7.17	evaṃ tisro dohayitvā bahu dogdhīndrāya devebhya iti triḥ saṃpreṣyati
3.7.18	indrayājina indram upalakṣayen mahendrayājino mahendram
3.7.19	visṛṣṭavāg ananvārabhyaṃ tūṣṇīm uttarā dohayati
3.8.1	sarvāsu dugdhāsu dohane 'pa ānīya dyauś cemam yajñam iti saṃkṣālya saṃpṛcyadhvam iti kumbhyām ānīya śrapayitvā tūṣṇīkena ghṛtenābhighārya dṛṃha gā iti karṣann ivodagudag vāsayati
3.8.2	śītīkṛtya yat pūrvedyur dugdhaṃ dadhy ekasyā dvayos tisṛṇāṃ vā gavāṃ dvyahe tryahe vā saṃtatam abhidugdham aupavasathādd havir ātañcanam upakḷptaṃ tena dadhnā somena tvātanacmīty ātanakti
3.8.3	yajñasya saṃtatir asīty agnihotrocchiṣeṇam anvātacyāyaṃ paya iti parṇavalkam anvātanakti taṇḍulaiḥ pūtikair oṣadhībhiḥ kvalair darbair vā
3.8.4	āpo haviṣv ity ayaspātre dārupātre vāpa ānīyād astam asi viṣṇave tvety apidadhāti
3.8.5	yadi mṛnmayaṃ tṛṇaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ vānupravidyet
3.8.6	imau parṇaṃ ca darbhaṃ ceti vimucya śākhāpavitraṃ surakṣitaṃ nidhāya viṣṇo havyaṃ rakṣasveti sāṃnāyaṃ gārhapatyadeśa uparīva guptaṃ nidadhāti
3.9.1	pūrvayā śākhayānyām āhṛtya vā prātardohāya vatsān apākaroti
3.9.2	upadhāya kapālāni prātardogdhi yathā sāyam
3.9.3	nātanakti
3.9.4	nāsomayājī saṃnayet
3.9.5	asomayājy apīty eke
3.9.6	aindraṃ sāṃnāyyam
3.9.7	someneṣṭvā mahendraṃ yajeta
3.9.8	api vā saṃvatsaram evendram iṣṭvāgnaye vratapataye 'ṣṭākapālaṃ nirupya kāmaṃ mahendraṃ yajeta
3.9.9	aurvo bhāradvājo gautamaḥ śṛśruvān grāmaṇī rājanya iti sarvatra kāmaṃ mahendraṃ yajeran
3.9.10	paristṛṇīteti darbhair agnīn paristṛṇāti
3.9.11	āraṇyān śitvā yajamāna ubhāv agnī iti paristīryamāṇeṣu japati
3.9.12	āhavanīyāgare gārhapatyāgāre vādhaḥ śayīta
3.9.13	amāvāsyāṃ rātriṃ jāgarty api vā yathāśakti jāgaraṇam
3.9.14	vratacārī tv eva syāt
3.9.15	vihārād apaparyāvarteta
3.9.16	etat sarvam amāvāsyāyām
3.9.17	paurṇamāsyāṃ tu pūrvedyur agnyanvādhānam idhmābarhir vedaṃ ca karotīty agniparistraṇaṃ ca
3.9.18	sadyo vā sarvaṃ bhavati bhavati
4.1.1	śvo bhūte prātar agnihotraṃ hutvodita āditye paurṇamāsyās tantram ārabhate prāg udayād amāvāsyāyāḥ
4.1.2	darśapūrṇamāsayor yajñakratvoś catvāra ṛtvijo brahmā hotādhvaryur agnīd iti
4.1.3	karmaṇe vām iti pāṇiṃ prakṣālya yajñasya saṃtatir asīti gārhapatyāt saṃtatam āhavanīyād ulaparājiṃ stṛṇāti tūṣṇīṃ dakṣiṇām uttarāṃ ca
4.1.4	dakṣiṇena āhavanīyaṃ brahmayajamānayor āsane karoti pūrvaṃ brahmaṇe 'paraṃ yajamānāya
4.1.5	uttareṇa gārhapatyaṃ darbhān saṃstīrya yajñāyudhāni dvandvaṃ nyañci sādayati sphyaṃ ca kapālāni cāgnihotrahavanīṃ ca śūrpaṃ ca kṛṣṇājinaṃ ca śamyāṃ colūkhalaṃ ca musalaṃ ca dṛṣac copalāṃ ceti pañca dvandvāni
4.1.6	khādiraṃ sruvaṃ pālāśīṃ juhūm āśvatthīm upabhṛtaṃ vaikaṅkatīṃ dhruvāṃ vedaṃ pātrīṃ mekṣaṇaṃ prāśitraharaṇam iḍāpātraṃ praṇītāpraṇayanam iti pañca dvandvāny ājyasthālīm anvāhāryasthālīm aśmānaṃ sāṃnāyyapātrāṇi saṃnayataḥ kumbhīṃ śākhāpavitram upaveṣam abhidhānīṃ nidāne dohanaṃ ca pūrvedyuḥ kṛte pavitre cāṣṭau dārupātrāṇi yāny ahomārthāni tāni vāraṇāni yena cārthaḥ
4.1.7	atra yajamāno bhūpate bhuvanapata iti brahmiṣṭhaṃ brahmāṇaṃ vṛtvāpareṇāhavanīyaṃ dakṣiṇātikramya dakṣiṇata udaṅmukha upaviśati
4.2.1	vṛto brahmā suprakṣālitapāṇipāda ācānto 'pareṇāhavanīyaṃ dakṣiṇātikramya dakṣiṇatas tiṣṭhan namo brahmaṇa iti brahmasadanam upasthāyāhe daidhiṣavyeti sadanāt tṛṇaṃ nirasyon nivata ud udvataś ca geṣam ity upaviśya pātaṃ mā dyāvāpṛthivī iti dyāvāpṛthivī samīkṣya bhūr bhuvaḥ suvaḥ ka idaṃ brahmety ahaṃ bhūpatir ity etau japitvā
4.2.2	mantravatsu karmasu vācaṃ yacchati
4.2.3	yadi vyāhared vaiṣṇavīm ṛcaṃ vyāhṛtīś ca japitvā vācaṃ yacchati
4.2.4	adhvaryur atrāsaṃnayataḥ pavitre kṛtvā dakṣāya tveti praṇītāpraṇayanaṃ camasam ādāya vānaspatyo 'sīty adbhis triḥ prakṣālayati
4.2.5	godohanena paśukāmasya praṇayen mṛnmayenānnādyakāmasya kaṃsena brahmavarcasakāmasya
4.2.6	apareṇa gārhapatyaṃ pavitrāntarhite camase ko vo gṛhṇāti sa vo gṛhṇātv ity apa ānayati
4.2.7	anayā vo grahīṣyāmīti pṛthivīṃ dhyāyann adbhiḥ pūrayitvā devo va iti pūrvavad utpūyābhimantrayate
4.3.1	brahmann apaḥ praṇeṣyāmi yajamāna vācaṃ yaccheti saṃpreṣyati
4.3.2	praṇaya yajñam iti brahmaṇā prasūtaḥ praṇayan vācaṃ yacchaty ā haviṣkṛto yajamānaś ca
4.3.3	ko3 vaḥ praṇayati sa vaḥ praṇayatv iti sphyenopayamya prāṇaiḥ samaṃ dhārayamāṇo 'viṣiñcan praṇayati
4.3.4	yāḥ purastād bhūś ca kaś ceti dvābhyāṃ yajamānaḥ praṇīyamānā anumantrayate brahmapūtā stheti cānena
4.3.5	adhvaryur uttareṇāhavanīyaṃ darbheṣu sādayitvā darbhair apidadhāti
4.3.6	tāḥ praṇītā neṅgayanty ā saṃkhyānāt
4.3.7	pavitre ādāya saṃviśantām iti sapavitreṇa pāṇinā pātrāṇi saṃmṛśati
4.3.8	dakṣāya tvā vānaspatyo 'sīty agnihotrahavaṇīm ādāya veṣāya tveti savyena śūrpaṃ ca pratyuṣṭam iti gārhapatye niṣṭapya yajamāna havir nirvapsyāmīti yajamānam āmantrayate
4.3.9	oṃ nirvapeti yajamānena prasūtaḥ pravasaty agne havir nirvapsyāmīty uktvorv antarikṣam anvihīti gacchati
4.4.1	apareṇa gārhapatyaṃ prāgīṣam udagīṣaṃ vāgniṣṭhaṃ śakaṭam avasthitaṃ vrīhimat parīṇaṭasahitaṃ bhavati yavamad vā
4.4.2	dhūr asīti tasya dakṣiṇāṃ dhuram abhimṛśya savyāṃ ca tvaṃ devānām iti śakaṭam abhimantrya viṣṇus tvākraṃsteti viṣṇum ātmānaṃ dhyāyan savye cakre dakṣiṇaṃ pādam ādadhāti viṣṇoḥ kramo 'sīti vā
4.4.3	ahrutam ity ārohati
4.4.4	mitrasya tveti parīṇāhādikaṃ prekṣyoru vātāyeti tasya dvāram apacchidya mitrasya tveti puroḍāśyāṃś ca prekṣyorjaṃ dhatsvety abhimṛśyāpahataṃ rakṣa iti tṛṇaṃ kiṃśāru vā nirasyāpa upaspṛśya havir nirvapsyan daśahotāraṃ vyācakṣīta
4.4.5	pavitrāntarhite śūrpe havanīṃ nidhāya yacchantām iti muṣṭiṃ pūrayitvā havanyām opya devasya tveti pavitrāntarhite śūrpe yathādevataṃ caturo muṣṭīn nirvapati trir mantreṇa tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
4.4.6	nirupyānvāvapati
4.4.7	evam uttaraṃ puroḍāśaṃ nirvapati
4.4.8	agniṃ hotāram iha taṃ huva iti yajamāno havir nirupyamāṇam abhimantrayate niruptaṃ vā
4.4.9	kas tvā yunakti sa tvā yunaktv iti sarvam anuvīkṣate
4.5.1	yadi śakaṭaṃ na syād apareṇa gārhapatyaṃ sphyaṃ nidhāya tasmin pātrīṃ tasyāṃ puroḍāśyān opya tasyāḥ pūrvārdhaṃ dhūr asīty abhimṛśya sarvāñchakaṭamantrān uktvā
4.5.2	idaṃ devānām iti niruptān abhimṛśati
4.5.3	idam u naḥ sahety apādānasthānam
4.5.4	sphātyai tveti niruptān eva
4.5.5	idam ahaṃ nir varuṇasya pāśād iti puroḍāśyān ādāya nirgacchati
4.5.6	suvar abhi vi khyeṣam iti sarvaṃ yajñam anuvīkṣate
4.5.7	āgneyo 'ṣṭākapāla upāṃśuyājaś cājyaṃ haviḥ prājāpatyo vaiṣṇavo 'gnīṣomīyo vāgnīṣomīyaś caikādaśakapālaḥ paurṇamāsyāṃ pradhānāni
4.5.8	nāsomayājino brāhmaṇasyāgnīṣomīyaḥ puroḍāśo vidyata ity eke
4.5.9	āgneyo 'ṣṭākapāla aindraṃ sāṃnāyyam amāvāsyāyāṃ saṃnayataḥ
4.5.10	asaṃnayata āgneyo 'ṣṭākapāla aindrāgna ekādaśakapālo dvādaśakapālo vā
4.5.11	tad aṅgam itare homāḥ
4.5.12	paurṇamāsyām indrāya vaimṛdhāya puroḍāśam ekādaśakapālam anunirvapet
4.5.13	yadi samānatantro vaimṛdho 'gnīṣomābhyāṃ nirupyendrāya vaimṛdhāya nirvapati
4.5.14	saṃsthitāyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vaimṛdham anunirvapatīty eke
4.6.1	vaiśvānaraṃ jyotir ity āhavanīyaṃ pratīkṣate
4.6.2	dṛṃhantāṃ duryā iti pratyavarohati
4.6.3	svāhā dyāvāpṛthivībhyām iti skannān abhimantryorv antarikṣam anvihīti hṛtvādityās tvopasthe sādayāmīty apareṇa gārhapatyaṃ yathādevatam upasādayaty uttareṇa vāgne havyaṃ rakṣasveti gārhapatyaṃ vopatiṣṭhate
4.6.4	saśūkāyāṃ tiraḥ pavitraṃ havanyāṃ prokṣaṇīḥ saṃskṛtya brahman prokṣiṣyāmīty āmantrya prokṣa yajñam iti tena prasūto devasya tveti yathādevataṃ triḥ prokṣet
4.6.5	nāgnim abhiprokṣet
4.6.6	pūrvavat pātrāṇi prokṣati
4.6.7	vātasya dhrājir asīti kṛṣṇājinam ādāyāvadhūtaṃ rakṣa ity ūrdhvagrīvaṃ bahir viśasanam utkare trir avadhūnoti
4.6.8	adityās tvag asīti purastāt pratīcīnagrīvam uttaralomopastṛṇāti
4.6.9	adhiṣavaṇam asīty anutsṛjan tasminn ulūkhalam adhivartayati
4.6.10	agnes tanūr asīty anutsṛjann ulūkhale havir āvapati trir mantreṇa tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
4.6.11	adrir asīti musalam ādāyāva rakṣo divaḥ sapatnaṃ badhyāsam iti trir avahanti
4.6.12	haviṣkṛd ehīti trir haviṣkṛtam āhvayati brāhmaṇasya haviṣkṛd āgahīti rājanyasya haviṣkṛd ādraveti vaiśyasya haviṣkṛd ādhāveti rathakārasya
4.6.13	haviṣkṛtā vācaṃ visṛjya kas tvā yunakti sa tvā yunaktv iti yajamāno yajñayogena yajñaṃ yunakti
4.7.1	prādurbhūteṣu taṇḍuleṣūccaiḥ samāhantavā iti saṃpreṣyati
4.7.2	adrir asi ślokakṛd ity āgnīdhro 'śmānam ādāyeṣam āvadorjam āvadeti vṛṣāraveṇa dṛṣad upale samāhanti śamyayā vā dvir dṛṣadi sakṛd upalāyām
4.7.3	triḥ saṃcārayan nava kṛtvaḥ saṃpādayati
4.7.4	uttuṣān kṛtvā varṣavṛddham asīti purastād uttarato vā śūrpam upayacchati
4.7.5	varṣavṛddhāḥ stheti puroḍāśyān abhimṛśya prati tvā varṣavṛddhaṃ vetv ity udvapati
4.7.6	parāpūtaṃ rakṣa ity utkare niṣpunāti
4.7.7	praviddhaṃ rakṣaḥ parādhmātā amitrā iti śūrpāt tuṣān kapāle dhvaṃsayati rakṣasāṃ bhāgo 'sīti tena tuṣāpūritenottaram aparam avāntaradeśam adhastāt kṛṣṇājinasya savyena pāṇinā tuṣān upavapati nānvīkṣate
4.7.8	avabāḍhaṃ rakṣa ity avabādhate
4.7.9	raudrākṣasanairṛtapaitṛkachedanabhedanakhanananirasanāvaghrāṇātmābhimarśanāni ca kṛtvā sarvatrāpa upaspṛśet
4.7.10	abhyukṣya kapālaṃ nidadhāti
4.7.11	vāyur va iti vivinakti
4.7.12	devo va iti pātryāṃ taṇḍulān praskandayati
4.7.13	adabdhena vaś cakṣuṣāvapaśyāmīty avekṣya viviktān avahantre prayacchaṃs triṣphalīkartavā iti saṃpreṣyati
4.7.14	devebhyaḥ śundhadhvaṃ devebhyaḥ śumbhadhvaṃ devebhyaḥ śudhyadhvam iti tribhis triṣphalīkaroti
4.8.1	suphalīkṛtān prakṣālya triṣphalīkriyamāṇānām ity antarvedi triḥ prakṣālanaṃ ninayati
4.8.2	kṛṣṇājinakalpo vyākhyātaḥ
4.8.3	divaḥ skambhanir asīti kṛṣṇājina udīcīnakumbāṃ śamyāṃ nidhāya dhiṣaṇāsi parvatyeti tasyāṃ prācīṃ dṛṣadaṃ paścārdhenādhivartayati
4.8.4	dhiṣaṇāsi pārvateyīti dṛṣady upalāṃ pūrvavad anutsṛjan
4.8.5	aṃśavaḥ stha madhumanta iti taṇḍulān avekṣya devasya tveti dṛṣadi yathādevataṃ taṇḍulān adhivapati trir mantreṇa tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
4.8.6	prāṇāya tveti prācīṃ prohaty apānāya tveti pratīcīṃ vyānāya tveti madhyadeśe dīrghām anv iti prācīm antataḥ
4.8.7	ata ūrdhvaṃ yathāsukhaṃ pinaṣṭi
4.8.8	devo va iti kṛṣṇājine piṣṭāni praskandayet
4.8.9	adabdhena tvā cakṣuṣāvekṣa ity avekṣyāsaṃvapantī piṃṣāṇūni kurutād iti haviḥpeṣīṃ saṃpreṣyati
4.8.10	sā pinaṣṭi
4.8.11	atra madantīr adhiśrayati
4.8.12	gārhapatye havīṃṣi śrapayati
4.8.13	dhṛṣṭir asīty upaveṣam ādāyāpahataṃ rakṣa ity abhimantrya tenāpareṇāgneḥ pratyañcāv aṅgārau vyasyāpāgne 'gnim iti dakṣiṇam aṅgāraṃ nirasyāpa upaspṛśyā devayajaṃ vahety avaśiṣṭam avasthāpya dhruvam asīti tasmin kapālam upadadhāti
4.9.1	nirdagdham iti tasminn aṅgāram adhivartayati dhartram asi iti tasmāt pūrvaṃ dharuṇam asīti tasmāt pūrvam
4.9.2	aṣṭākapālasya dve madhyamād dakṣiṇe trīṇy uttarāṇi dakṣiṇayor dharmāsīti pūrvaṃ marutāṃ śardha ity aparam
4.9.3	yantram asīty uttareṣām aparaṃ viśvābhya iti pūrvaṃ cid asīti madhyamam
4.9.4	tata uttara ekādaśakapālasyāṣṭākapālavat trīṇy upadadhāti cid asīti tat pūrvaṃ caturthaṃ yathoktam avāntaradeśeṣu
4.9.5	citaḥ sthety avaśiṣṭāni
4.9.6	bhṛgūṇām aṅgirasām iti vedena kapāleṣv aṅgārān adhyūhati
4.9.7	yāni gharma ity anudrutyendravāyū yuṅktām iti kapālāni yunakti
4.9.8	pātryāṃ niṣṭapyopavātāyāṃ pavitrāntarhitāyāṃ devasya tveti kṛṣṇājināt piṣṭāni yathādevataṃ saṃvapati trir mantreṇa tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
4.9.9	saṃvapan vācaṃ yacchaty abhivāsayan visṛjate
4.9.10	devo va iti prokṣaṇīvat piṣṭāny utpūya sruveṇa praṇītābhya ādāya vedenopayamya sam āpa iti piṣṭeṣu ninayati
4.9.11	yadi praṇītā na vidyeran yāḥ kāś cāpo mantreṇotpūya tābhiḥ saṃnayed ity āpatkalpaḥ
4.9.12	adbhyaḥ pari prajātāḥ stheti madantīr ninayati
4.9.13	sam adbhiḥ pracyadhvam iti pradakṣiṇaṃ pariplāvayati
4.10.1	janayatyai tvā saṃyaumīti saṃyutya makhasya śiro 'sīti piṇḍaṃ kṛtvā yathābhāgaṃ vyāvartethām iti vibhajati
4.10.2	samau piṇḍau kṛtvedam agnaya ity āgneyam abhimṛśatīdam amuṣmā iti yathādevatam
4.10.3	idam ahaṃ senāyā iti vedena dakṣiṇakapālayogād aṅgārān apohaty uttarasmāc ca
4.10.4	makhasya śiro 'sīti dakṣiṇaṃ piṇḍam ādāya gharmo 'si viśvāyur iti dakṣiṇasminn adhiśrayati
4.10.5	evam uttaram
4.10.6	anuccam anatinīcaṃ kūrmasyeva pratikṛtiṃ karoti
4.10.7	uru prathasveti yāvatkapālaṃ prathayati
4.10.8	pātryām apa ānīya tvacaṃ gṛhṇīṣveti pradakṣiṇaṃ salepādbhiḥ ślakṣṇīkurvann anatikṣārayann anuparimārṣṭi
4.10.9	dadhy upanidhāyāntaritaṃ rakṣa ity ulmukena triḥ sarvāṇi havīṃṣi paryagnikaroti
4.10.10	devas tvā savitā śrapayatv iti dakṣiṇaṃ puroḍāśaṃ darbhair abhijvalayañ chrapayati
4.10.11	agne havyaṃ rakṣasveti gārhapatyāgnim abhimantrayate
4.10.12	saṃ brahmaṇā pṛcyasveti vedena puroḍāśe sāṅgāraṃ bhasmābhivāsayati
4.10.13	avidahantaḥ śrapayateti vācaṃ visṛjate
4.10.14	aṅguliprakṣālanaṃ pātranirṇejanaṃ colmukenābhitapya hṛtvāntarvedi sphyenodīcīs tisro lekhāḥ kṛtvaikatāya svāheti tribhiḥ paścāt tisṛṣu lekhāsv asaṃsṛṣṭaṃ ninayati
4.11.1	apareṇāhavanīyaṃ yajamānāyatām aparimitāṃ vā vediṃ karoti yāvad arthavistārāṃ
4.11.2	yajamāna idaṃ tasmai harmyaṃ karomīti vedideśam abhimṛśati
4.11.3	adhvaryur ayaṃ veda iti vedam ādāya vedena vediṃ vividur iti vediṃ purastāt triḥ saṃmārṣṭi
4.11.4	catuḥśikhaṇḍeti yajamānaḥ saṃmṛjyamānām anumantrayate
4.11.5	adhvaryuḥ pūrvārdhād veder vitṛtīyadeśāt stambayajur harati
4.11.6	devasya tveti sphyam ādāyendrasya bāhur asīty abhimantrya vāyur asīti tasya darbheṇāgraṃ tīkṣṇīkṛtya pṛthivyai varmāsīti prāgagram udagagraṃ vā darbhaṃ nidhāya pṛthivi devayajanīti tasmin sphyena prahṛtyāpahato 'rarur iti sphyena sadarbhamūlān pāṃsūn apādāya vrajaṃ gaccheti harati
4.11.7	yo mā hṛdeti yajamāno hriyamāṇam abhimantrayate
4.11.8	varṣatu te dyaur ity adhvaryur vedim avekṣate varṣatu te parjanya iti yajamānaṃ ca
4.11.9	namo diva ity āgnīdhra uttarataḥ prakrame 'parimite vottānau hastau kṛtvopaviśati
4.11.10	tasyāñjalāv adhvaryur badhāna deva savitar iti sadarbhamūlān pāṃsūn nivapati
4.11.11	apahato 'raruḥ pṛthivyā ity āgnīdhro nyuptaṃ sthaṇḍile nikṣipyābhigṛhṇāti
4.11.12	sa utkaro bhavati
4.11.13	evaṃ dvitīyam
4.11.14	idam āpaḥ śivā iti dvitīyaṃ prahṛtyāpahato 'raruḥ pṛthivyai devayajanyā ity ādāyāpahatā yātudhānā ity ābhigṛhṇāti dvitīyam
4.12.1	drapsas te divaṃ mā skān iti tṛtīyaṃ prahṛtyāpahato 'raruḥ pṛthivyā adevayajana ity ādāyāpahato 'ghaśaṃsa ity abhigṛhṇāti
4.12.2	tūṣṇīṃ caturthaṃ sarvaṃ tṛṇaṃ haraty ararus te divaṃ mā skān iti caturtham abhigṛhṇāti
4.12.3	vedeḥ pūrvaṃ parigrāhaṃ parigṛhṇāti vasavas tveti sphyena dakṣiṇataḥ prācīṃ likhati
4.12.4	yajñasya tveti parigṛhyamāṇāṃ yajamāno 'numantrayate
4.12.5	rudrās tvety adhvaryuḥ paścād udīcīṃ lekhāṃ likhaty ādityās tvety uttarataḥ prācīṃ
4.12.6	te 'gninā prāñco 'jayann ity uktam
4.12.7	prāñcau vedyaṃsāv unnayaty abhita āhavanīyaṃ pratīcī śroṇī abhito gārhapatyaṃ madhye saṃnatā vedir vediḥ
5.1.1	imāṃ narāḥ kṛṇuteti saṃpreṣya devasya savituḥ sava iti vedeḥ sphyenottamāṃ tvacam uddhanti
5.1.2	yad udghnanta iti yajamāna uddhanyamānām anumantrayate
5.1.3	dvyaṅgulāṃ caturaṅgulāṃ rathavartmamātrīṃ prādeśamātrīṃ vaitā iyatīr nātikhanet
5.1.4	pitṛdevatyātikhātety uktam
5.1.5	dakṣiṇato varṣīyasīṃ purīṣavatīṃ prācīnapravaṇām udīcīnapravaṇāṃ prāgudakpravaṇāṃ vā vediṃ karoti
5.1.6	yan mūlam atiriktaṃ sphyena tac chinatti na nakhena
5.1.7	yat purīṣam atiriktam utkaraṃ tad gamayati
5.1.8	āhāryapurīṣāṃ paśukāmasya vediṃ karoti
5.1.9	yat prāk khananāt tat kṛtvā yad āharet tan mantreṇa khanet
5.1.10	bhūmir bhūtveti yajamānaḥ kṛtāṃ vedim anumantrayate
5.1.11	adhvaryur brahmann uttaraṃ parigrāhaṃ parigrahīṣyāmīty āmantrya bṛhaspate parigṛhāṇa vedim iti tena prasūta ṛtam asīti tribhiḥ pūrvavad vediṃ parigṛhṇāti
5.2.1	viparītau parigrāhāv eke
5.2.2	dhā asīti vediṃ sphyena pratīcīṃ yoyupyeta
5.2.3	purā krūrasyety abhimantrya paścārdhe vedeḥ pūrveṇa vitṛtīyadeśe sphyaṃ tiryañcaṃ stabdhvā prokṣaṇīr āsādayety āgnīdhraṃ saṃpreṣyati
5.2.4	āgnīdhro havanyāṃ tiraḥ pavitram apa ānīyodañcaṃ sphyam apakṛṣyāntarvedi havanīṃ dhārayan sphyasya vartmany upaninīyartasadhaḥ stheti sphyapade sādayati
5.2.5	yaṃ dviṣyāt taṃ dhyāyet
5.2.6	śatabhṛṣṭir asīty utkare sphyam udasyati
5.2.7	yaṃ dviṣyāt taṃ dhyāyet
5.2.8	īḍenyakratūr iti yajamānaḥ prokṣaṇīr āsādyamānā anumantrayate
5.2.9	āgnīdhro hastāv avanenekti
5.2.10	nānavanijya pātrāṇi saṃmṛśati na ca vedim ā staraṇāt sphyaṃ prakṣālayati nāgraṃ parimṛśati
5.2.11	āhavanīyam uttareṇa praṇītā idhmābarhir upasādayati prāgagraṃ dakṣiṇam idhmam uttaraṃ barhiḥ
5.2.12	vedāgraiḥ sruvaṃ srucaś ca saha saṃmārṣṭi
5.2.13	aniśitāḥ stha sapatnakṣayaṇīr ity abhimantrya ghṛtācīreteti dakṣiṇena pāṇinā sruvaṃ juhūpabhṛtau savyena dhruvāṃ prāśitraharaṇaṃ vedāgrāṇi cādāya pratyuṣṭam iti gārhapatye niṣṭapya goṣṭhaṃ mā nirmṛkṣam iti sruvam agrair antarato 'bhyākāraṃ sarvato bilam abhisamāhāraṃ nirlepaṃ trir abhitaḥ saṃmārṣṭi bāhyato mūlair daṇḍam
5.2.14	vācaṃ prāṇam iti juhūṃ cakṣuḥ śrotram ity upabhṛtaṃ prajāṃ yonim iti dhruvāṃ tūṣṇīṃ prāśitraharaṇam
5.2.15	pūrvavat srucaḥ prāśitraharaṇaṃ ca niṣṭapyottarato vediśroṇyāṃ nidadhāti
5.3.1	divaḥ śilpam iti prokṣitāni sruksaṃmārjanāny agnau praharati
5.3.2	apareṇa gārhapatyaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ patnīm udaṅmukhīm upaveśyāśāsānā saumanasam iti mauñjena yoktreṇānyatarataḥ pāśenordhvajñum āsīnāṃ prāṅmukhīṃ tiṣṭhantīṃ vā saṃnahyet
5.3.3	pūṣā te granthiṃ grathnātv ity uttarato nābher niṣṭarkyaṃ granthiṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇato nābheḥ parikarṣati
5.3.4	patny ācamyāgne gṛhapata iti tiṣṭhantī gārhapatyam upasthāya devānāṃ patnīr iti devapatnīś cendrāṇīvety udaṅmukhy anvāste
5.3.5	suprajas tvā vayam iti japati mama putrā iti ca
5.3.6	pūṣā te bilaṃ viṣyatv ity āgnīdhraḥ sarpirdhānasya bilam apāvṛtyedaṃ viṣṇur vicakrama ity anvāhāryapacane 'dhiśrityāditir asy acchidrapatrety ājyasthālīm ādāya mahīnāṃ paya iti tasyāṃ pavitravatyāṃ prabhūtam ājyaṃ nirvapati
5.3.7	iṣe tveti dakṣiṇārdhe gārhapatyasyādhiśrityorje tvety apādāya vedenopayamya mahīnāṃ payo 'sīti patnīṃ pradarśayati
5.3.8	tat sā nimīlya vīkṣyānucchūsanty avekṣate
5.3.9	tejo 'sīty uttarārdhe 'dhiśritya tejase tvety apādāya tejo 'nuprehīty āhavanīyam abhyuddrutyāgnis te tejo mā vinaid ity āhavanīye 'dhiśrityāgner juhvāsīty uttareṇa prokṣaṇīḥ sphyasya vartman sādayati
5.3.10	īḍenyakratūr iti yajamāna āsādyamānā anumantrayate
5.4.1	yadi sāṃnāyyasyājyasya vānyatra barhiṣaḥ purottamāt prayājāt skandet saṃ tvā siñcāmīti tasya svayaṃ saṃbhṛtya bhūpataye svāheti tribhiḥ skannam anumantrayate
5.4.2	adhvaryuyajamānāv ājyam asīti nimīlya vīkṣyānucchūsantāv ājyam avekṣete
5.4.3	śukram asīti tribhir udagagrābhyāṃ pavitrābhyām adhvaryuḥ punarāhāram ājyaṃ trir utpunāti
5.4.4	devo va iti triḥ prokṣaṇīr adbhir ājyam iti yajamāna ājyam apaś cotpūyamānā anumantrayate
5.4.5	adhvaryur antarvedi samaṃbilaṃ juhūṃ dhārayamāṇa ājyasthālyā vedenopayamya sruveṇa śukraṃ tvā śukrāyām iti catuḥ pañcakṛtvo vā juhvāṃ prabhūtam ājyaṃ gṛhṇāti
5.4.6	pañcānāṃ tvā vātānām iti catuḥ pañcakṛtvo vā yajamāno japati
5.4.7	adhvaryur jyotis tvā jyotiṣi dhāmne dhāmna iti madhyadeśe dhārayamāṇa upabhṛty aṣṭau daśakṛtvo vālpiṣṭhaṃ gṛhṇāti
5.4.8	pañcānāṃ tvartūṇām iti trīn yajamāno japati pañcānāṃ tvā salilānāṃ pañcānāṃ tvā pṛṣṭhānām iti ca dvau caros tvā pañcabilasyeti pañca
5.4.9	adhvaryur arcis tvārciṣīti catuḥ pañcakṛtvo vā bhūmau pratiṣṭhitāyāṃ dhruvāyāṃ bhūyiṣṭhaṃ gṛhṇāti
5.4.10	suprajāstvāya tvā gṛhṇāmīti catuḥ pañca vā yajamāno japati
5.5.1	bahirvedy anyatrotkarād ājyāni sādayaty ājyasthalīṃ ca praticīnaṃ harati
5.5.2	tathā prokṣaṇīr abhimantrya brahmāṇam āmantrya tena prasūto muktagranthīn idhmān kṛṣṇo 'sīti triḥ prokṣati tathā vedir asīti vediṃ barhir asīti barhiḥ
5.5.3	antarvedi purogranthi tad āsādayati
5.5.4	sumanaso yajamānāya santv iti yajamāno barhir abhimantrayate
5.5.5	adhvaryur dive tveti barhiragraṃ prokṣaty antarikṣāya tveti madhyaṃ pṛthivyai tveti mūlam
5.5.6	yajamāno 'śiśrema barhir iti prokṣyamāṇaṃ barhir abhimantrayate
5.5.7	adhvaryur barhiragrāṇi havanyāṃ prasicya mūlāni prasecayati
5.5.8	poṣāya tveti saha havanyā purastāt pratyañcaṃ granthiṃ pratyukṣati
5.5.9	svadhā pitṛbhya iti veder dakṣiṇāyāḥ śroṇeḥ saṃtatam ottarasyā apāṃ śeṣaṃ ninayati
5.5.10	pūṣā te granthiṃ viṣyatv iti barhiṣo granthiṃ viṣyati
5.5.11	viṣṇoḥ stūpo 'sīti karṣann ivāhavanīyaṃ prati prastaram ādatte
5.5.12	yajamāne prāṇāpānau dadhāmīti prastare pavitre apisṛjya prāṇāpānābhyāṃ tvā satanuṃ karomīti brahmaṇe prayacchati
5.6.1	brahmā yajamānāya
5.6.2	tṛṇair antardhāyākṣṇayā śulbaṃ ca nidhāyorṇāmradasaṃ tvā stṛṇāmīti bahulam anatidṛśnaṃ prāgapavargaṃ pratyagapavargaṃ vā barhiṣā vediṃ stṛṇāti
5.6.3	ūrṇāmṛdu prathamānaṃ catuḥśikhaṇḍeti dvābhyāṃ stīryamāṇāṃ yajamāno 'numantrayate
5.6.4	adhvaryur agrair mūlāny abhicchādayan tridhātu pāñcadhātu vā kṛtvā dhātau dhātau mantram āvartayati
5.6.5	śivā ca ma iti stīrṇāṃ vediṃ yajamāno 'numantrayate
5.6.6	adhvaryur anūyājārthe prāñcāv aṅgārau nirūhyāhavanīyaṃ kalpayitvā prastaraṃ dhārayan gandharvo 'sīty udagagraṃ madhyamaṃ paridhiṃ paridadhāti
5.6.7	asmin yajña upa bhūya iti dhruvo 'si dhruvo 'ham iti dvābhyāṃ yajamāno madhyamaṃ paridhim anumantrayate
5.6.8	adhvaryur indrasya bāhur asīti mitrāvaruṇau tveti dakṣiṇottarau prāgagrau saṃspṛṣṭau madhyamena dakṣiṇam āhavanīyam abhyagram uttaram avāgram
5.6.9	asmin yajña ugro 'sy asmin yajñe 'bhibhūr asīti yajamāno 'numantrayate yathā madhyamam
5.6.10	adhvaryuḥ sūryas tvā purastāt pātv iti sūryeṇa purastāt paridadhāti
5.6.11	yunajmi tvā yan me agna iti dvābhyāṃ yajamāno 'gniṃ yunakti
5.7.1	vītihotram iti dakṣiṇām ūrdhvām ādhārasamidham ādadhāti samidasyāyuṣe tvety uttarāṃ tūṣṇīṃ vā
5.7.2	tejiṣṭhā ta iti parihitam agniṃ yajamāno 'numantrayate
5.7.3	adhvaryur viśo yantre stha iti samāv anantargarbhau darbhau vidhṛtī udagagre nidadhāti
5.7.4	vicchinadmi viśo yantre nudamāne iti dvābhyāṃ yajamāno 'bhimantrayate
5.7.5	vasūnāṃ rudrāṇām ity adhvaryus tayoḥ prastaraṃ sādayati
5.7.6	ayaṃ prastara iti sādyamānaṃ yajamānaḥ
5.7.7	juhūr asīty adhvaryuḥ prastare juhūṃ sādayati
5.7.8	āroha patho juhūr asi ghṛtācī gāyatriyāmnīti dvābhyāṃ sādyamānāṃ juhūṃ yajamānaḥ
5.7.9	upabhṛd asi ghṛtācīty adhvaryur upabhṛtam adhastād vidhṛtyoḥ pratikṛṣṭatarām iva sādayati
5.7.10	upariṣṭāt prastara ity eke
5.7.11	avāhaṃ bādhe subhṛd asy upabhṛd iti dvābhyāṃ sādyamānāṃ yajamānaḥ
5.7.12	dhruvāsi ghṛtācīty adhvaryur dhruvāṃ sādayati
5.7.13	yo mā vācā manasā dhruvāsi dharaṇī dhanasyeti dvābhyāṃ sādyamānāṃ yajamānaḥ
5.7.14	ṛṣabho 'si śākvara ity adhvaryuḥ sruvaṃ sādayati
5.8.1	syono me sīdāyaṃ sruva iti dvābhyāṃ sruvaṃ yajamānaḥ
5.8.2	iyaṃ sthālīty adhvaryur ājyasthālīṃ sādayati
5.8.3	tayaiva yajamānaḥ
5.8.4	etā asadann ity adhvaryuḥ sannāḥ sruco 'bhimantrayate viṣṇūni sthety ājyāni ca
5.8.5	atha sasruvām ājyasthālīm ādāya savyena vedam apareṇa gārhapatyam upaviśya kapālavad vedena dakṣiṇasmāt puroḍāśād aṅgārān apohyottarasmād apohati
5.8.6	sūrya jyotir iti puroḍāśam abhimantryāpyāyatāṃ ghṛtayonir ity āgneyaṃ puroḍāśam abhighārayati tūṣṇīm uttaraṃ yas ta ātmeti śṛtam
5.8.7	syonaṃ te sadanaṃ karomīti pātryām upastīryārdraḥ prathasnur iti puroḍāśam abhindann aparyāvartayann udvāsayati
5.8.8	vedena bhasma pramṛjya tasmin sīdeti pātryām upastīrṇe puroḍāśaṃ nidadhāti
5.8.9	tūṣṇīṃ yavamayaṃ puroḍāśam
5.8.10	irā bhūtiḥ pṛthivyai raso motkramīd iti kapālāny ekaikaśo 'bhighāryaikaṃ dve trīṇīty ādibhiḥ saṃkhyāyodvāsayati śṛtaṃ ca dadhi ca
5.8.11	devas tvā savitā madhvānaktv iti sruveṇa puroḍāśaṃ sarvato 'nakti
5.8.12	sruveṇa hasta ājyam avadāya puroḍāśam adhastād abhyajyālaṃkaroty ājyena śṛtaṃ ca dadhi ca
5.9.1	ājyena sruvaṃ pūrayitvāntareṇa puroḍāśāv āsādya sarvāṇi havīṃṣi pātryāṃ saṃgṛhya bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar iti vyāhṛtībhir havīṃṣy apareṇa sruco 'ntarvedyāsādayet prathamataḥ
5.9.2	athā saṃvatsare
5.9.3	itarakāleṣu caturhotrā paurṇamāsyāṃ pañcahotrāmāvāsyāyāṃ priyeṇa nāmnā priyaṃ sada āsīdety etebhyo 'nyaddhaviḥ
5.9.4	apareṇa srucaḥ puroḍāśau dakṣiṇasyāṃ śroṇyāṃ śṛtam uttarasyāṃ dadhi
5.9.5	ayaṃ veda ity agreṇa dhruvāṃ vedaṃ nidhāya vedyantān paristīrya paribhojanīyān darbhān ādāya hotṛṣadanaṃ kalpayati
5.9.6	yajño 'sīty āgneyam āsannaṃ yajamāno 'bhimṛśati prajāpatir asīty agnīṣomīyam idam indriyam amṛtam iti prātardohaṃ yat pṛthivīm acarad iti dadhi yo naḥ kanīya ity aindrāgnam ayaṃ yajña iti sarvāṇi mamāgna iti vihavyena ca paurṇamāsyām abhimṛśati caturhotrā pañcahotrāmāvāsyāyām
5.9.7	hotar ehīty adhvaryur hotāram āmantryāgnaye samidhyamānāyānubrūhīty saṃpreṣyati saṃpreṣyati
6.1.1	athāsīno 'dhvaryur idhmād ekaikāṃ samidham ādāya praṇave praṇave prati sāmidhenyādadhāti yāvat pañcadaśa
6.1.2	anūyājebhya ekāṃ samidham avaśinaṣṭi
6.1.3	purastād upariṣṭād vā sāmidhenīnāṃ yajamāno daśahotāraṃ vyācakṣīta
6.1.4	āṅgiraso māsya yajñasyeti madhya ucchuṣmo agna iti samidhyamānam agnim anumantrayate samiddho agnir āhuta iti samiddham
6.1.5	ājuhotety ucyamāne 'dhvaryur idhmaśeṣaṃ prakṣipya vedenāhavanīyaṃ trir upavājyānūktāsu sāmidhenīṣu sruveṇa dhruvāyā ājyam ādāya vedenopayamyottaraṃ paridhisandhiṃ spṛṣṭvā prajāpataye svāheti manasā saṃtatam ṛjuṃ jyotiṣi prājāpatyam āghāram āghārayati
6.2.1	mano 'si prājāpatyam iti sruvāghāraṃ yajamāno 'numantrayate
6.2.2	āpyāyatāṃ dhruvā ghṛtenety adhvaryuḥ sruveṇājyasthālyā ājyam ādāya dhruvām āpyāyayati
6.2.3	sarvatraivam
6.2.4	agnīn paridhīṃś cāgniṃ ca tris triḥ saṃmṛḍḍhīti saṃpreṣyati
6.2.5	idhmasaṃnahanāni sphya upasaṃgṛhyāgnīdhraḥ pradakṣiṇam anuparikrāman paridhīn saṃmārṣṭi madhyamam udañcaṃ prāñcāv itarau
6.2.6	agne vājajid ity agniṃ triḥ saṃmārṣṭi
6.2.7	sarveṣu homeṣūpabhṛtā juhūm upayacchaty asaṃśabdayan mukhato 'bhininīyopabhṛti juhūm avadhāya
6.2.8	hoṣyaṃs tenaiva pratininīya nābhiṃ prati srucau dhārayate
6.2.9	samaṃ prāṇair ity eke
6.3.1	sruvāghāram āghārayiṣyan bhuvanam asīti juhūpabhṛtāv agreṇa devebhyaḥ prācīnam añjaliṃ karoti svadhā pitṛbhya iti pitṛbhyo dakṣiṇam
6.3.2	apareṇāhavanīyaṃ dakṣiṇena padā dakṣiṇātikrāmati savyenodaṅ
6.3.3	juhv ehīti juhūm ādatta upabhṛd ehīty upabhṛtam
6.3.4	suyame me adyety upabhṛti juhūm avadhāyāgnāviṣṇū ity anavakrāman prastaraṃ dakṣiṇātikramya viṣṇoḥ sthānam asīty avasthāyāntarvedi dakṣiṇaṃ pādaṃ tat spṛṣṭaprapadaṃ savyaṃ kṛtvordhvas tiṣṭhann anvārabdhe yajamāne dakṣiṇaṃ paridhisaṃdhiṃ spṛṣṭveśānāntaṃ samārabhyordhva iti pūrvavad aindram āghārayati
6.3.5	hutvābhiprāṇiti
6.3.6	bṛhad bhā iti srucam udgṛhṇāti
6.3.7	vāg asy aindrīti yajamāno 'numantrayate
6.3.8	adhvaryuḥ srucāv asaṃsparśayan pāhi māgna ity udaṅmukhaḥ pratyākrāmati
6.3.9	ete evākramaṇapratyākramaṇe mantravatī
6.3.10	makhasya śiro 'sīti juhvā dhruvāṃ triḥ samanakti
6.4.1	sruveṇa dhruvāyā unnītaṃ rāya ity ājyam ādāya suvīrāya svāheti juhūṃ pratyabhighārayati yajñena yajñaḥ saṃtata iti juhvā dvis trir vā dhruvām
6.4.2	yathāsthānaṃ srucau sādayati
6.4.3	sphyopasaṃnaddhānīdhmasaṃnahanāni vedeś ca tṛṇam avyantam ādāyottarato 'dhvaryuḥ pravarāyāvasthāya ka idam adhvaryur bhaviṣyatīti japati
6.4.4	tāny anvārabhyādhvaryoḥ paścād avasthāyāgnīdhraḥ ka idam agnīd iti
6.4.5	adhvaryur brahman pravarāyāśrāvayiṣyāmīty āmantrya vācaspate vācam āśrāvayeti tena prasūta āśrāvayo śrāvaya śrāvayeti vāśrāvayati
6.4.6	astu śrauṣaḍ ity agnīd utkare dakṣiṇāmukhas tiṣṭhan sphyaṃ dhārayan pratyāśrāvayati
6.4.7	sarvatraivam āśrutapratyāśrute bhavataḥ
6.4.8	ūrdhvajñum āsīnaṃ hotāram adhvaryur agnir devo hoteti vṛṇīte 'muvad amuvad iti yathā yajamānasyārṣeyaṃ saha pravareṇa trīn anantarān iti
6.4.9	ūrdhvān mantrakṛto 'dhvaryur vṛṇīte 'muto 'rvāco hoteti vijñāyate
6.4.10	api vaikaṃ dvau trīn pañca
6.4.11	na caturo vṛṇīte na pañcātipravṛṇīte
6.5.1	purohitasya pravareṇa pravṛṇīte
6.5.2	anājñātabandhor ācāryapravareṇāpi vā manuvad iti pravṛṇīte
6.5.3	dvigotrasya trīṃs trīn ekaikasmād gotrād upalakṣayet
6.5.4	brahmaṇvad ā ca vakṣad iti pravaraśeṣaḥ
6.5.5	asāv iti hotur upāṃśu nāma gṛhṇāti mānuṣa ity uccaiḥ
6.5.6	āste hotā
6.5.7	vedyāṃ tṛṇam apisṛjati
6.5.8	devāḥ pitara iti hotradhvaryupravarayor yajamāno japati māṃ deveṣv āśrāvayāyuṣe varcasa iti cādhvaryupravaraḥ
6.5.9	ājyabhāgapradhānasviṣṭakṛtpatnīsaṃyājeṣu yājyāpuronuvākye yājyaiva prayājānūyājeṣu sarveṣv eteṣv āśrutapratyāśrute yājyāsaṃpraiṣaś ca
6.5.10	ye prastutās te svakarmaṇo 'nyatra tad anapavyāharantaḥ pracareyuḥ
6.6.1	avadyann avatte 'vadāsyan vottarato 'muṣmā anubrūhīti yathādevataṃ puronuvākyāṃ saṃpreṣyati
6.6.2	ākramya dakṣiṇata āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite 'muṃ yajeti yathādevataṃ yājyāṃ saṃpreṣyati
6.6.3	vaṣaṭkṛte vaṣaṭkriyamāṇe vā juhoti caturavattaṃ pañcāvattaṃ vā
6.6.4	pañcāvattaṃ jamadagnīnāṃ caturavattam itareṣām
6.6.5	aṅguṣṭhaparvamātrāṇi daivatāny avadānāni tebhyaḥ sthavīyāṃsi sauviṣṭakṛtāni tathaivaiḍāni tathā cāturdhākaraṇikāni
6.6.6	ghṛtavatīm adhvaryo srucam iti yatra hotur abhijānāti juhūpabhṛtāv ādāya sakṛd dakṣiṇātikrāntaḥ pañca prayājān prācaḥ pratidiśaṃ vā yajati
6.7.1	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite samidho yajeti prathamaṃ prayājaṃ saṃpreṣyati yaja yajety uttarān
6.7.2	yajamānaś caturhotāraṃ vyākhyāya vasantam ṛtūṇāṃ prīṇāmīty etaiḥ prayājānāṃ hutaṃ hutam anumantrayate
6.7.3	adhvaryuḥ samidhaḥ purastāj juhuyāt tanūnapātaṃ dakṣiṇata iḍaḥ paścāt
6.7.4	ardham aupabhṛtam ājyaṃ juhvām ānīya barhir uttarato madhye svāhākāram
6.7.5	udaṅṅ atyākramya prayājaśeṣeṇa havīṃṣy abhighārayati yad anupūrvāṇi pradīyante
6.7.6	dhruvām abhighāryāgneyam abhighārayaty upabhṛtam antataḥ
6.7.7	ājyabhāgāv ājyahaviṣkau prabāhug jyotiṣy uttarārdhe 'gnaye dakṣiṇārdhe somāya
6.7.8	tāv antareṇetarā āhutīr juhoti
6.8.1	agnīṣomayor iti yajamānas tāv anumantrayate
6.8.2	adhvaryuḥ pratyākramya juhvām upastīrya mā bher mā saṃvikthā ity avadāsyan puroḍāśam abhimṛśati
6.8.3	pañcahotāraṃ yajamāno vyācakṣīta
6.8.4	adhvaryur māṃsasaṃhitābhyāṃ dakṣiṇānāmikāmadhyamābhyām aṅguṣṭhena cāṅguṣṭhaparvamātraṃ madhyāt puroḍāśasya tiraścīnam avadyati
6.8.5	pūrvārdhād dvitīyaṃ caturavattino 'nūcīnaṃ
6.8.6	tadvat paścārdhāt pañcāvattinas tṛtīyam
6.8.7	avadānāny abhighārya dhruvām āpyāyya yad avadānānīti haviḥ pratyabhighāryāgnaye 'nubrūhīti dakṣiṇātikramya vaṣaṭkāra ājyaṃ hutvā sruveṇa prastarabarhiḥ samajyāpidadhad ivāprakṣiṇan puroḍāśāvadānaṃ juhoti
6.8.8	ājyenāntato 'nvavasrāvayati
6.8.9	mukhena puroḍāśād itarā āhutīḥ srāvayati
6.8.10	pūrvāṃ pūrvāṃ saṃhitām āhutiṃ juhoti
6.8.11	srucyam āghāram abhijuhoti
6.8.12	agner aham iti hutam āgneyaṃ yajamāno 'numantrayate
6.9.1	ājyahaviṣkeṇopāṃśuyājena yajate
6.9.2	tasyoccair āśrutapratyāśrute yājyāpuronuvākyā saṃpraiṣau praṇava āgūr vaṣaṭkāraś cāto 'nyad upāṃśu
6.9.3	ājyasāṃnāyyayoḥ sruveṇāvadyati mekṣaṇena carūṇām
6.9.4	dabdhir asīty upāṃśuyājasya hutaṃ yajamānaḥ
6.9.5	yathādevatam uttareṇa puroḍāśenādhvaryuḥ pracarati
6.9.6	agnīṣomayor ahaṃ devayajyayā vṛtrahā bhūyāsam ity agnīṣomīyasya hutaṃ yajamāna indrāgnyor ahaṃ devayajyayendriyāvy annādo bhūyāsam ity aindrāgnasya hutam anumantrayate
6.9.7	adhvaryuḥ samavadāya sāṃnāyyābhyāṃ pracarati
6.9.8	dviḥ śṛtasyāvadyati dvir dadhnas tris triḥ pañcāvattinaḥ
6.9.9	indrasyāham ity aindrasya sāṃnāyyasya hutaṃ yajamāno 'numantrayate mahendrasyāham iti māhendrasyendrasya vaimṛdhasyeti vaimṛdhasya hutam
6.9.10	adhvaryur ṛṣabhaṃ vājinaṃ vayam amāvāsyā subhageti yathāliṅgaṃ vibhajya sruveṇa pārvaṇau homau juhoti
6.10.1	daśa te tanuvo yajñeti ṣaḍbhiḥ pratimantraṃ nāriṣṭhahomāñ juhoti
6.10.2	purastāt samiṣṭayajuṣa ity eke
6.10.3	juhvām upastīrya sarvebhyo havirbhya uttarārdhāt sakṛt sakṛt sviṣṭakṛte 'vadyati dviḥ pañcāvattino yad anupūrvāṇi pradīyante
6.10.4	dvir abhighārayati haviḥśeṣān
6.10.5	na pratyabhighārayati
6.10.6	asaṃsṛṣṭām itarābhir āhutibhir uttarārdhapūrvārdhe jyotiṣi juhoti
6.10.7	agneḥ sviṣṭakṛto 'ham iti yajamānaḥ sviṣṭakṛto hutam anumantrayate 'gnir mā duriṣṭāt pātv iti ca
6.10.8	adhvaryur udaṅṅ atyākramya juhvām apa ānīya vaiśvānare havir idaṃ juhomīti madhyamaṃ paridhiṃ pradakṣiṇam anupariṣiñcati
6.10.9	antaḥparidhi ninayatīty eke
6.10.10	srucau nidhāya sruveṇa tiryañcaṃ prāñcaṃ vāgneyaṃ virujyāṅguṣṭhenānāmikayā ca vyūhya madhyāt pippalamātraṃ yavamātraṃ vā jyāyo yavamātrād iti prāśitraṃ prāśitraharaṇe 'vadyati
6.10.11	evam avirujyottarasmāt puroḍāśād avadāyābhighārayati
6.10.12	āgneyād evāvadyatīty eke
6.10.13	mitrasya tveti brahmāvadīyamānaṃ prekṣate
6.11.1	tad apareṇa praṇītā nidhāyeḍāpātra upastīrya manunā dṛṣṭām iti caturavattāṃ pañcāvattāṃ vā sarvebhyo havirbhyaḥ sviṣṭakṛdvat prabhūtām iḍāṃ samavadyati dakṣiṇārdhāt puroḍāśasya pūrvam avadāya saṃbhedād dvitīyam
6.11.2	pūrvārdhād yajamānabhāgam aṇum iva dīrgham
6.11.3	ājyena tam abhyajya dhruvāyā agreṇa nidhāyābhighārayati
6.11.4	paścārdhāt tṛtīyaṃ pañcāvattinaḥ
6.11.5	evaṃ sarvasya haviṣaḥ
6.11.6	yo me 'nti dūra iti yajamānabhāge 'vadīyamāne yajamāno japati
6.11.7	iḍāṃ sakṛd abhighārya hotre 'dhvaryur āharati
6.11.8	surūpavarṣavarṇa ehīti yajamāna iḍām āhriyamāṇāṃ pratīkṣate
6.11.9	adhvaryur dakṣiṇena hotāram atikrāmaty anutsṛjan
6.11.10	hotādhvaryum iḍayā parigṛhṇāti
6.11.11	paścāt prāṅ āsīnaḥ sruveṇa hotur dviḥ pradeśinyaṅgulāv anakti parvaṇoḥ
6.11.12	sa tad avaghrāyāpa upaspṛśati
6.12.1	yathetaṃ pratyetya pratyag agreṇāsīno dakṣiṇe hotuḥ pāṇāv iḍāyā avāntareḍām avadyati
6.12.2	iḍālepād upastīrya prathamam adhvaryur avadyaty aṅguṣṭhaprabhṛtāṅgulīr antareṇa savyaṃ hotā dvitīyaṃ gṛhṇāti lepena cādhvaryur abhighārayati
6.12.3	dviḥ pañcāvattinaḥ
6.12.4	aṅguṣṭhenopasaṃkucyāmuṣṭiṃ kṛtvā mukhasaṃmitam iḍāpātraṃ dhārayamāṇam iḍopahutā saha divetīḍām upahūyamānaṃ hotāram adhvaryur agnīd yajamānaś cānvārabhante
6.12.5	iḍa ehy adita ehīty upāṃśūpahave yajamānaḥ sapta devagavīr japati
6.12.6	cid asi manāsīty uccair upahave sapta manuṣyagavīḥ
6.12.7	viśvā tvaṃ bhūtvetīḍām upahūyamānām anumantrayate
6.12.8	vāyav iḍā te māteti hotāram īkṣamāṇo vāyuṃ manasā dhyāyet
6.12.9	daivyā adhvaryur upahūto 'yaṃ yajamāna ity ucyamāne 'dhvaryuyajamānāv upahūtaḥ paśumān asānīti krameṇa japataḥ sā me satyāśīr ity āśiḥṣu yajamāna iḍāyā ahaṃ devayajyayety upahūtām iḍāṃ bhakṣāyāhriyamāṇām abhimantrayate
6.12.10	upahūtāyām iḍāyām agreṇāhavanīyam adhvaryur brahmaṇe prāśitraṃ pariharati pariharati
7.1.1	ṛtasya pathā paryehīti brahmā parihriyamāṇam abhimantrya sūryasya tvā cakṣuṣety āhriyamāṇaṃ pratīkṣya devasya tveti pratigṛhya pṛthivyās tvā nābhāv iti pṛthivyām āsādya suparṇasya tvā garutmata ity avekṣyāṅguṣṭhenānāmikayā copasaṃgṛhyātihāya dato 'gnes tvāsyena prāśnāmīti jihvāgre nidhāyāpaś ca brāhmaṇasyodareṇa bṛhaspater brahmaṇendrasya tvā jaṭhare sādayāmīti sahādbhir asaṃmletyābhigirati
7.1.2	yā apsv antar devatā ity apaḥ prāśyācamya ghasīnā me meti nābhim abhimṛśya vāṅ ma āsann iti yathāliṅgam indriyāṇi saṃmṛśyāriṣṭā viśvānīti sarvāṇy aṅgāni mayi prāṇāpānāv iti vā prāśitraharaṇaṃ prakṣālya pūrayitvā diśo jinveti parāñcaṃ ninayati
7.1.3	punar adbhiḥ pūrayitvā māṃ jinvety abhyātmaṃ ninayati
7.1.4	tasmin prāśite vācaspataye tvā hutaṃ prāśnāmi sadasaspataye tvā hutaṃ prāśnāmīti hotāvāntareḍāṃ prāśnāti
7.1.5	juṣṭir asīti prāśyamānāṃ yajamāno 'numantrayate

7.3.1	anyenādhvaryave

7.3.3	dakṣiṇāgnau pakvaṃ mahāntam aparimitam anvāhāryam odanam abhighāryodag udvāsyāntarvedy āsādayati

7.3.5	dakṣiṇasadbhya upahartavā ity adhvaryuḥ saṃpreṣyati dakṣiṇata eteti yajamānaḥ
7.3.6	brāhmaṇā ayaṃ va odana iti dakṣiṇatas tebhyo 'nvāhāryaṃ caturdhā vibhajya dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti

7.4.1	sphyād unmucyedhmasaṃnahanair anuparikrāmann āgnīdhraḥ pūrvavat paridhīn agniṃ ca sakṛt sakṛt saṃmārṣṭi

7.5.1	udaṅṅ atyākramyādhvaryur yathāyatanaṃ srucau sādayitvā vājasya mā prasavenety anuṣṭugbhyāṃ vājavatībhyāṃ vyūhati
7.5.2	vājasya mā prasaveneti dakṣiṇenottānena pāṇinā saprastarāṃ juhūm udgṛhṇāti
