8.2.8	tvam agne saprathā asi soma yās te mayobhuva iti sadvantāv ājyabhāgāv āpyāyasva saṃ ta iti haviṣaḥ preddho agna imo agna iti saṃyājye
8.2.9	yathartu veṇupriyaṅgunīvāraiḥ śyāmākavad yajeta
8.2.10	yat prāk prokṣaṇāt tat kṛtvā śatāyudhāyeti pañcājyānīr juhoti purastāt sviṣṭakṛto vā
8.2.11	agniḥ prathamaḥ prāśnātv iti śyāmākasya yajamānabhāgaṃ prāśnāti
8.2.12	bhadrānnaḥ śreya iti vrīhīṇām etam u tyaṃ madhuneti yavānām
8.2.13	api vā paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāyāṃ vāgrayaṇeṣṭim anvāyātayet
8.2.14	api vā navair eva paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāyāṃ vā yajeta navair vāgnihotraṃ juhuyāt
8.2.15	sarvāsām oṣadhīnāṃ grāmyāṇām āraṇyānāṃ vaupāsane gārhapatye vā sthālīpākaṃ śrapayitvāgrayaṇadevatābhyaḥ sviṣṭakṛccaturthībhyo juhuyāc caturo vā brāhmaṇān bhojayet
8.2.16	aniṣṭe apy āgrayaṇe brahmaṇi hutaṃ bhavati
8.3.1	atha cāturmāsyāni
8.3.2	akṣayyaṃ ha vai sukṛtaṃ cāturmāsyair bhavati
8.3.3	tāni yakṣyamāṇo vasante prācīnapravaṇe vaiśvadevena yajate
8.3.4	phālgunyāṃ caitryāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vodagayana āpūryamāṇapakṣasya puṇyāhe vā prayuñjīta
8.3.5	tasya pūrvedyur agnir hoteti manasānudrutenānuvākenāhavanīye hutvārambhaṇīyām iṣṭiṃ kuryād vaiśvānaraṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ pārjanyaṃ caruṃ ca
8.3.6	vaiśvānaro na ūtyā pṛṣṭo divīti vaiśvānarasya yājyānuvākye parjanyāya pragāyatācchā vada tavasaṃ gīrbhir iti pārjanyasya
8.3.7	vaiśvānare hiraṇyaṃ dakṣiṇā dhenuḥ pārjanye
8.3.8	ato 'nyat siddheṣṭiḥ
8.3.9	cāturmāsyānāṃ yajñakratoḥ pañcartvijo 'dhikaḥ pratiprasthātā
8.3.10	yathāsyaitad ahar udavasāyānudavasāya vā vaiśvadevahavirbhir yakṣyamāṇo 'tra paśubandhavad gārhapatyād agniṃ praṇīya tadvad agnyāyatane 'gniṃ pratiṣṭhāpayatīty eke
8.3.11	agnīn anvādhāyāmikṣāyai vaiśvadevyai vatsān apākaroti
8.3.12	saptadaśa sāmidhenyaḥ
8.3.13	tredhā prasūmayaṃ barhiḥ saṃnaddham
8.3.14	tad ekadhā punaḥ saṃnahyati
8.3.15	evam idhmam
8.3.16	ubhayatra punaḥsaṃnahane mantraḥ
8.3.17	sāyaṃ hute 'gnihotre sāṃnāyyaṃ dohayati
8.3.18	dadhnātanakti
8.4.1	prātarhute 'gnihotre pāṇiprakṣālanādi karma pratipadyate
8.4.2	pātrasaṃsādanakāle dve upabhṛtau pṛṣadājyadhānī dvitīyā dve ājyasthālyau dadhidhānī dvitīyā pālāśaṃ vājinapātraṃ camasam
8.4.3	nirvapanakāla āgneyam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapati saumyaṃ caruṃ sāvitraṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ sārasvataṃ caruṃ pauṣṇaṃ carum ity etāni pañca saṃcarāṇi
8.4.4	mārutaṃ saptakapālaṃ vaiśvadevīm āmikṣāṃ dyāvāpṛthivyam ekakapālam
8.4.5	triṣphalīkṛteṣu yathābhāgamantreṇa saumyaṃ caruṃ sārasvataṃ caruṃ vibhajya piṣṭeṣu saṃyuteṣu tathā pauṣṇaṃ ca vibhajya kapālāny upadhāya caruṃ cādhiśritya prātardohavad dugdhvā tapte payasi sāyaṃdugdham ānayati
8.4.6	yā saṃhatā sāmikṣā
8.4.7	yad dravati tad vājinam anyasmin pātre niṣicya nidadhāti
8.5.1	kṛtvottaraṃ parigrāham ājyena dadhnā codehīti praiṣaṃ saṃnamati
8.5.2	ājyaṃ nirupya pṛṣadājyāya dadhi nirvapati
8.5.3	tasyājyadharmaḥ syāt
8.5.4	nādhiśrayati
8.5.5	ājyagrahaṇe juhūpabhṛtoś caturgṛhīte gṛhītvā niruptājyasya tṛtīyaṃ nirupte dadhy ānīya mahīnāṃ payo 'sīti dvitīyopabhṛti pañcagṛhītaṃ pṛṣadājyaṃ gṛhṇāti
8.5.6	havirudvāsaneṣu dvayoḥ pātrayor āmikṣām uddhṛtya vājinaikadeśenopasiñcati
8.5.7	ekakapālaṃ pātre 'nyasminn udvāsya tad ājyenābhipūrayitvāviḥpṛṣṭhaṃ kuryād ity eke
8.5.8	prathamaṃ cāturmāsyāny anvārabhamāṇasya vyāhṛtībhir havīṃṣy āsādayati tathā saṃvatsare
8.5.9	utkare vājinam āsādayati
8.5.10	agnir hoteti pañcahotrā yajamāno havīṃṣy āsannāny abhimṛśati vājinaṃ ca
8.5.11	nirmanthyaṃ kariṣyann agner janitram asīti śakalam ādāya barhiṣy apareṇāhavanīyaṃ nidhāya vṛṣaṇau stha iti prācīne barhiṣī śakale nidhāyorvaśy asīty adharāraṇim ādāya purūravā ity uttarāraṇiṃ ca ghṛtenākte ity ājyasthālyā bile 'ktvāyur asīti samavadadhāti
8.5.12	agnaye mathyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyābhi tvā deva savitar iti hotrā trir anūktāyāṃ gāyatraṃ chando 'nu prajāyasveti prajātibhis tribhis triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ mantham āvartya yathākāmaṃ manthati
8.5.13	jātāyānubrūhīti jāte saṃpreṣyati
8.6.1	prahriyamāṇāyānubrūhīti prahriyamāṇe
8.6.2	bhavataṃ naḥ samanasāv ity uttaraparidhisaṃdhinā nirmanthyam āhavanīye praharati
8.6.3	agnāv agnir iti pratyabhijuhoti
8.6.4	agnaye samidhyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
8.6.5	yathāprakṛti caturo dura uṣāsānaktā daivyā hotārā tisro devīr iti caturaḥ prakṛtivad uttama iti nava prayājā ijyante
8.6.6	caturthe 'rdhaṃ samānīyāṣṭame sarvaṃ samānayate
8.6.7	teṣv āditaś caturbhir anumantraṇaiś caturo yajamāno 'numantrayate duraḥprabhṛtīṃś caturaś caturthasyānumantraṇena pañcame navamam
8.6.8	sāvitraikakapālayor devatām upāṃśv adhvaryur yajati
8.6.9	akhaṇḍam ekakapālam avadāyarjuṃ pratiṣṭhitam aparyāvartayañ juhoti yathāyaṃ na dikṣu padyeta
8.6.10	yadi padyeta varaṃ dattvā srugagreṇa pratiṣṭhāpayet pratyādāya vā punaḥ sthāpayen na pāṇinety eke
8.6.11	madhuś ca mādhavaś ceti caturbhir māsanāmabhir ekakapālam abhijuhoti
8.6.12	prathamajo vatso dakṣiṇā mithunau vā gāvau
8.6.13	pṛṣadājyaṃ yad upabhṛti taj juhvām ānīya tām evopabhṛtyaitena navānūyājā ijyante
8.7.1	paśuvad aṣṭāv ādyān yajamāno 'numantrayata uttamenottamam
8.7.2	saṃvatsarīṇāṃ svastim āśāste divyaṃ dhāmāśāsta iti hotā sūktavākasyāśiḥṣv anuvartayati
8.7.3	prahṛtya paridhīn saṃsrāveṇābhihutya vājinapātra upastīrya barhiṣi viṣiñcan vājinena tat pātraṃ pūrayati
8.7.4	nābhighārayati
8.7.5	vājibhyo 'nubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
8.7.6	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite vājino yajeti saṃpreṣyati
8.7.7	anavānaṃ hotā yājyām anvāha
8.7.8	vaṣaṭkṛte 'dhvaryuḥ srucā srāvayañ juhoti
8.7.9	vājinasyāgne vīhīti hotānuyajati
8.7.10	vājinodrekeṇa pratidiśaṃ yajati diśaḥ svāheti prācyāṃ pradiśaḥ svāheti dakṣiṇata ādiśaḥ svāheti paścimato vidiśaḥ svāhety uttarata uddiśaḥ svāheti madhye svāhā digbhya iti pradakṣiṇam anupariṣiñcati namo digbhya iti vopatiṣṭhate
8.7.11	antarvedi śeṣaṃ samupahūya parasparam asāv upahvayasvety āmantraṇe kṛta upahūta iti prativacane ca vājināṃ bhakṣo avatv iti sarve vājinaṃ bhakṣayanti tatra prathamo hotā yajamānaś caramaḥ
8.8.1	paśuvat samiṣṭayajūṃṣi
8.8.2	ato 'nyatsiddheṣṭiḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
8.8.3	śvaḥ paurṇamāsyeṣṭvā yajamānaḥ svāyatana upaviśyāpa undantv ity adbhiḥ śiro 'bhyudya treṇyā śalalyekṣuśalākayā vā keśān vibhajyartam eva parameṣṭhīti pratidiśaṃ keśān nirvartayati
8.8.4	śmaśrūṇy agre vāpayate sarvaṃ vā vāpayate
8.8.5	tad ṛtam iti yajamāno japati brāhmaṇa ekahoteti cānuvākam
8.8.6	eteṣu parvasu madhye māṃsānaśanādivratāni
8.8.7	caturṣu māseṣu yo yajate sa cāturmāsyayājī
8.8.8	vasante vaiśvadevena varṣāsu varuṇapraghāsaiḥ śaradi sākamedhair yo yajate sa ṛtuyājī
8.9.1	āṣāḍhyāṃ śrāvaṇyāṃ vā varuṇapraghāsair yajate
8.9.2	vaiśvadevavat tantram
8.9.3	eteṣāṃ vedau kṛtvāgreṇa gārhapatyaṃ same dve prācyau vedī pratiprasthātā dārśikīṃ dakṣiṇāṃ vediṃ karoti pāśukīm adhvaryur uttarāṃ tatra pāśukīm uttaravediṃ ca
8.9.4	pṛthamātreṇa caturaṅgulena vā śroṇyaṃseṣv asaṃbhinne vedī
8.9.5	adhvaryupratiprasthātārau brahmāṇaṃ saṃpreṣyataḥ
8.9.6	dvau brahmā prasauti
8.9.7	pratiprasthātāntarā vedī saṃcarati
8.9.8	apareṇottarāṃ vediṃ stambayajur harannādhvaryum abhipariharati
8.9.9	uttarasminn evotkare nivapati
8.9.10	yad evādhvaryuḥ karoti pratiprasthātā tat karoti
8.9.11	uttarāt parigrāhākṛtvā dakṣiṇaveder uttaraśroṇeḥ prakramyottarasyā veder dakṣiṇād aṃsāt sphyenaikasyām anusaṃbhinatti
8.9.12	paśubandhavad ubhāv āhavanīyau praṇīyobhayatrottaravedisaṃbhāreṣv agnī pratiṣṭhāpayataḥ
8.9.13	agnīn anvādhāya mārutyā vāruṇyāś cobhayor āmikṣayor vatsān apākurutaḥ sāyaṃdohau pṛthagdadhinī kurutaḥ
8.10.1	sadyaskālā varuṇapraghāsā ity eke
8.10.2	prātarhute 'gnihotre pāṇiprakṣālanādi pratipadya pṛthak pātrāṇi prayuṅktaḥ
8.10.3	srucaḥ śamīmayyo hiraṇmayyo vā
8.10.4	adhvaryuḥ pañca saṃcarāṇy aindrāgnam ekādaśakapālaṃ ca nirvapati
8.10.5	pratiprasthātā mārutīm āmikṣāṃ prati mārutyai meṣyai yavān nirvapaty adhvaryur vāruṇīm āmikṣāṃ prati vāruṇāya meṣāya yavān nirupya kāyam ekakapālaṃ nirvapati
8.10.6	puṃvyañjano meṣaḥ strīvyañjanī meṣī
8.10.7	prokṣaṇīśeṣeṇa yavān saṃyutyāvahanti
8.10.8	aindrāgnaparyantānāṃ kapāleṣūpahiteṣu manāgupataptānām avāñjanapiṣṭānāṃ yavānāṃ pratipuruṣaṃ karambhapātrāṇy ekātiriktāni teṣām evādhvaryur vāruṇaṃ meṣaṃ pratiprasthātā mārutīṃ meṣīm ekādaśasu dvādaśasu vā kapāleṣv adhiśrayati
8.10.9	āpyebhyo ninīyāgnī praṇayata ity eke
8.10.10	agnivaty uttaraṃ parigrāhaṃ parigṛhya sruvaṃ srucaś ca saṃmṛḍḍhi patnīṃ saṃnahyājyena dadhnā codehīti saṃpraiṣaṃ saṃnamati
8.11.1	vaiśvadevavat pṛṣadājyaṃ gṛhṇītaḥ
8.11.2	haviṣām udvāsane 'naiḍakībhir ūrṇāstukābhī romaśau kurutaḥ
8.11.3	yadi tā na vindetāṃ kuśāgraiḥ
8.11.4	camase vājinopastīryāmikṣām uddhṛtya tasyāṃ meṣam avadadhāti tathā vāruṇyāṃ meṣīm
8.11.5	tayoḥ śamīparṇakarīrasaktūn upavapataḥ
8.11.6	tāni karambhapātreṣu copyottarasyāṃ vedyām āgneyādīny anyāni havīṃṣy adhvaryuḥ sādayati dakṣiṇāyāṃ mārutīṃ pratiprasthātā karambhapātrāṇi ca
8.11.7	meṣau vyatyasyato mārutyāṃ meṣīṃ vāruṇyāṃ meṣam
8.11.8	utkare 'dhvaryur eva vājine āsādayati
8.11.9	nirmanthyena caritvā vedaṃ nidhāyāgnaye samidhyamānāyeti saṃpreṣyati
8.11.10	sāmidhenīṣv anūktāsu vedābhyām āhavanīyau trir upavājayataḥ
8.11.11	uttare saṃmṛṣṭe 'saṃmṛṣṭe dakṣiṇe praghāsyān havāmaha iti pratiprasthātā patnīṃ vācayitvodānayati
8.12.1	patni kati te jārā iti tāṃ pṛcchati
8.12.2	sā yān prabrūyāt tān varuṇo gṛhṇātv iti nirdiśati
8.12.3	yaj jāraṃ santaṃ na prabrūyāt priyaṃ jñātiṃ rundhyād asau me jāra iti nirdiśet
8.12.4	viparītau vānayanapraśnau
8.12.5	aiṣīke śūrpa opya karambhapātrāṇi patnī śīrṣann adhi nidhāyāntarā vedī gatvāgreṇa dakṣiṇam agniṃ pratyaṅmukhy avatiṣṭhate pratyaṅmukhaś ca yajamānaḥ
8.12.6	tāni patnī yajamānāya prayacchati
8.12.7	śīrṣann adhi nidhāya mo ṣū ṇa iti puronuvākyām anvāha yad grāma iti patnī yajamānaś ca yājyām anubrūtaḥ
8.12.8	juhutaś ca śūrpaṃ cānupraharati
8.12.9	adhvaryuḥ pratiprasthātā vā juhoty anvārabhete itarau
8.12.10	akran karma karmakṛta iti viparāyantau japato 'dhvaryur vā
8.13.1	pratiprasthātā dakṣiṇam agniṃ saṃmārṣṭi
8.13.2	aindrāgnaparyantaḥ pracarite mārutyā āmikṣāyāḥ prathamenāvadānena saha pratiprasthātā sarvāṃ meṣīm avadyati
8.13.3	dvitīyenāvadānena śamīparṇakarīrasaktūn avadyan marudbhyo 'nubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
8.13.4	vāruṇyā āmikṣāyāḥ prathamenāvadānena sahādhvaryuḥ sarvaṃ meṣam avadyati
8.13.5	dvitīyena śamīparṇakarīrasaktūn avadyan varuṇāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣya vaṣaṭkṛte 'dhvaryur hutvaikakapālam avadāya kāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣya pūrvavaddhutvā nabhaś ca nabhasyaś ceti caturbhir māsanāmabhir ekakapālam abhijuhoti
8.13.6	saptabhyo vāruṇyantebhya iḍāṃ samavadāya pratiprasthātre prayacchati
8.13.7	tasmin pratiprasthātā mārutyā avadāyādadhāti
8.13.8	upahūtāṃ yajamānaṣaṣṭhāḥ prāśnanti
8.13.9	dhenur dakṣiṇā
8.13.10	parivatsarīṇāṃ svastim āśāsta ity āśiḥṣu hotā pūrvavad anuvartayati
8.13.11	prahṛtya paridhīn ubhau vājibhyo 'nubrūhīti pūrvavac carataḥ
8.13.12	ā mā viśantv indava iti sarve vājinaṃ bhakṣayanti
8.13.13	pūrṇapātravarjam ato 'nyatsiddheṣṭiḥ
8.14.1	pūrṇapātrasthāne 'vabhṛthaḥ
8.14.2	caturgṛhītāny ājyāni
8.14.3	vāruṇyā niṣkāsaṃ tuṣāṃś cādāya cātvālotkarāv antareṇodaṅṅ atikramya yatrāpas tatra saumikāvabhṛtham abhyavayanti
8.14.4	nāyurdādi na sāma gīyate
8.14.5	ṛjīṣasthāne tuṣā bhavanti
8.14.6	vāruṇavan niṣkāsam apsu juhoti
8.14.7	avabhṛthād udetya yajamānaḥ patnī ca manojñāya vāsasī dattaḥ
8.14.8	naiva vāvabhṛthaḥ
8.14.9	tūṣṇīṃ tuṣaniṣkāsam apsūpavaped ity eke
8.14.10	imaṃ viṣyāmīti yoktrapāśaṃ viṣyate
8.14.11	devīr āpa iti saumikavat
8.14.12	samāropyāgnīn udavasāya nirmathya śvobhūte paurṇamāsyeṣṭvā nivartanaṃ vāpanaṃ ca vyākhyātam
8.14.13	atra yaddharma iti nivartanamantro mantraḥ
9.1.1	pūrvavac caturṣu māseṣu kārttikyāṃ mārgaśīrṣyāṃ vā pūrvasmin parvaṇy aupavasathye 'hani dvyahaṃ sākamedhahavirbhir yajate
9.1.2	agnaye 'nīkavate puroḍāśam aṣṭākapālaṃ nirvapati sākaṃ sūryeṇodyateti yathā samāmnātā anīkavānt sāṃtapano gṛhamedhīya iti tisra iṣṭayaḥ
9.1.3	yad anīkavato barhis tat sāṃtapanasya tad gṛhamedhīyasya
9.1.4	tat stīrṇaṃ barhir nānyad idhmābarhir na prayājānūyājāḥ
9.1.5	tūṣṇīṃ gṛhamedhīyasya vatsān apākaroty api vā sāyaṃdohavad dugdhe carur bhavati
9.1.6	sāyaṃ hute 'gnihotre 'gnīn anvādhāya vedaṃ kṛtvā paristaraṇādi pratipadya pātrasaṃsādanakāle kumbhīṃ tisraś ca pātrīḥ saṃsādayati
9.1.7	nirvapaṇakāle marudbhyo gṛhamedhibhyaś caturo muṣṭīn nirupya yāvadyajur utpūtābhimantritadugdhaṃ prabhūtān vrīhīn anvāvapati
9.1.8	kapālasthāne dhruvo 'sīti mantraṃ saṃnamya carum upadadhāti
9.1.9	piṣṭotpavanasthāne taṇḍulān utpunāti
9.1.10	prokṣaṇīr āsādaya sruvaṃ ca srucaś ca saṃmṛḍḍhi patnīṃ saṃnahyājyenodehīti saṃpreṣyati
9.2.1	ājyagrahe dhruvāyām eva gṛhītvā brahmāṇam āmantrya vediṃ prokṣya taccheṣaṃ ninīyāpisṛjya pavitre antarvedi vidhṛtau nidhāya prastaram āsādya dhruvāṃ sruvaṃ ca sādayati
9.2.2	eṣāsadad ity abhimantraṇaṃ saṃnamati
9.2.3	viṣṇv asīty ājyābhimantraṇam
9.2.4	havirudvāsane śṛtāddhaviṣaḥ śaram ādāya surakṣitaṃ nidhāya nirṇijya pātrīṣūpastīrya tāsu pratipuruṣam odanān uddharati
9.2.5	trīn ity eke
9.2.6	niṣkāsitāṃ kumbhīṃ nidadhāti
9.2.7	anirmṛṣṭaṃ darvyudāyuvanam avadhāyodanān uddhṛtān abhighāritān utpūtān alaṃkṛtān antarvedy āsādayati
9.2.8	anvāhāryapacane patnyai strīkumārebhyaś ca prativeśam odanaṃ pacati
9.2.9	taddvayoḥ pātrayor uddhṛtyoddhṛtayor odanayor bile kṛtvā tayoḥ prabhūtam ājyam āsicyāntarvedy āsādayati
9.2.10	hotṛṣadanakalpanānte 'gnim upavājyājyabhāgābhyāṃ pracarya srucy upastīrya sarvebhya odanebhyo dvir dviḥ samavadāyābhighārya pratyajya marudbhyo gṛhamedhibhyo 'nubrūhīti saṃpreṣya dakṣiṇātikramyāśrāvya pratyāśrāvite maruto gṛhamedhino yajeti saṃpreṣyati
9.2.11	vaṣaṭkṛte hutvodaṅṅ atyākramya sarveṣām uttarārdhebhyaḥ sakṛt sakṛt samavadāyāgniṃ sviṣṭakṛtaṃ yajati
9.2.12	iḍānto gṛhamedhīyaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.3.1	havirbhojanebhya odanān upaharati
9.3.2	prativeśapakvān patnī strīkumārāḥ prāśnanti yaḥ sthālyām odanas tam anye brāhmaṇāḥ
9.3.3	sarva āśitā āñjate 'bhyañjate 'nu vatsān vāsayanti
9.3.4	suhitā etāṃ rātriṃ vasanti
9.3.5	pūrṇadarvyāya śaraniṣkāsaṃ darvyudāyuvanaṃ ca pariśinaṣṭi
9.3.6	apararātre 'dhvaryur abhivānyavatsāyā agnihotryāś ca vatsau saṃyamya purā prātaragnihotrād darvyām upastīrya tasyāṃ sarvaśa eva niṣkāsaṃ śaraṃ cānimṛṣṭaṃ darvyudāyuvanam avadhāya dvir ājyenābhighārayati
9.3.7	ṛṣabhe nardati pūrṇā darvīty anudrutya dehi ma iti gārhapatye juhoti
9.3.8	yady ṛṣabho na narded brahmā hiṃkuryāt
9.3.9	yo nardati sa dakṣiṇā
9.3.10	payasā prātarhute 'gnihotre marudbhyaḥ krīḍibhyaḥ puroḍāśaṃ saptakapālaṃ nirvapati sākaṃ sūryeṇodyatā
9.3.11	marudbhyaḥ svatavadbhya ity eke
9.3.12	atha pañca saṃcarāṇy aindrāgnam ekādaśakapālam aindraṃ caruṃ vaiśvakarmaṇam ekakapālam ity aparāṇy aṣṭau mahānti havīṃṣi varuṇapraghāsottaravihāravat prayunakti
9.3.13	asaṃsṛṣṭam aindrāgnam avahṛtya surakṣitaṃ pṛthak tuṣān nidadhāti
9.3.14	agne ver hotraṃ ver dūtyam iti srucyam āghāram āghārayati
9.3.15	vāg asyāgneyīti yajamāno 'numantrayate
9.3.16	sahaś ca sahasyaś ceti caturbhir ekakapālam abhijuhoti
9.3.17	dhenur dakṣiṇā
9.3.18	idāvatsarīṇāṁ svastim āśāsta ity āśiḥṣu hotānuvartayati
9.3.19	aindrāgnatuṣair avabhṛtham abhyavayanti
9.4.1	atha mahāpitṛyajño bhavati
9.4.2	vedaṃ kṛtvānvāhāryapacanasya dakṣiṇāpūrvasyāṃ diśi dikṣu sraktimatīṃ caturaratnīṃ yajamānamātrīṃ vā samacaturaśrāṃ vedim uddhṛtya na khanet
9.4.3	devapravāde mantre sarvatropari devaśabdasya pitṛśabdaṃ saṃnamati yathā devebhyaḥ pitṛbhyo juṣṭaṃ devānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ pariṣūtam asi devapitṛbarhir iti
9.4.4	sarvataḥ pariśrityodīcyāṃ sraktau dvāraṃ karoti
9.4.5	aparigṛhīta uttarasmin parigrāhe 'nvāhāryapacanād aṅgārān uddhṛtya vedimadhye nidadhāti
9.4.6	ayam atrāhavanīyaḥ
9.4.7	etam āhavanīyaṃ gārhapatyam anvāhāryapacanaṃ cānvādhāya piṇḍapitṛyajñavad barhir āharati
9.4.8	varṣīyān idhma idhmād bhavati
9.4.9	madhyamottarau dvau paridhī trayo vā
9.4.10	pātrasaṃsādane 'rdhapātraṃ prokṣaṇīkumbha ikṣuśalākā vāraṇaṃ pātraṃ śarāvaṃ vā yena cārthas tāny ekaikaśaḥ prayunakti
9.4.11	nirvapaṇakāle somāya pitṛmate puroḍāśaṃ ṣaṭkapālaṃ nirvapatīti yathā samāmnātāni trīṇi havīṃṣi
9.4.12	dakṣiṇataḥ prācīnāvītī yavān nirvapati
9.4.13	uttarata evopavīya nirvaped iti vijñāyate
9.4.14	prokṣaṇībhir yavān saṃyutyāvahatya triṣphalīkṛtya yathābhāgamantreṇa ṣaṭkapālaṃ vibhajya pinaṣṭi
9.5.1	dakṣiṇataḥ ṣaṭkapālāny upadhāya dhruvam asīti prathamena mantreṇānvāhāryapacane dhānābhyaḥ kapālam upadadhāti makhasya śiro 'sīti ṣaṭkapālam adhiśritya tenaiva mantreṇa gharmāḥ stha viśvāyuva iti saṃnamya vā dhānā āvapati tāś ca vidahyamānāḥ śerate vidahyamānā bahurūpā bhavanti
9.5.2	parigṛhīta uttarasmin parigrāhe patnīsaṃnahanād anyat saṃpreṣyati
9.5.3	na patny anvāste na saṃyājayantīti vijñāyate
9.5.4	caturgṛhītāny uttareṇa gārhapatyam ājyāni gṛhṇāti dvir vopabhṛti
9.5.5	vedistaraṇe prācīnāvīty agreṣu barhir abhigṛhya vediṃ stṛṇaṃs triḥ prasavyaṃ dhūnvan paryeti
9.5.6	śiṣṭān abhigṛhītān darbhān prastarīkṛtyopavīya trir adhūnvann astṛṇan pradakṣiṇaṃ paryeti
9.5.7	dvau trīn vā paridhīn paridadhāti
9.5.8	yadi trīn āvāhane paridhīṁr aporṇv ity ucyamāne vā dakṣiṇaṃ madhyame paridhāv upasamasyati
9.6.1	vihāya vidhṛtī tūṣṇīṃ prastaraṃ nyasyati
9.6.2	haviṣām udvāsane yathābhāgamantreṇa dhānā vibhajya piṣṭvārdhān saktūn kṛtvā vāraṇapātre 'bhivānyavatsāyā dugdham ānīya tasmin saktūn opyekṣuśalākāmanthena dakṣiṇenāhavanīyaṃ triḥ prasavyaṃ dakṣiṇāmukho 'nārabhyopamanthati
9.6.3	anvāhāryapacanād ekolmukam ādāyāpareṇa gārhapatyaṃ hṛtvāgreṇāhavanīyaṃ paryāhṛtyāntarvedi dakṣiṇenāhavanīyaṃ nidadhāti
9.6.4	havīṃṣy alaṃkṛtyājyāni puroḍāśaṃ dhānāḥ karambham iti havīṃṣy ekaikam anūcīnāny udāharanti dakṣiṇataḥ puroḍāśaṃ madhyato dhānā uttarataḥ karambham
9.6.5	dakṣiṇena pariśrayaṇam āñjanam abhyañjanaṃ kaśipūpabarhaṇaṃ daśā sphyam udakumbhaṃ caikaikaṃ sthāpayati
9.6.6	brahmā ca yajamānaś ca dakṣiṇato hotādhvaryur āgnīdhraś cottarataḥ
9.6.7	adhvaryur vedaṃ nidhāyāgnaye devebhyaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ samidhyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
9.6.8	uśantas tvā havāmaha ity ekāṃ sāmidhenīṃ hotā trir anvāha
9.6.9	imam adhvaryus traidhaṃ vibhajyānūyājasamidham avaśiṣya praṇave praṇave traidham ādadhāti
9.7.1	saṃmṛṣṭe 'gnau nārṣeyaṃ vṛṇīte na hotāram
9.7.2	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite sīda hotar ity etāvantaṃ pravaraṃ brūyāt
9.7.3	apabarhiṣaḥ prayājāḥ
9.7.4	aupabhṛtasyārdhaṃ juhvām ānīyā no 'gne suketunā tvaṁ soma mahe bhagam iti jīvavantāv ājyabhāgau
9.7.5	sarve prācīnāvītino viparikrāmanty ājyāni havīṃṣi ca vipariharanty uttareṇāhavanīyaṃ brahmayajamānau dakṣiṇenetare
9.7.6	dakṣiṇena juhūm upabhṛtaṃ sādayati tāṃ dakṣiṇena dhruvāṃ dakṣiṇena puroḍāśaṃ dhānāḥ sādayati tā dakṣiṇena mantham
9.7.7	ṣaḍavattaḥ pañcāvattināṃ pañcāvattaś caturavattinām
9.7.8	upāṃśu pitṛyajñena caranti
9.7.9	tribhyo havirbhyaḥ samavadāyaikaikāṃ devatāṃ yajati
9.7.10	tattaddevatāyai tattaddhaviṣaḥ prathamam avadyed dviḥ pañcāvattinaḥ sakṛc caturavattinaḥ
9.7.11	juhvām upastīrya puroḍāśād avadāya dhānābhyaś ca manthāc ca sakṛt sakṛd avadāya sakṛd abhighārayati caturavattinaḥ
9.7.12	somāya pitṛmate 'nu svadheti saṃpreṣyati
9.7.13	tvaṁ soma pracikito manīṣā tvayā hi naḥ pitaraḥ someti hotā dve puronuvākye sapraṇave anvāha
9.7.14	athādhvaryur dakṣiṇato havir ādāyodaṅṅ atikramyā svadhā svadheti vāśrāvayati
9.7.15	astu svadhā svadheti vā pratyāśrāvayati
9.8.1	somaṃ pitṛmantaḥ svadheti svadhā kurv iti vā saṃpreṣyati
9.8.2	ye svadhāmaha ity āgūr bhavati
9.8.3	tvaṁ soma pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidāna iti hotā yajati
9.8.4	svadhā nama iti vaṣaṭkaroti
9.8.5	etayaivāvṛtottarābhyāṃ yathādevataṃ yajati
9.8.6	apy āśrutapratyāśrutāny eva
9.8.7	na svadhāśabda ity eke
9.8.8	dhānābhyaḥ puroḍāśān manthāc cāvadāya pitṛbhyo barhiṣadbhyo 'nu svadheti saṃpreṣyati barhiṣadaḥ pitaro 'haṃ pitṝn iti dve
9.8.9	udaṅṅ atikramyāśrāvya pratyāśrāvite pitṝn barhiṣadaḥ svadhā svadhā kurv iti vā saṃpreṣyati
9.8.10	ye svadhāmaha ity āgūḥ
9.8.11	upahūtāḥ pitara iti yajati
9.8.12	svadhā nama iti vaṣaṭkaroti
9.8.13	udaṅṅ atikramya manthāt puroḍāśād dhānābhyaś cāvadāya pitṛbhyo 'gniṣvāttebhyo 'nu svadheti saṃpreṣyati
9.8.14	agniṣvāttāḥ pitaro ye agniṣvāttā ye 'nagniṣvāttā iti puronuvākye
9.8.15	pitṝn agniṣvāttān svadhā svadhā kurv iti vā saṃpreṣyati
9.8.16	ye svadhāmaha ity āgūr bhavati vānyāyai dugdha iti yajati
9.8.17	svadhā nama iti vaṣaṭkaroti
9.8.18	juhvām upastīrya trayāṇāṃ haviṣāṃ dakṣiṇārdhebhyaḥ samavadāya dvir abhighāryāgnaye kavyavāhanāya sviṣṭakṛte 'nu svadheti saṃpreṣyati
9.8.19	yad agne kavyavāhana tvam agna īḍita iti dve
9.8.20	agniṃ kavyavāhanaṁ sviṣṭakṛtaṁ svadhā svadhā kurv iti vā saṃpreṣyati
9.9.1	ye svadhāmaha ity āgūr bhavati
9.9.2	mātalī kavyair iti yajati
9.9.3	svadhā nama iti vaṣaṭkaroti
9.9.4	dakṣiṇapūrvārdha itarābhir asaṃsaktāṃ juhoti
9.9.5	mekṣaṇam ikṣuśalākāṃ cānupraharati
9.9.6	yajñopavītinaḥ sarve viparikrāmanty ājyāni havīṃṣi ca vipariharanti dakṣiṇenāhavanīyaṃ brahmayajamānāv uttareṇetare
9.9.7	juhūm uttareṇopabhṛtaṃ dhruvāṃ ca puroḍāśam uttareṇa dhānāmanthau
9.9.8	na prāśitrāvadānam
9.9.9	manthād eveḍām avadyati
9.9.10	upahūtāyām iḍāyāṃ tataḥ kiṃcid avaghrāya barhiṣi lepaṃ saṃnyasyati
9.9.11	prācīnāvītino haviḥśeṣān pātryāṃ saṃprayutya trīn piṇḍān kṛtvaitat te tatāsau ye ca tvām anv iti pratimantraṃ tisṛṣu sraktiṣu pūrvadakṣiṇāparāsu piṇḍān pradāya parān pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahān anvācaṣṭe ṣaṣṭhaṃ prathame piṇḍe pañcamaṃ dvitīye caturthaṃ tṛtīye
9.9.12	uttarasyāṃ sraktyāṃ lepaṃ nimārṣṭi
9.9.13	atra pitaro yathābhāgaṃ mandadhvam ity udañco niṣkrāmanti
9.9.14	susaṃdṛśaṃ tvā vayam ity aindryarcā praṇavāntayāhavanīyam ā tamitor upatiṣṭhante 'kṣann amīmadanteti gārhapatyam
9.9.15	akṣan pitara iti pariśritaṃ praviśanti
9.10.1	udakumbham ādāya yajamānaḥ śundhantāṃ pitara iti triḥ prasavyaṃ vedim apaḥ pariṣiñcan paryeti
9.10.2	nidhāya kumbham ayā viṣṭhā janayann iti trir apariṣiñcan pratiparyeti
9.10.3	āñjanābhyañjanādi piṇḍapitṛyajñavat kṛtvā pariśritaṃ visṛjya paridhīn yathāpūrvaṃ nidhāya yajñopavītino brahman prasthāsyāma ity apabarhirbhyām anūyājābhyāṃ saṃpreṣyati devau yajeti prathamam anūyājaṃ yajety uttaram
9.10.4	srucau sādayitvā vājavatībhyāṃ vyūhati
9.10.5	hotā sūktavākaṃ pratipadyate
9.10.6	na patnīḥ saṃyājayanti na samiṣṭayajuḥ
9.10.7	pātrāṇi dvandvam udāharanti
9.10.8	sarvam anyat siddham
9.10.9	pratipūruṣaṃ traiyambakān raudrān ekakapālān nirvapaty ekam atiriktaṃ yāvanto yajamānasyāmātyāḥ sastrīkās teṣām
9.10.10	yāvanto gṛhyāḥ sma iti nirupyamāṇeṣu vrīhiṣu yajamāno japati
9.10.11	ayajuṣkāḥ puroḍāśā bhavanti
9.10.12	gārhapatyād udīco 'ṅgārān nirūhya teṣv adhiśritya nābhighārayati
9.10.13	sate havīṃṣy udvāsyāntarvedy āsādya paśūnāṃ śarmāsīti mūte mahaty opyaika eva rudra ity anvāhāryapacanād ekolmukam ādāyāpareṇa gārhapatyaṃ gatvottarapūrvaṃ catuṣpathaṃ yanti
9.10.14	ākhus te rudra paśur ity ākhumūṣāyām ekaṃ puroḍāśam upavapati
9.11.1	asau te rudra paśur iti vā nirdiśed yaṃ dviṣyāt
9.11.2	catuṣpathe sthaṇḍilam ullikhyaikolmukaṃ nidhāyopasamidhya paristīrya madhyamena palāśaparṇena sarvebhyaḥ puroḍāśānām uttarārdhebhyaḥ sakṛt sakṛd avadāyaiṣa te rudra bhāga iti tasminn agnau juhoti
9.11.3	etat parṇaṃ yaṃ dviṣyāt tasya saṃcare paśūnāṃ nyasyet
9.11.4	bheṣajaṃ gava iti dvābhyām agnim upatiṣṭhante 'vāmba rudramadimahīti yajamāno japati
9.11.5	yajamānasyāmātyāḥ sarva ekam ekaṃ puroḍāśam ādāya tryambakaṃ yajāmaha ity etam agniṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ dakṣiṇān ūrūn āghnānāḥ pariyanti
9.11.6	tān puroḍāśān ūrdhvam udasya pratilabhyottaratas tiṣṭhato yajamānasyāñjalau samopya bhagaḥ stha bhagasya vo lapsīyety upādadate
9.11.7	evaṃ dvitīyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ ca
9.11.8	tṛtīye paryāye nopādadate
9.11.9	bhagena tvā saṃsṛjāmi māsareṇa surām iveti saṃsṛjanti
9.11.10	tam ādāya vṛkṣe badhnāti
9.11.11	eṣa te rudra bhāga iti praṇavāntenā tamitor upatiṣṭhante
9.11.12	apaḥ pariṣicyāpratīkṣam āyanti
9.11.13	hastapādān prakṣālya yathetam etya goṣṭhe mārjayante
9.12.1	edho 'sy edhiṣīmahīty āhavanīye samidho 'bhyādhāyāpo 'nvacāriṣam ipatyutiṣṭhante tathā patnī gārhapatye
9.12.2	ādityaṃ ghṛte carum anunirvapati viṣṇave caruṃ nirvapati
9.12.3	yajño vai viṣṇur yajña evāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhatīti vijñāyate
9.12.4	śveto 'śvo dakṣiṇā gaur vā
9.12.5	prabhāte paurṇamāsyeṣṭvondanaprabhṛti vyākhyātam
9.12.6	yo asyāḥ pṛthivyā ity atra nivartanam
9.12.7	ito 'nyat siddhaṃ saṃtiṣṭhate
9.12.8	saṃtiṣṭhante sākamedhahavīṃṣi
9.12.9	atha caturahe tryahe dvyahe caturṣu māseṣu vā vaiśvadevavacchunāsīrīyahavirbhir yajate
9.12.10	pañca saṃcarāṇy aindrāgnaṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ vaiśvadevaṃ carum indrāya śunāsīrāya puroḍāśaṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ vāyavyaṃ payaḥ sauryam ekakapālam
9.12.11	dvādaśagavaṃ sauraṃ dakṣiṇā
9.12.12	yady uttaravedir bhavati yathā vāruṇapraghāsikottaravihāravat
9.12.13	saṃsarpo 'sy aṃhaspatyāya tvety uttamena māsanāmnaikakapālam abhijuhoti
9.12.14	anuvatsarīṇāṃ svastim āśāste vatsarīṇām iti vā
9.12.15	aparapakṣe parvaṇy etāni samasyan paurṇamāsyā svakālayeṣṭvā
9.12.16	vyākhyātam undanaprabhṛti
9.12.17	ekaṃ māsam udasṛjaditi nivartanamantraḥ
9.12.18	saṃtiṣṭhante cāturmāsyāni cāturmāsyāni
10.1.1	aindrāgnena sauryeṇa prājāpatyena vā nirūḍhapaśubandhena pratisaṃvatsaraṃ pratyayanaṃ pratiṣāṇmāsaṃ vā yakṣyamāṇaḥ paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāyām āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre vā yajeta
10.1.2	mṛtyor ātmānaṃ niṣkrīṇāti sarvān kāmān avāpnoti
10.1.3	paśubandhasya yajñakratoḥ ṣaḍṛtvija āgnīdhro brahmā ca brahmāṇau hotā maitrāvaruṇaś ca hotārāv adhvaryuḥ pratiprasthātā cādhvaryū
10.1.4	sūryaṃ ta iti manasānudrutenānuvākena hutvāgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālam anvārambhaṇīyāṃ nirvapaty, api vāgnāvaiṣṇavyarcāhāvanīye caturgṛhītam juhoti
10.1.5	śeṣaṃ kṛtvāvasthāpyāhavanīyam, uru viṣṇo vikramasvety āhavanīye sruveṇāhutiṃ juhoti
10.1.6	hutaśeṣam sruvaṃ cādāya takṣṇe śastraṃ pradāya gacchanti
10.1.7	palāśo bilvo rohitakaḥ khadiraś ca yūpavṛkṣāḥ
10.1.8	pālāśo nirūḍhapaśubandhasyāto 'nye saumyādhvarasya
10.1.9	tāṃs tryavarārdhān atītya yaḥ same bhūmyai svād yone rūḍha ṛjur ūrdhvaśākho bahuparṇo bahuśākho 'pratiśuṣkāgro 'vraṇaḥ pratyaṅṅ upanatas tam aty anyān agām ity upasthāya taṃ tvā juṣa iti spṛṣṭvā devas tvā savitā madhvānaktv iti sruveṇa gulphamātre paryajyauṣadhe trāyasvainam ity ūrdhvāgraṃ barhir antardhāya svadhite mainaṃ hiṃsīr iti pradakṣiṇam anakṣasaṅgaṃ vṛścet
10.2.1	yaḥ prathamaḥ śakalaḥ parāpatet tam apy āharet
10.2.2	divam agreṇeti prāgagram udagagraṃ vā nipātayet
10.2.3	vanaspate śatavalśo virohety āvraścane hiraṇyam nidhāya paristīryābhijuhoti
10.2.4	sahasravalśā ity ātmānaṃ pratyabhimṛśati
10.2.5	yaṃ tvāyam iti mūlād agrāntaṃ śākhāḥ prahāpayati
10.2.6	acchinno rāyaḥ suvīra iti pañcāratnāv agraṃ parivṛścati caturaratnau tryaratnau vā
10.2.7	sahopareṇa yūpaṃ saṃcakṣīta
10.2.8	aṣtāśrim asthūlam anaṇuṃ gopucchavad ānupūrvyeṇāgrato 'ṇīyāṃsam viśiṣṭāgniṣṭhāśrimat aṣṭadviprādeśoparaṃ yūpaṃ takṣayati
10.2.9	eṣām evāvatakṣaṇānāṃ svaruṃ karoty adhimanthanaśakalaṃ ca
10.2.10	yūpasyaivāgrata ādāyāṣṭāśri pṛthamātraṃ madhye saṃnataṃ caṣālaṃ karoti dvyaṅgulaṃ tryaṅgulaṃ vordhvaṃ caṣālād yūpasyātirecayati
10.2.11	atirikte caṣālam saṃdhāyātiriktaṃ prakāśayati
10.3.1	vedaṃ kṛtvāgreṇāhavanīyaṃ nirūḍhapaśubandhasya ṣaḍbhir aratnibhiḥ prācīṃ caturbhiḥ paścāttiraścīṃ tribhiḥ purastāt tiraścīṃ darśapūrṇamāsavad asaṃnatām vediṃ karoti
10.3.2	aparigṛhīta uttarasmin parigrāhe vedyagre yūpāvaṭāya deśaṃ śiṣṭvottaravediṃ śamyayā parimimīte
10.3.3	pratidiśam udīcīnāgrāṃ vā śamyāṃ nidhāya vittāyanī me 'sīti caturbhiḥ pratimantram udīcyau prācyau ca sphyena lekhā abhyantaraṃ parilikhati
10.3.4	uttaravedyaṃsam uttareṇa prakrame dvayos triṣu vottaravedivat tūṣṇīṃ cātvālaṃ parilikhati
10.3.5	devasya tvety abhrim ādāya parilikhitam iti triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ parilikhya vider agnir nabho nāmeti trivitastaṃ khanati
10.4.1	agne aṅgira ity abhriṃ nidhāya yo 'syāṃ pṛthivyām asīti pāṃsūn ādāyāyuṣā nāmnehīti hṛtvā yat te 'nādhṛṣṭaṃ nāma yajñiyam ity uttaravedyāṃ nivapati
10.4.2	vider agnir iti dvitīyaṃ khātvāgne aṅgira ity abhriṃ nidhāya yo dvitīyasyām iti dvitīyam ādāya pūrvavan nivapati
10.4.3	tathā tṛtīyam
10.4.4	tṛtīyasyām iti viśeṣaḥ
10.4.5	tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
10.4.6	siṃhīr asi mahiṣīr asīty uttaravediṃ kṛtvoru prathasveti prathayati
10.4.7	dhruvāsīti sphyena śamyayā vā saṃhanti
10.4.8	devebhyaḥ śundhasvety adbhir avokṣya devebhyaḥ śumbhasveti sikatābhir anuprakīrya yat te krūraṃ yad āsthitam ity uttareṇottaravediṃ prokṣaṇīr ninayati, punar eva tābhir avokṣed ity eke
10.4.9	āpo ripraṃ nirvahatety uttarato dakṣiṇato vā sphyenaikasphyām ullikhyāpo ripraṃ nirvahatety uttaravedyāṃ prokṣaṇīśeṣaṃ ninayet
10.4.10	vibhrāḍ bṛhatv ity uttaravedyāḥ paryantān ākalpya catuḥśikhaṇḍe yuvatī kanīne ity uttaravediṃ vediṃ ca yugapat saṃmṛśati
10.4.11	uttaravedimadhye caturdiśaṃ prādeśamātrīṃ madhyamāṅgulocchritām uttaranābhiṃ kalpayet
10.5.1	indraghoṣas tvā vasubhiḥ purastāt pātv ity etair yathārūpaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ pariyan pratidiśam uttaravediṃ prokṣaty upariṣṭāc ca
10.5.2	prokṣaṇyuccheśaṃ pūrvavad dakṣiṇata uttaravedyai ninayet
10.5.3	yadi dvyahaḥ paśur audumbarībhiḥ śākhābhiś channām uttaravediṃ kalpayet
10.5.4	āhavanīye 'gnipraṇayanīyān idhmān ādīpyāgnaye praṇīyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣya dīptān idhmāṃccharāva uddhṛtya sikatāpūritena pātreṇopayamyedhmaṃ codyamya jānudaghne 'gnau dhāryamāṇe yat te pāvaketi śiṣṭe 'gnāv udyatahomaṃ juhoti
10.5.5	prathamāyāṃ trir anūktāyāṃ hṛtvottaravediṃ prāpya juhvāṃ pañcagṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā hiraṇyaṃ nidhāyottaravediṃ pañcagṛhītena vyāghārayati siṃhīr asi sapatnasāhī svāheti dakṣiṇe 'ṃse siṃhīr asi suprajāvaniḥ svāhety uttarasyāṃ śroṇyāṃ siṃhīr asi rāyaspoṣavaniḥ svāheti dakṣiṇasyām śroṇyāṃ siṃhīr asy ādityavaniḥ svāhety uttare 'ṃse siṁhīr asy āvaha devān devayate yajamānāya svāheti madhye
10.5.6	bhūtebhyas tveti srucam udgṛhṇāti hiraṇyaṃ ca
10.5.7	pautudravān paridhīn ādāya viśvāyur asīti tribhir mantraiḥ pūrvavad uttaravediṃ paridadhāti
10.6.1	guggulasugandhitejine śuklorṇāstukā petvasyāntarā śṛṅge yadromaitān saṃbhārān agner bhasmāsīti sakṛd evottaranābhau nyupyorṇāvantam ity ucyamāne 'gne bādhasva yajña pratitiṣṭheti dvābhyāṃ saṃbhāreṣu jvalantam agnim abhyādadhāti
10.6.2	agneḥ kulāyam asīti dakṣiṇata upayamanīḥ sikatā nivapati
10.6.3	manuṣvat tvā nidhīmahīty upasamidhyāgnir yajñaṃ nayatu prajānann iti catasro 'timuktīr hutvā sapta ta iti pūrṇāhutiṃ juhoti
10.6.4	ayam atrāhavanīyo yasmād eṣa praṇīyate sa gārhapatyaḥ
10.6.5	āhavanīyaṃ gārhapatyam anvāhāryapacanaṃ cānvādhāyedhmābarhiṣī
10.6.6	saptadaśa sāmidhenyaḥ
10.6.7	āśvavālaḥ prastara aikṣavī vidhṛtī kārṣmaryamayāḥ paridhayaḥ
10.6.8	agnīn paristīrya pātrasādane vaiśvadevavat pātrāṇy āsādayati
10.7.1	sruvasvadhitī vedasamavattadhānī dviguṇāṃ dvivyāyāmāṃ triguṇāṃ trivyāyāmāṃ ca raśane dve dviśūlaikaśūlā ca dve kārṣmayamayyau vapāśrapaṇyau kumbhīṃ hṛdayaśūlaṃ plakṣaśākhāṃ svarum audumbaraṃ maitrāvaruṇādaṇḍam āsyāntaṃ cubukantaṃ vā prathamaparāpātitaṃ śakalam araṇī suvarṇaśakalāni yena carthaḥ
10.7.2	pavitre kṛtvā yajamāna vācaṃ yaccheti saṃpreṣya vāgyataḥ pātrāṇi saṃmṛśya prokṣiteṣu vācaṃ visṛjate
10.7.3	parigṛhīta uttarasmin parigrāha ājyena dadhnā codehīti saṃnamya saṃpreṣyati
10.7.4	pātrasaṃmārjanakāle sruvānantaraṃ sruvavat svadhitiṃ saṃmārṣṭi
10.7.5	vaiśvadevavad ājyasādanāntaṃ kṛtvā devasya tvety abhrim ādāyārdham antarvedy ardhaṃ barhirvedi sarvataḥ prādeśasaṃmitaṃ yūpāvaṭaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ parilikhitam iti parilikhati
10.7.6	agnīd yūpāvaṭaṃ khanoparasaṃmitaṃ dvyaḥṅgulena tryaṅgulena caturaṅgulena voparam atikhanatād iti saṃpreṣyati
10.7.7	yathoparaṃ nāvirbhavati tathā khanaty āgnīdhraḥ
10.8.1	adhvaryur agreṇāvaṭaṃ yūpaṃ prāgagraṃ sthāpayitvā yat te śikvaḥ parādadhīd iti yūpaṃ prakṣālayati
10.8.2	yavamatīḥ prokṣaṇīr āhṛtya yūpāgre caṣālaṃ saṃdhāya pṛthivyai tveti tribhir mantrair yūpasya mūlam adhyāgrāṇi prokṣati
10.8.3	śundhatāṃ lokaḥ pitṛṣadana iti yūpāvaṭe prokṣaṇīr ninīya yavo 'sīti yavaṃ prahrtya pitṝṇāṃ sadanam asīty avaṭe prāgagraṃ barhir avastṛṇāti
10.8.4	svāveśo 'sīti prathamaparāpātitaṃ śakalam adhastvakkam avadhāya ghṛtena dyāvāpṛthivī āpṛṇethāṃ svāheti hiraṇyaṃ nidhāya sruveṇābhijuhoti
10.8.5	devas tvā savitā madhvānaktv ity agreṇāhavanīyam aniruptenājyena yajamānaḥ prācyāṃ pratyaṅmukhas tiṣṭhan yūpaśakalenānakti
10.8.6	caṣālam unmucya tenaiva mantreṇa yūpāgram anakti
10.8.7	aindram asīti caṣālam ābhyajya supippalābhya iti taṃ pratimucya yūpāyājyam ānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣya devas tvā savitā madhvānaktv iti sruveṇāgniṣṭhām aśriṃ saṃtatam abhidhārayati yāvaduparam
10.8.8	noparam anakati
10.8.9	anaktīty eke
10.8.10	raśanādeśe yūpaṃ sarvatas triḥ parimṛśati
10.8.11	añjanaprabhṛti yajamāno yūpaṃ notsṛjati yāvat parivyayati
10.9.1	ud divaṃ stabhāneti yūpam ucchrayan yūpāyocchrīyamāṇāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
10.9.2	te te dhāmānīti yūpamn avaṭe 'vadadhāti
10.9.3	viṣṇoḥ karmāṇīti dvābhyām agniṣṭhām aśrim āhavanīyāgninā sadiśaṃ kalpayati
10.9.4	brahmavaniṃ tveti pradakṣiṇaṃ purīṣeṇānāvir uparaṃ paryūhya brahma dṛṃheti maitrāvaruṇadaṇḍena parito dṛṃhati
10.9.5	unnambhaya pṛthivīm ity apaḥ pariṣiñcati
10.9.6	devasya tveti triguṇāṃ raśanām ādāyedaṃ viṣṇur vicakrama iti sapāṇyā raśanayā yūpaṃ trir unmārṣṭi
10.9.7	tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam iti yūpāgraṃ paśyet
10.9.8	raśanām adbhiḥ saṃmṛśya triḥ saṃbhujya madhyamena guṇena madhye nābhidaghne vā yūpaṃ parivyayan yūpāya parivīyamāṇāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣya parivīr asīti triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ parivīya sthavimad aṇīyasi pravayati
10.9.9	divaḥ sūnur asīti svaruśakalam ādāyāntarikṣasya tvety uttame guṇe 'gniṣṭhām uttareṇāvagūhati madhyame dvayor vā
10.9.10	kūṭakarṇakāṇakhaṇḍakhañjaghṛṣṭavaṇḍaśloṇasaptaśaphavarjaṃ pannadantaṃ yūthyaṃ mātṛpitṛbhrātṛsakhimantaṃ supalpūlitaṃ paṭṭānītaṃ cātvālotkarāvantareṇa nītvā yūpam agreṇa purastāt pratyaṅmukham avasthāpyeṣe tveti barhiṣī adāyopavīr asīti plakṣaśākhām upo devān iti yajuṣā prajāpater jāyamānā imaṃ paśum ity ṛgbhyāṃ ca tābhyāṃ tayā ca paśum upaspṛśann indrāgnibhyāṃ tvā juṣṭam upākaromīti yathādevam upākaroti
10.10.1	surakṣite barhiṣī nidhāya plakṣaśākhāṃ ca prajānantaḥ pratigṛhṇantīty upākṛtya pañca juhoti
10.10.2	agniṃ manthati
10.10.3	mathitvopākuryād ity eke
10.10.4	agner janitram asīty avaśiṣṭaṃ śakalam ādāyāpareṇāhavanīyaṃ barhiṣi nidhāya tasmin vaiśvadevavad darbau nidadhāti tathāraṇī cādāyājyasthālyā bile 'bhyajya ghṛtenākte ity abhimantryāyur asīti prajanate pramanthaṃ saṃdhāyāgnaye mathyamānāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
10.10.5	trir anūktāyāṃ vaiśvadevavad agnipraharaṇāntaṃ karoti
10.10.6	yadi mathyamāno na jāyeta tatsthāne hiraṇyaṃ vyāhṛtībhir juhuyāt
10.10.7	agnāv agnir iti prahṛtyābhihutya devasya tveti dviguṇāṃ raśanām ādāya tadagreṇa paśor dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum unmṛjya ṛtasya tvā devahaviḥ pāśenārabha iti dakṣiṇe pūrvapāde 'rdhaśirasi ca pratimucya dharṣā mānuṣān iti purastāt pratyaṅmukham udaṅmukhaṃ vā yūpe paśuṃ niyunakti
10.10.8	adbhis tvauṣadhībhyaḥ prokṣāmīti prokṣati
10.10.9	apāṃ perur asīty apaḥ pāyayitvā svāttaṃ cid ity adhastād upokṣati sarvata evainaṃ medhyaṃ karotīti vijñāyate
10.10.10	vedanidhānādi
10.10.11	srucyam āghāryodaṅṅ atikramya saṃ te prāna iti paśor dakṣiṇe 'rdhaśirasi juhvā samajya saṃ yajatrair aṅgānīti kakudi saṃyajñapatir āśiṣeti bhasadi makhasya śiro 'sīti pratipadya hotāraṃ vṛtvāśrāvya pratyāśrāvite mitrāvaruṇau praśāstārau praśāstrād iti maitrāvaruṇaṃ vṛṇīte
10.11.1	asau mānuṣa ity asya nāma gṛhṇāti
10.11.2	asmai daṇḍaṃ dadyāt
10.11.3	avakro 'vidhuro bhūyāsam iti gṛhṇāti
10.11.4	jīvati paśāv ekādaśa prayājān yajati
10.11.5	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite 'dhvaryuḥ samidbhyaḥ preṣyeti maitrāvaruṇaṃ prati prathamaṃ prayājaṃ saṃpreṣyati preṣyety uttarān
10.11.6	hotā yakṣad ity asau hotāraṃ codayati
10.11.7	caturthe prayāje prāpte 'rdhaṃ samānīyāṣṭame sarvaṃ samānayate
10.11.8	iṣṭe daśama ekādaśāyājyam avaśinaṣṭi
10.11.9	tān yajamāna ādyair anumantranaiś caturo 'numantrya caruthasyānumanraṇena duraḥ prabhṛtīṃs trīn uttamenetarān
10.11.10	udaṅṅ atikramyādhvaryur ghṛtenānaktāv iti juhvā svarusvadhitī anakti triḥ svaruṃ sakṛt svadhiter ekām aśrim
10.11.11	ghṛtenāktau paśuṃ trāyethām iti svarusvadhitibhyāṃ paśuṃ samanakti
10.12.1	śamitar eṣā te 'śriḥ prajñātāstv ity ādiśya śamitre svadhitiṃ prayacchati
10.12.2	yathāpūrvaṃ svarum avaguhya paryagnaye kriyamāṇāyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
10.12.3	āgnīdhra āhavanīyād ulmukam ādāya parivājapatir iti triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ ṣaṭ paryeti paśuṃ śāmitradeśaṃ cātvālaṃ yūpam āhavanīyam ājyāni ca
10.12.4	ye badhyamānam anubadhyamānā iti tribhir apāvyaiḥ pratiparyāyaṃ juhoti
10.12.5	apisṛjyāhavanīya ulmukaṃ triḥ punar yathetaṃ pratiparyeti
10.12.6	pramucya paśum āśrāvya pratyāśrāvita upapreṣya hotar havyā devebhya iti saṃpreṣyati
10.12.7	adhriguṃ hotānuvakti
10.12.8	revatīr yajñapatim ity adhvaryuyajamānau vapāśrapaṇībhyāṃ barhirbhyām plakṣaśākhayā ca paśum anvārabhete
10.13.1	nānā prāṇa iti yajamānam abhimantrayate
10.13.2	prāsmā agniṃ bharata ity ucyamāne tad ulmukaṃ punar ādāyāgnīdhraḥ prathamo 'ntareṇa cātvālotkarāv udaṅṅ atikrāmaty uro antarikṣety antareṇa cātvālotkarāv udaṅmukhaṃ paśuṃ nayanti
10.13.3	prājahitād ulmukam ādāyāgnīdhro niṣkrāmatīty eke
10.13.4	uttareṇa cātvālaṃ śāmitrāyatanam
10.13.5	tasminn ulmukam ādhaya śāmitram uttareṇātikrāmati
10.13.6	udīcīnāṃ asya pado nidhattād ity ucyamāne samasya tanuvā bhavety upākaraṇabarhiṣor anyatarad dakṣiṇena śāmitraṃ prāgagram udagagraṃ vā nyasyati
10.13.7	ūvadhyagohaṃ parthivaṃ khanatād ity ucyamāna ūvadhyagohaṃ khanati
10.13.8	tasmin barhiṣi paśuṃ pratyakśirasam udīcīnapādaṃ saṃjñapayanti
10.13.9	amāyuṃ kṛṇvantaṃ saṃjñapayateti saṃpreṣya yathetaṃ parāñca āvartante
10.13.10	iha prajā viśvarūpā ramantām iti pṛṣadājyam avekṣamāṇāḥ parāñca āsate
10.13.11	indrasya bhāgaḥ suvite dadhātanety adhvaryur yadi rauti paśus tam abhimantrayate
10.13.12	svarvid asīti caturo mantrān saṃjñapyamāne yajamāno japati nānā prāṇa ity adhvaryuḥ
10.13.13	yat paśur māyum akṛteti saṃjñapte saṃjñaptahomaṃ juhoti
10.14.1	śamitāra upetaneti paśum abhyupayann aditiḥ paśuṃ pramumoktv iti saṃjñpatāt pāśaṃ pramuñcati
10.14.2	tam ekaśūlayādāyārātīyantam adharaṃ kṛṇomītīmāṃ diśaṃ nirasyati
10.14.3	namas ta ātāneti patny ādityam upatiṣṭhate
10.14.4	anarvā prehīti pratiprasthātā pūrṇapātreṇa saha patnīm udānayati
10.14.5	antareṇa cātvālotkarav udaṅ patnīṃ niṣkrāmayati
10.14.6	āpo devīr iti niṣkrāntām adhvaryur apo 'vamarśayati
10.14.7	vāk ta āpyāyatām ity etair yathāliṅgam anupūrvaṃ patnī paśoḥ prāṇān āpyāyayaty adhvaryur vābhiṣiñcati
10.14.8	yā te prāṇān iti hṛdayam abhimṛśati
10.14.9	tān eva prāṇān punaḥ saṃmṛśatīty eke
10.14.10	nābhis ta āpyāyatām iti nābhiṃ meḍhraṃ ta āpyāyatām iti meḍhraṃ pāyus ta āpyāyatām iti pāyuṃ śuddhāś caritrā iti saṃpragṛhya caturaḥ pādān prakṣālayati
10.14.11	śam abhobhyām ity anupṛṣṭhaṃ śeṣam ninayati dakṣiṇato vā
10.14.12	uttānaṃ paśum āvartya dakṣiṇena nābhiṃ dvyaṅgule tryaṅgule vā vivarte 'vaśiṣtam upākaraṇabarhiṣor anyatarad oṣadhe trāyasvainam iti prāgagraṃ nidadhati
10.14.13	svadhite mainaṃ hiṃsīr iti svadhitinā tiryag ācchinatti
10.14.14	agram ādāya surakṣitaṃ nidadhāti mūlaṃ lohitenāktvā rakṣasām bhāgo 'sītīmāṃ diśaṃ nirasyed idam ahaṃ rakṣo 'dhamaṃ tamo nayāmīti tat savyena padātiṣṭhet
10.15.1	tau pāṇipādau prakṣālyāpaupaspṛśyeṣe tveti vapām utkhidya ghṛtena dyāvāpṛthivī prorṇvāthām iti vapayā dviśūlāṃ vapāśrapaṇīṃ prorṇoti
10.15.2	ūrje tvety ekaśūlayopastṛṇatti vapā yathā vistīrṇā bhavati
10.15.3	devebhyaḥ śundhasveti tāṃ prokṣya devebhyaḥ śunbhasveti svadhitinā vapām unmṛjya devebhyaḥ kalpasvety abhimantryācchinno rāyaḥ suvīra iti tām adhastāduntatkṛti
10.15.4	śamitā vapoddharaṇaṃ muṣṭināpidadhāti yāvadvapāṃ juhoti
10.15.5	vapām adbhir abhyukṣya pratyuṣṭam iti śāmitre pratitapya namaḥ sūryasya saṃdṛśa ity ādityam upasthāya śāmitrād ekolmukam ādāyāgnīdhraḥ pūrvaṃ gacchaty anvag adhvaryur vapāśrapaṇībhyāṃ vapāṃ dhārayann urv antarikṣam iti gacchati
10.15.6	yajamāno vapāśrapaṇī punar anvarabheta
10.15.7	upa tvāgne dive diva iti tisṛbhir āgnīdhro 'dhvaryur yajamānaś cāhavanīyam upayanti
10.15.8	tata ulmukam apisṛjyāhavanīyasyāntame 'ṅgāre vapāṃ nigṛhya vāyo vīhi stokānām iti surakṣitaṃ chinnāgram adhastād vapāyā antame 'ṅgāre prāsyati
10.15.9	antarā yūpam āhavanīyaṃ ca pratiprasthātā vapām āhṛtya dakṣiṇata udaṅmukho vapāṃ śrapayati
10.15.10	tvāmute dadhire havyavāham iti vapāṃ sruveṇābhijuhoti
10.15.11	prādurbhūteṣu stokeṣu stokebhyo 'nubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
10.15.12	juṣasva saprathastamam iti stokīyā hotā pratipadyate
10.16.1	śyenīṃ suṣṛtāṃ vapāṃ kṛtvā supippalā oṣadhīḥ kṛdhīty uttaravediśroṇyāṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ barhiṣi plakṣaśākhāyāṃ nidhāya prayuto dveṣāṃsīti vapāśrapaṇyau pravṛhati
10.16.2	ghṛtavatīm adhvaryo srucam ity ucyamāne juhūpabhṛtāv ādāyātyākramyāśrāvya pratyāśrāvite svāhākṛtibhyaḥ preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
10.16.3	vaṣaṭkṛte hutvā pratyākramya prayājaśeṣeṇa dhruvāṃ pṛṣadājyaṃ ca sakṛt sakṛd abhighārya vapām abhighārayati nopabhṛtam
10.16.4	paśāv ājyabhāgau kṛtvā juhvām upastīrya hiraṇyaśakalaṃ nidhāya kṛtsnāṃ vapām avadyati
10.16.5	upariṣṭāddhiraṇyam avadhāyābhighāryendrāgnibhyāṃ chāgasya vapāyā medaso 'nubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
10.16.6	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvita indrāgnibhyāṃ chāgasya vapāṃ medaḥ prasthitaṃ preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
10.16.7	maitrāvaruṇo hotāraṃ codayati
10.16.8	prāg vapāhomāt svāhā devebhya iti pūrvaṃ parivapyaṃ hutvā vaṣaṭkṛte jātavedo vapayā gaccha devān iti vapāṃ hutvā devebhyaḥ svāhety uttaraṃ parivapyaṃ hutvā pratyākramya vapoddharaṇam abhighārayati
10.16.9	svāhordhvanabhasam ity āhavanīye viṣūcyau vapāśrapaṇyau praharati
10.16.10	saṃsrāveṇābhijutvā srucāv anyatra sādayati
10.16.11	atra varaṃ dadāti yajamānas tisro vā dakṣiṇāḥ
10.17.1	āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuva iti tisṛbhir idam āpaḥ pravahata nir mā muñcāmīti dvābhyāṃ ca sarve patnī ca cātvāle 'dbhir mārjayante
10.17.2	athādhvaryur agnīt paśupuroḍāśam nirvapa pratiprathātaḥ paśuṃ viśādhīti saṃpreṣyati
10.17.3	samānadevataṃ paśunaikādaśakapālaṃ vrīhimayaṃ puroḍāśam āgnīdhro nirvapati
10.17.4	pratiprasthātā paśuṃ viśāsti
10.17.5	hṛdayajihvāvakṣāṃsi tanima matasnū savyaṃ dor ubhe pārśve dakṣiṇā śroṇir gudatṛtīyam ity ekādaśa daivatāni
10.17.6	dakṣiṇaṃ doḥ savyā śroṇir gudatṛtīyam iti sauviṣṭakṛtāni
10.17.7	klomānaṃ plīhānaṃ purītataṃ vaniṣṭhum adhyuddhiṃ medo jāghanīm ity uddharati
10.17.8	gudaṃ mā nirvleṣīr vaniṣṭhuṃ mā nirvleṣīr iti saṃpreṣyati
10.17.9	yad yac ca medhyaṃ manyate
10.17.10	kumbhyāṃ paśuṃ samavadhāya śāmitre śrapayati
10.17.11	śūle hṛdayam upatṛdya pratapati
10.17.12	ūvadhyagohe śakṛt saṃpravidhyati lohitaṃ ca nirasyati
10.17.13	śṛte paśau puroḍāśena pracaret
10.17.14	juhūpabhṛtor upastīryāvadāyabhighāryendrāgnibhyāṃ puroḍāśasyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
10.17.15	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvita indrāgnibhyāṃ puroḍaśasya preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
10.17.16	maitrāvaruṇo hotāraṃ preṣyati
10.17.17	aupabhṛtaṃ juhvāṃ nidhāyāgnaye 'nubrūhīti sviṣṭakṛte saṃpreṣyati
10.17.18	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite 'gnaye preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
10.17.19	maitrāvaruṇo hotāraṃ presyati
10.18.1	vaṣaṭkṛte hutvā virujya prāśitram avadyatīḍāṃ ca na yajamānabhāgam
10.18.2	iḍāntaḥ paśupuroḍāśaḥ
10.18.3	upahūtām iḍāṃ maitrāvaruṇaṣaṣṭhāḥ prāśnanti
10.18.4	prastare mārjayante
10.18.5	kṛtsnasaṃsthety eke
10.18.6	juhvāṃ pañcagṛhītaṃ gṛhītvā pṛṣadājyaṃ gṛhītvā sruvaṃ prṣadājyaṃ cādāya śṛtaṃ haviḥ śamitar ity abhyāgamyābhyāgamya triḥ pṛcchati
10.18.7	śṛtam iti śamitā triḥ pratyāha
10.18.8	uttarataḥ parikramya śūlādd hṛdayaṃ pravṛhya kumbhyām avadhāya saṃ te manasā mana iti pṛṣadājyena hṛdayam abhighārayati
10.18.9	ūṣmāṇam udgatam svāhoṣmaṇo 'vyathiṣyā ity anumantrya yas ta ātmā paśuṣv ity ājyena paśum abhighārya dṛṃha gā iti kumbhīm udvāsya yūpāhavanīyayor antareṇa dakṣinātihṛtya vapāvat pañcahotrā paśum āsādayati ṣaḍḍhotrā vā
10.18.10	hṛdayaśūlaṃ surakṣitaṃ nidadhāti
10.18.11	juhvām upabhṛti vasāhavanyāṃ samavattadhānyāṃ ca catasṛṣv ājyenopastṛṇāti
10.18.12	juhvāṃ hiraṇyaśakalaṃ nidadhāty upabhṛti ca
10.18.13	plakṣaśākhāyāṃ svadhiter aśryāktayā haviṣo 'vadānāny avadyan manotāyai haviṣo 'vadīyamānasyānubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
10.18.14	hṛdayasyāgre 'vadyaty atha jihvāyā atha vakṣasaḥ
10.18.15	etad vai paśor yathāpūrvam
10.18.16	yathākāmam uttareṣām avadyati
10.18.17	yathoddhṛtam avadyatīty eke
10.18.18	madhyato gudasyāvadyati
10.18.19	dvirdvir avadāya daivatāni juhvām
10.18.20	sauviṣṭakṛtāni sakṛtsakṛd avadāyopabhṛti nidhāya śeṣāṇi samavattadhānyāṃ nidadhāti
10.18.21	gudaṃ dvidhā vibhajya sthavīya upayaḍbhyo nidadhāti
10.19.1	aṇīyas traidhaṃ vibhajya madhyamaṃ dvidhā kṛtvā juhvaṃ nidhāyāvaśiṣṭayor anyatarat sthavīya upabhṛtītarat samavattadhānyāṃ nidadhāti
10.19.2	traidhaṃ medo vibhajya yūṣṇy avadhāya tṛtīyena juhūṃ prorṇoti tṛtīyenopabhṛtaṃ ca
10.19.3	upastṛtasamavattadhānyāṃ hṛdayajihvāvakṣāṃsi tanima matasnū gudamedasos tṛtīyau bhāgau ṣaḍvaniṣṭhuṃ saptamaṃ kṛtvā nasthibhir iḍāṃ vardhayati
10.19.4	klomānaṃ plīhānaṃ purītatam ityavadhāya yūṣṇopasiñcati
10.19.5	śīrṣāṃsāṇūkāparasakthīny anavadānīyāni śṛtaiḥ saṃnidhāyaindraḥ prāṇa iti saṃmṛśati
10.19.6	apāṃ tvauṣadhīnām iti vasāhavanyām upastīrya vasāṃ gṛhṇāti
10.19.7	śrīr asīti sravantīṃ dhārāṃ svadhitinā sakṛcchinatti dviḥ pañcāvattinaḥ
10.19.8	āpaḥ samariṇann iti pārśvena vasahomam apidadhāti
10.19.9	daivateṣu sauviṣṭakṛteṣv avatteṣu yūṣnopasiktaṃ hiraṇyaśakalam avadhāyābhighāryendrāgnibhyāṃ chāgasya haviṣo 'nubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
10.19.10	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvita indrāgnibhyāṃ chāgasya haviṣaḥ preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati
10.19.11	maitrāvaruṇo hotāraṃ preṣyati
10.19.12	yājyāyā ardharcānte pratiprasthātottaratas tiṣṭhan ghṛtaṃ ghṛtapāvāna iti vasāhomaṃ juhoti
10.19.13	vasāhomoccheṣeṇa vājinavad diśaḥ prati yajati
10.19.14	atraiva tiṣṭhan juhvām upastīrya pṛṣadājyāt sakṛt sruveṇādāya juhvām avadāya dvir āghārayati
10.19.15	vanaspataye 'nubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
10.19.16	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite vanaspataye preṣyeti
10.20.1	maitrāvaruṇo hotāraṃ preṣyati
10.20.2	vaṣaṭkṛta uttarārdhapūrvārdhe 'tihāya pūrvā āhutīr juhoti
10.20.3	aupabhṛtāni juhvāṃ viparyasyāgnaye sviṣṭakṛte 'nubrūhīti saṃpreṣyati
10.20.4	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite 'gnaye sviṣṭakṛte preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati maitrāvaruṇo hotaram preṣyati
10.20.5	vaṣaṭkṛte vanaspativadd hutvā pratyākramya yathāyatanaṃ srucau sādayati
10.20.6	medasvinīm avāntareḍām avadyati
10.20.7	medasopastīrya hotur haste prakṛtivad iḍām avadāya medasābhighārayati
10.20.8	hotre 'dhyuddhiṃ haraty agnīdhre medasvinaṃ vaniṣṭhuṃ brahmaṇe vakṣaḥ
10.20.9	vayaṃ soma vrate taveti brahmā tat prāśnāti
10.20.10	prāśyācamyāntarvedi mārjayante
10.20.11	agnīd aupayajān aṅgārān āharopayaṣṭar upasīda brahman prasthāsyāmaḥ samidham ādhāyāgnīt paridhīṃś cāgniṃ ca sakṛsakṛt saṃmṛḍḍhīti saṃpreṣyati
10.20.12	śāmitrād āgnīdhrīyād vāgnīdhro 'ṅgārān āhṛtyottarasyam vediśroṇyāṃ hotrīye va barhir vyūhya nyupyopasamādhāya nihitaṃ sthavīyo gudakāṇḍam ekādaśadhā tiryagasaṃchindan pracchidyānūyājānāṃ hutaṃ hutam aparyāvartayan pratiprasthātā samudraṃ gaccha svāhety etaiḥ pratimantraṃ vasāhavanyā hastena vopayajati
10.21.1	yad upabhṛti pṛṣadājyaṃ taj juhvām ānīya tām evopabhṛtya sakṛd dakṣiṇātikrāntaḥ pṛṣadājyenaikādaśānūyājān yajati
10.21.2	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite devebhyaḥ preṣyeti prathamam anūyājaṃ saṃpreṣyati preṣya preṣyety uttarān
10.21.3	yajamānaś catura ādyān anūyājān prathamenānumantrayate daśamaṃ cānūyājaṃ pañcamaprabhṛtīṃś caturo dvitīyenottamena navamaikādaśau
10.21.4	pañcamaprabhṛtiṣv adhvaryumaitrāvaruṇau yajeti hotāraṃ preṣyato daśamavarjam
10.21.5	upayaṣṭā sarvāṇi hutvādbhyas tvauṣadhībhya ity uttarato lepaṃ nimṛjya mano me hārdi yaccheti hṛdayam abhimṛśati
10.21.6	tanūṃ tvacam iti dhūmaṃ preksate
10.21.7	adhvaryuḥ pratyākramya juhvā triḥ svarum aktvāhavanīyepurastāt pratyaṅmukhas tiṣṭhan dyāṃ te dhūmo gacchatv ity anūyājānte juhvā svaruṃ juhoti
10.21.8	śṛṅgāṇīvecchṛṅgiṇām iti yajamāno hutaṃ svarum upatiṣṭhate
10.21.9	adhvaryuḥ srugvyūhanādi pratipadyāśrāvya pratyāśrāvite sūktā preṣyeti sūktavāke saṃpreṣyati
10.21.10	agnim adyeti sa hotāraṃ preṣyati
10.21.11	juhvā bile juhūpabhṛtām agrāṇya avadhāya saṃsrāvabhāgaḥ stheti tān paridhīn prahṛtān abhiprasrāvayati
10.21.12	pratyañcaḥ paretya patnīḥ saṃyājayanti
10.21.13	dakṣiṇena vihāram jāghanīm āhṛtya tayā patnīr agniṃ gṛhapatiṃ ca yajati
10.21.14	pūrvasyottānāyā jāghanyā avadyaty uttarasya nīcyās tathottānabhāgayor hotra iḍāyām agnīdhre ṣaḍavattaṃ ca krameṇa bhavataḥ
10.21.15	prāśitāyām jāghanyāṃ śeṣam patnyai prayacchati
10.21.16	sādhvaryave
10.21.17	bāhuṃ śamitre yadi brāhmaṇaḥ
10.22.1	dhruvām āpyāyya yajña yajñaṃ gaccheti trīṇi samiṣṭayajūṃṣi juhoti
10.22.2	hṛdayaśūlena carati
10.22.3	asaṃspṛśan hṛdayaśūlam antareṇa cātvālotkarāv udaṅ gatvā śug asi tam abhiśoceti dveṣyaṃ manasā dhyāyan śukrasya cārdrasya ca sandhāv udvāsayati
10.22.4	apa upaspṛśya dhāmno dhāmna ity upasthāya sumitrā na ity adbhir mārjayante
10.22.5	apratīkṣam āgatyaidho 'sy edhiṣīmahīty āhvanīye samidha ādhāyāpo anvācāriṣam ity upatiṣṭhante
10.22.6	tathā gārhapatye patnī ca
10.22.7	sarveṣāṃ paśubandhānam eṣa kalpaḥ
10.22.8	namaḥ sakhibhyaḥ sannān māvagātāśāsānaḥ suvīryam iti yajamānaḥ saṃsthite yūpam upatiṣṭhata upatiṣṭhate
11.1.1	atha sautrāmaṇī
11.1.2	tayā brāhmaṇo rājanyo vaiśyo vā bhūtikāmo yajeta somātipavitaḥ somavāmī rājā cāparuddho 'bhicarann abhicaryamāṇo 'bhiṣekeṣu ca sarvatra
11.1.3	sautrāmaṇyā yakṣyamāṇasya purastāt trirātre sīsena klībācchaṣpāṇi vrīhyādīn krīṇāti
11.1.4	tāni kṣaume nyupyopanahyati
11.1.5	agnyanvādhānādi paristaraṇāntaṃ kṛtvā pāṇiprakṣālanādi pratipadya kapālānāṃ sthāne sthālīṃ prayunakti
11.1.6	aśvibhyāṃ sarasvatyā indrāya sutrāmṇe prabhūtān vrīhīn nirvapati
11.1.7	teṣv ardhān avahatya carukalpena śrapayaty ardhān gārhapatye lājān bharjayati
11.1.8	agreṇa gārhapatyam avaṭaṃ khātvā tasmiṃś caruṃ surāyāḥ kalpena surāṃ saṃdadhāti yathā parisrud bhavati
11.1.9	svādvīṃ tveti parisrutā śaṣpāṇi saṃsṛjati
11.2.1	somo 'sy aśvibhyām iti saṃsṛṣṭān abhimṛśati
11.2.2	tisṛṣu rātriṣu vyuṣṭāsu paśubandhas tāyate sautrāmaṇiḥ
11.2.3	tasyā nirūḍhapaśubandhavat kalpaḥ
11.2.4	saumikaveditṛtīye yajata iti vijñāyate
11.2.5	pūrvedyur ekam eva yūpaṃ chinatti
11.2.6	trīn ity eke
11.2.7	prāktanena vedena kāryaṃ karoti
11.2.8	uttaraveder dakṣiṇato vimitā paristṛtā bhavati yadi dvyahaḥ kālaḥ
11.2.9	yasmin kāle 'dhvaryur uttaravediṃ karoti tadā pratiprasthātā cātvālāt purīṣam āhṛtyottaravediṃ dakṣiṇena kharaṃ caturaśraṃ dvyaṅgulonnataṃ karoty agreṇānvāhāryapacanaṃ dvitīyaṃ kharaṃ ca
11.2.10	yadādhvaryur agniṃ praṇayati tadānvāhāryapacanād aṅgārān āhṛtya pratiprasthātā pūrvasmin khare pratiṣṭhāpayati
11.2.11	atra pāṇī na prakṣālayate
11.2.12	aśvibhyāṃ sarasvatyā indrāya sutrāmṇe trīṇi vaikaṅkatāny ūrdhvapātrāṇy aparasmin khare prayunakti sataṃ śatātṛṇṇāṃ sthālīṃ rukmaṃ vālasrāvaṃ śyenapattraṃ śrayaṇāni
11.2.13	paśūpākaraṇakāle surām udbhidya sate niḥṣicya punātu te parisrutam ityādinā sadaśena vālamayena pavitreṇa surāṃ punāti
11.3.1	vāyuḥ pūtaḥ pavitreṇeti somavāminaḥ somātipavitasya ca prāṅ soma iti somavāminaḥ pratyaṅ soma iti somātipavitasya
11.3.2	pūtāṃ surāṃ brāhmaṇasya mūrdhni khare vāsādya paśūn upākaroti
11.3.3	samāno yūpaḥ svaruś ca
11.3.4	āśvinaṃ dhūmram ajam ālabhate sārasvataṃ meṣam aindram ṛṣabhaṃ meṣaṃ vā
11.3.5	bārhaspatyaṃ paśuṃ caturtham atipavitasyālabhate somavāminaś ca
11.3.6	pāśukāni pātrāṇi saṃsṛjya juhavad ūrdhvapātrāṇi saṃmārṣṭi
11.3.7	vapāsu hutāsu rukmam ṛṣabhaḥ sṛtvarī vaḍabā ca dakṣiṇā
11.3.8	cātvāle mārjayitvordhvapātraiḥ kuvid aṅgeti purorucam anūcyāparasmin khare surāgrahān gṛhṇāti
11.3.9	sarveṣāṃ grahāṇām ekā purorug yuvaṁ surāmam aśvinā putram iva pitarāv iti devatātrayavatyau yājyānuvākaye bhavataḥ
11.3.10	upayāmagṛhīto 'sy acchidrāṃ tvācchidreṇāśvibhyāṃ juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīty āśvinaṃ graham adhvaryur gṛhṇāti
11.3.11	upayāmagṛhīto 'sy acchidrāṃ tvācchidreṇa sarasvatyai juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti pratiprasthātā sārasvatam
11.3.12	upayāmagṛhīto 'sy acchidrāṃ tvācchidreṇendrāya sutrāmṇe juṣṭaṃ gṛhṇāmīti yajamāno brahmā vaindram
11.4.1	kvalasaktūn siṃhalomāni cāśvine śrīṇāti badarasaktūṃchārdūlalomāni ca sārasvate karkandhusaktūn vṛkalomāni caindre
11.4.2	api vā siṃhāv adhvaryur manasā dhyāyecchārdūlau pratiprasthātā vṛkau yajamānaḥ
11.4.3	śyenapattreṇa grahān parimṛjyaiṣa te yonir aśvibhyāṃ tvety adhvaryur yathāyatanaṃ sādayaty eṣa te yoniḥ sarasvatyai tveti pratiprasthātaiṣa te yonir indrāya sutrāmṇe tveti yajamānaḥ
11.4.4	api vā payograhān gṛhṇāti na surāgrahān ity ekeṣām
11.4.5	puroḍāśān nirupyaindram ekādaśakapālaṃ sāvitraṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ vāruṇaṃ daśakapālaṃ ca nirvapati
11.4.6	tān āsādya tattadgrahais te pracaranti
11.4.7	aśvibhyāṃ sarasvatyā indrāya sutrāmṇe somānāṃ surāmṇām anubrūhīty adhvaryuḥ saṃpreṣyati
11.4.8	āśrāvya pratyāśrāvite 'śvibhyāṃ sarasvatyā indrāya sutrāmṇe somān surāmṇaḥ prasthitān preṣyeti saṃpreṣyati maitrāvaruṇo hotāraṃ preṣyati
11.4.9	vaṣaṭkṛte juhvati
11.4.10	somasyāgne vīhīty anuyajati
11.4.11	ahāvy agne havir āsye te yasminn aśvāsa iti dvābhyāṃ yajamāno hutam anumantrayate
11.5.1	brāhmaṇasya yajamānasya brāhmaṇaṃ parikrīṇīyād uccheṣaṇasya pātāram
11.5.2	yadi brāhmaṇaṃ na vinded valmīkavapāyām avanayed iti brāhmaṇam
11.5.3	nānā hi vāṃ devahitaṃ sado mitaṃ yad atra śiṣṭaṃ rasina iti dvābhyām uccheṣaṇaṃ pibet
11.5.4	dve srutī aśṛṇavaṃ pitṝṇām iti vā sarvahutaṃ juhuyāt
11.5.5	dakṣiṇe 'gnau śikyena dhṛtāyāṃ sthālyāṃ śatātṛṇṇāyāṃ pavitram udīcīnadaśaṃ vitatya yan me manaḥ parāgatam iti rukmaṃ kuṇḍalaṃ niṣkatrayaṃ dvayaṃ vā śatamānam anūnaṃ dhārayan somapratīkāḥ pitaras tṛpṇuteti suroccheṣaṃ samavanayati
11.5.6	tvaṃ so pracikita ity etābhiḥ pitṛmatībhiḥ saumībhis tisṛbhir yājyānuvākyābhiḥ sravantīṃ purastād adhvaryur upatiṣṭhata uttarābhis tisṛbhir dakṣiṇato brahmottarābhis tribhiḥ paścāddhotā
11.5.7	yad agne kavyavāhaneti kāvyavāhanībhir āgnīdhraḥ śatātṛṇṇāṃ dakṣiṇe 'gnau nidadhāti
11.5.8	rājanyavaiśyau tu suroccheṣaṃ svayam eva pibetām
11.6.1	puroḍāśaiḥ pracarya paśubhiḥ pracarati
11.6.2	aindrasāvitravāruṇaiḥ puroḍāśaiḥ pracarati
11.6.3	paśūnāṃ puroḍāśānāṃ ca samānaṃ sviṣṭakṛdiḍam
11.6.4	saṃsthāpya hṛdayaśūlair māsareṇa pātraiś cāvabhṛthaṃ yanti
11.6.5	māsaram ṛjīṣakalpena pratipādayati
11.6.6	yas te deva varuṇa gāyatracchandā ity āśvinaṃ pātram avabhṛthe saṃpravidhyati yas te varuṇa triṣṭupchandā iti sārasvataṃ pātraṃ yas te deva varuṇa jagatīcchandā ity aindraṃ pātraṃ yas te deva varuṇānuṣṭupchandā iti śatātṛṇṇāṃ sthālīṃ yas te deva varuṇa paṅkticchandā iti hṛdayaśūlam
11.6.7	tūṣṇīṃ pratyāyanti
11.6.8	saṃtiṣṭhate sautrāmaṇī
11.7.1	juhvādīnāṃ srucāṃ catasṛṇām āyāmaṃ caturviṃśatyaṅgulaṃ bāhumātraṃ vā
11.7.2	mūlena mūlam agreṇāgraṃ tvakpārśvordhvabilaṃ ca kartavyaṃ daṇḍasyāyāmaṃ dvādaśāṅgulaṃ mūlenāham aṣṭāṅgulam agranāhaṃ ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ tadūrdhve dvādaśāṅgulaṃ tasmiṃs tryaṅgulaṃ ghanaṃ ṣaḍaṅgulivistāram agraṃ gajasyoṣṭhavad vā bilaṃ nimnam agrāntaṃ ghṛtadhārāpātanārthaṃ kulyāṃ ca kārayet
11.7.3	dhruvāyā daṇḍasyordhvaṃ caturaṅgulaṃ ghanaṃ madhye dvyaṅgulanimnaṃ ceti viśeṣaḥ
11.7.4	juhūvadāyāmau darśapūrṇamāsāgnihotrārthau sruvau dvayoś ca daṇḍāyatam ekaviṃśatyaṅgulaṃ tanmūlam agraṃ ca pūrvavad daṇḍordhvaṃ tryaṅgulaṃ samavṛttaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ ghanaṃ nāsikavad dvipuṭaṃ bilam
11.7.5	tatpuṭayor vistāraghananimnaṃ caikāṅgulam eteṣāṃ
11.7.6	bāhumātrāyāme 'py aviśeṣa ūrdhve sāgraṃ bilam ekam eveti vijñāyate
11.7.7	śiṣṭaṃ daṇḍāyāmaṃ kurvīta
11.7.8	sphyayasyāyāmo dviprādeśaḥ
11.7.9	tasya vistāraghanaṃ ca dvyaṅgulaṃ haṃsasya mukhavan mūlaṃ khananārtham agraṃ kuśatīkṣṇaṃ ca
11.8.1	śamyā juhūvadāyāmā tathaiva daṇḍasya mūlam agraṃ ca
11.8.2	daṇḍaṃ viṃśatyaṅgulam ūrdhve 'gre caturaṅgulaṃ padmasya mukulopamaṃ kumbam etasya bāhupramāṇe ca
11.8.3	evaṃ kumbaśeṣaṃ daṇḍāyataṃ kuryāt
11.8.4	aṣṭāṅgulivistārāyatā praṇītā caturaṅgulonnatā madhye ṣaḍaṅgulivistārāyatā tryaṅgulinimnā caturaśrā prasthārdhodakapūrṇā vṛttā vā tathā karoti dohanī ca prasthapayaḥpūrṇā
11.8.5	mekṣaṇaṃ sphyāyāmavistāraṃ ghanam ekāṅgulaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ vā
11.8.6	caturaṅgulivistārāyatam agraṃ prāśitrapātraṃ dvādaśāṅgulāyāmam
11.8.7	tasya mūlaṃ tryaṅgulam unnataṃ caturaṅgulaṃ tadūrdhve navāṅgulāyataṃ ṣaḍaṅgulivistāraṃ ca
11.8.8	madhye dvādaśāṅgulāyataṃ caturaṅgulavistāraṃ tryaṅgulanimnaṃ tatpramāṇākarau gokarṇavad vā bhavetām
11.8.9	iḍāpātraṃ caturviṃśatyaṅgulāyataṃ tadūrdhvavistāram unnataṃ ca prādeśamūlavistṛtaṃ prādeśārdhaṃ bhittiḥ paritaś caikāṅgulā madhyataḥ śeṣavistārāyataṃ daśāṅgulaṃ nimnaṃ camasaṃ prasthapūrṇaṃ suvṛttaṃ caturaśraṃ vā bhavet
11.8.10	ulūkhalaṃ hastonnataṃ tasya nāhaṃ dviguṇaṃ paritobhitti dvyaṅgulāyatam aṣṭakaśeṣavistārāyataṃ bilam
11.8.11	tasya nimnaṃ ṣoḍaśāṅgulam
11.9.1	musalaṃ caturhastaṃ yajamānāyataṃ vā yuktanāhaṃ mūle 'yasā nibaddham
11.9.2	etau yāvatā havirdravyasyāvaghātayogyau tāvatpramāṇau vā
11.9.3	veṇuvetrakarīṣakeṣv ekenāratnimātrāyataṃ vṛttamūlaṃ viṃśatyaṅgulivistāram aṣṭādaśāṅgulivistāraṃ vā kramān nyūnaṃ dvyaṅgulāgraṃ śūrpam
11.9.4	yājñikaṃ yat kiṃcit kāṣṭhaṃ dvitāladīrghaṃ dhṛṣṭiḥ
11.9.5	adharā dṛṣad ūrdhvopalā ca dve peṣaṇyau saṃpeṣaṇaśakte
11.9.6	tathā grāvāṇau dvau yathoktayogyau
11.9.7	mṛnmayī prasthapūrṇājyasthālī
11.9.8	kāṃsyādilohamayīty eke
11.9.9	viṃśatyaṅgulivistārāyatā piṣṭasaṃyavanī pātrī suvṛttā catuḥprasthodakapūrṇā madantipayodohas tāvatpayaḥpūrṇā sāṃnāyyadadhikumbhyau ca saṃyukteṣu puroḍāśanidhānāya yāvattālaṃ taduktasaṃkhyāpramāṇāni kapālāni dvyaṅgulāyatavistārāṇi vā sarveṣāṃ mānam ardhāṅgulam
11.9.10	prasthataṇḍulapākā carusthālī haviḥśeṣadānokte dviprasthataṇḍulapākā vā prasthārdhataṇḍulapākā prasthacaturbhāgataṇḍulapākā vā
11.9.11	saṃsrāvasrotoyuktau
11.9.12	vṛttordhvakapālāgnihotrasthālī
11.9.13	droṇārdhataṇḍulapākānvāhāryasthālī
11.9.14	prasthapūrṇas tadardhapūrṇo vā śarāvaḥ syāt
11.10.1	karmaṇy adhike ca tathaivādhikāni pātrāṇi prakṣepaṇīyāni laukikāni bhāṇḍāni tattatkarmārhāṇi syuḥ
11.10.2	dviprādeśaiḥ kuśair yugmaiḥ prādeśavistṛtaṃ dvikānubaddham agre grathitaṃ copāharaṇīyaṃ kūrcaṃ tathaivopasādanīyaṃ camasam ādadāti
11.10.3	prādeśo vitastis tālam iti dvādaśāṅgulasya hasto 'ratnir iti caturviṃśatyaṅgulasya saṃjñā bhavet
11.10.4	si̍katāsūktāsu śuṣkāḥ sikatā grāhyāḥ
11.10.5	tāsv ārdratṛṇam utkāṣṭhāśmaloṣṭalomādīn visṛjet
11.10.6	paristaraṇakūrcapavitrādīnāṃ barhiruktau kuśān kāśān aśvavālān vā
11.10.7	tadalābhe sugandhitejanamuñjolapaśyāmākanīvārasasyadūrvātṛṇāny anyāni palālāni vā gṛhṇāti
11.10.8	śuṇṭhaśaraśūkaviśīrṇatṛṇanaḍadamūtavabalbajāni varjayet
11.10.9	paridhīdhmoktau palāśakhadirabilvāśvatthaśamīnāṃ śākhāḥ samidhaḥ paridhayaś ca mukhyāḥ
11.10.10	vikaṅkatodumbaranyagrodhaplakṣakārṣmaryapautudravarohītakādīnāṃ yajñoktavṛkṣāṇāṃ madhyamāḥ
11.10.11	tadanyavanaspatīnāṃ gauṇāḥ
11.10.12	svayaṃśuṣkā na grāhyāḥ
11.11.1	triparṇāḥ sarve palāśopamāḥ
11.11.2	sarvatra vihitadravyālābhe pratinidhiṃ gṛhṇīyāt
11.11.3	anāmikāṅgulināhā mukhyāḥ kaniṣṭhāṅgulināhā madhyamā nyūnanāhā gauṇāḥ
11.11.4	śamyodumbarāḥ paridhaya ity eke
11.11.5	mūlāgre vijñāya prāgagrāḥ samidho hotavyāḥ
11.11.6	nimbaśleṣmātakanīpatilvarājavṛkṣavibhītakaśalmalikovidārakarañjabādhakanirguṇḍipalāṇḍujapānāṃ samidhaḥ paridhīṃś ca varjayet
11.11.7	haviruktau yavanīvāraveṇuśyāmākavrīhijātipriyaṅgavo dhānyāni haviṣyāṇām
11.11.8	teṣām alābhe mūlakandaphalāni vā grāhyāṇi
11.11.9	sarveṣu dhānyeṣu varakakodārakodravāṇi varjanīyāni
11.11.10	ājyoktau gavyaṃ ghṛtaṃ śreṣṭham
11.11.11	tadabhāve ghṛtam ājaṃ māhiṣaṃ vā
11.11.12	tadabhāve payas tailaṃ sārṣapaṃ pratinidhiḥ
11.11.13	kusumbhātasīnārikelavṛkṣāṇāṃ sneham anyac ca yad rasavad bhojyaṃ tad vāpi piṣṭamiśrodakaṃ ca homyaṃ bhavati
11.11.14	abhojyaṃ gandharasaduṣṭaṃ ca varjanīyam
11.11.15	sarveṣāṃ pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ śreṣṭhatamam
11.11.16	pūrveṣām alābhe 'paraṃ gṛhṇāty aparaṃ gṛhṇāti
12.1.1	athāgniṣṭomaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
12.1.2	yakṣyamāṇaḥ śraddhāvān prajñāvān śucir vidhyupārjitopakaraṇo yathottaropayogaṃ buddhvā saṃbhārān yatnena saṃbharati
12.1.3	brāhmaṇān ārṣeyān anivṛttavidyān annaśuddhyupetān lakṣaṇasaṃpannān ṛtvijaḥ ṣoḍaśa brahmaprathamān hotṛprathamān adhvaryuprathamān udgātṛprathamān vā vṛṇīte
12.1.4	prathamān mahartvijaś caturo vā
12.1.5	tān anyaḥ karmajño yajamānānujñāto 'bhivadaty amuṣya somo bhaviṣyatīti
12.1.6	ka ṛtvijaḥ ke yājayanti kaccin nāhīnaḥ kaccinna nyastam ārtvijyaṃ kaccit kalyāṇyo dakṣiṇā iti vijñāyata evaṃ tam ṛtvijaḥ pṛcchanti
12.1.7	athaita ṛtvija ete yājayanti nāhīno 'gniṣṭomo na nyastam ārtvijyaṃ kalyāṇyo dakṣiṇā iti sa tān pratyāha
12.1.8	bhūr bhuvaḥ suvar āyur me prāvoca iti yājayiṣyan japati
12.1.9	ayājayiṣyan namaḥ somāya rājña iti somaṃ rājānam upasthāya pratyācakṣīta
12.1.10	devo devam etv ity abhipravrajati
12.1.11	padvā nāmāsīti panthānam āsthāya pitaro bhūr iti triḥ pitṝn abhimantrayate
12.1.12	brāhmaṇācchaṃsī potā cāvaśiṣṭau brahmāṇau
12.1.13	acchāvāko grāvastuc ca hotārau
12.1.14	neṣṭonnetā cādhvaryū
12.1.15	udgātā prastotā pratihartā subrahmaṇyaś codgātāraḥ
12.1.16	abhigaro dhruvagopaḥ saṃsrāva sadasya iti sadasyāś catvāraś cety eke
12.1.17	vāsiṣṭhabhārgavāṅgirasāyāsyā mahartvijaḥ kramaśo bhavanti
12.1.18	śeṣāḥ kāśyapā bhāradvājā bhārgavā aṅgiraso vā
12.1.19	vaiśvāmitro hotety eke
12.1.20	api vā sarveṣāṃ yonir vṛttaṃ vidyā ca pramāṇam
12.1.21	daśaikādaśa vā camasādhvaryavaḥ
12.1.22	tān ekaikaśo vṛṇīte
12.2.1	candramā devo daivyo brahmety etair yathāliṅgam ṛtvija upāṃśu devān vṛtvāsau mānuṣa ity uccair mānuṣān āpo devīr daivyā hotrāśaṃsinya iti maitrāvaruṇaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaṃ hotāraṃ neṣṭāram acchāvākam āgnīdhram ity etān hotrakān raśmayo devā daivyā iti camasādhvaryūṃś ca tān yathopapādam alaṃkṛtya madhuparkaṃ dattvāmāvāsyāyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vā dīkṣate
12.2.2	saṃvatsarād arvāg aparimitā dīkṣākalpā bhavanti
12.2.3	darśapūrṇamāsābhyām iṣṭvāgniṣṭomam āharet
12.2.4	eṣa prathamaḥ somānām atirātra ity eke

12.2.7	api vā pṛthakkāmaḥ pṛthagāharet
12.3.1	vasante vasante somena yajeta
12.3.2	tadā tisro dakṣiṇā iti vijñāyate
12.3.3	rathantarasāmā somo bṛhatsāmā vā
12.3.4	prathamaṃ rathantarasāmānam āharet paścād yathākāmam
12.3.5	paurṇamāsyām amāvāsyāyāṃ vā sutyam ahar bhavati dīkṣate vā
12.3.6	ekā dīkṣā tisro vā
12.3.7	tadā pañcamīṃ saptamīṃ vā prasutaḥ
12.3.8	deva varuṇeti rājānaṃ devayajanaṃ yācet
12.3.9	sa cen na dadyād anyaṃ rājānaṃ yācet
12.3.10	yadi dadyād devayajanavān bhūyā ity enam abhinandet
12.3.11	sa yadi na dadyād yad ahaṃ devayajanaṃ veda tasmiṃs tvā devayajana āchinadmīty etair yathāliṅgaṃ yajamāna ṛtvijaś cainam abhivyāharanti
12.3.12	yadi rājā yajamāno 'gnir hotā sa me hotety etair yathāliṅgam ṛtvijo devayajanaṃ yācet
12.3.13	api vā sarve na yācayeyuḥ sakṣedaṃ paśyeti devatā evopatiṣṭheta
12.4.1	yad dṛḍhasthaṇḍilaṃ śuddham uccatamam acchidram avalmīkam aniriṇam apāṣāṇaṃ samaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ prākpravaṇam udakpravaṇaṃ vā śuddhauṣadhi śuddhadravyaṃ pradakṣiṇodakaṃ śvetamṛttikaṃ pītamṛttikaṃ vā devabrāhmaṇajuṣṭam anāsuraṃ sunimitropalakṣitam
12.4.2	purastād devayajanād devayajanamātrā na śiṣṭā devayajanam ity ācakṣate
12.4.3	kalyāṇyo vā dakṣiṇā devayajane pramāṇam
12.4.4	edam aganma devayajanaṃ pṛthivyā iti yakṣyamāṇo devayajanam adhyavasyati
12.4.5	purohaviṣi devayajane yājayed iti brāhmaṇoktāni kāmyāni devayajanāni yathākāmam
12.4.6	atra sarvataḥ pariśritāṃ purastādunnatāṃ pratidigdvārāṃ prācīnavaṃśāṃ śālāṃ kurvanty uttarataḥpurastāt pañcamaṃ dvāram
12.4.7	avāntaradikṣu sraktayaḥ
12.4.8	sraktiṣv ārokāḥ
12.4.9	paścāt patnīśālā prāgdvārā
12.4.10	atha prāg dīkṣaṇīyāyā agnir yajurbhir iti saṃbhārayajūṃṣy āhavanīye hutvā vāgghoteti manasānudrutyānuvākena juhoti
12.4.11	dīkṣitānnaṃ na bhuñjate prāg agnīṣomīyād vibhakte yajñārthe śeṣād bhuñjīran krīte vā rājani
12.4.12	somāya rājñe śālāyāṃ pāyasamannaṃ lājāṃś cā krayād upāharanti
12.5.1	aparāhne dīkṣate yajamānaḥ pūrvāhṇe vā
12.5.2	athādhvaryur dīkṣaṇīyām iṣṭiṃ nirvapaty āgnāvaiṣṇavam ekādaśakapālaṃ ghṛte caruṃ vā
12.5.3	saptadaśa sāmidhenyaḥ
12.5.4	na yajamānabhāgaṃ karoti
12.5.5	na barhiṣadaṃ puroḍāśaṃ karoti
12.5.6	na dakṣiṇā
12.5.7	patnīsaṃyājāntaiṣā
12.5.8	ājyeḍāṃ bhakṣayitvā viramanti
12.5.9	dhruvāyāḥ śeṣaṃ karoti
